BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evam etat purā pṛṣṭo maitreyo bhagavān kila
BhP kṣattrā vanaṃ praviṣṭena tyaktvā svagṛham ṛddhimat
BhP yad vā ayaṃ mantrakṛd vo bhagavān akhileśvaraḥ
BhP pauravendragṛhaṃ hitvā praviveśātmasāt kṛtam
BhP rājovāca
BhP kutra kṣattur bhagavatā maitreyeṇāsa saṅgamaḥ
BhP kadā vā sahasaṃvāda etad varṇaya naḥ prabho
BhP na hy alpārthodayas tasya vidurasyāmalātmanaḥ
BhP tasmin varīyasi praśnaḥ sādhuvādopabṛṃhitaḥ
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP sa evam ṛṣivaryo 'yaṃ pṛṣṭo rājñā parīkṣitā
BhP praty āha taṃ subahuvit prītātmā śrūyatām iti
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP yadā tu rājā svasutān asādhūn puṣṇan na dharmeṇa vinaṣṭadṛṣṭiḥ
BhP bhrātur yaviṣṭhasya sutān vibandhūn praveśya lākṣābhavane dadāha
BhP yadā sabhāyāṃ kurudevadevyāḥ keśābhimarśaṃ sutakarma garhyam
BhP na vārayām āsa nṛpaḥ snuṣāyāḥ svāsrair harantyāḥ kucakuṅkumāni
BhP dyūte tv adharmeṇa jitasya sādhoḥ satyāvalambasya vanaṃ gatasya
BhP na yācato 'dāt samayena dāyaṃ tamojuṣāṇo yad ajātaśatroḥ
BhP yadā ca pārthaprahitaḥ sabhāyāṃ jagadgurur yāni jagāda kṛṣṇaḥ
BhP na tāni puṃsām amṛtāyanāni rājoru mene kṣatapuṇyaleśaḥ
BhP yadopahūto bhavanaṃ praviṣṭo mantrāya pṛṣṭaḥ kila pūrvajena
BhP athāha tan mantradṛśāṃ varīyān yan mantriṇo vaidurikaṃ vadanti
BhP ajātaśatroḥ pratiyaccha dāyaṃ titikṣato durviṣahaṃ tavāgaḥ
BhP sahānujo yatra vṛkodarāhiḥ śvasan ruṣā yat tvam alaṃ bibheṣi
BhP pārthāṃs tu devo bhagavān mukundo gṛhītavān sakṣitidevadevaḥ
BhP āste svapuryāṃ yadudevadevo vinirjitāśeṣanṛdevadevaḥ
BhP sa eṣa doṣaḥ puruṣadviḍ āste gṛhān praviṣṭo yam apatyamatyā
BhP puṣṇāsi kṛṣṇād vimukho gataśrīs tyajāśv aśaivaṃ kulakauśalāya
BhP ity ūcivāṃs tatra suyodhanena pravṛddhakopasphuritādhareṇa
BhP asatkṛtaḥ satspṛhaṇīyaśīlaḥ kṣattā sakarṇānujasaubalena
BhP ka enam atropajuhāva jihmaṃ dāsyāḥ sutaṃ yadbalinaiva puṣṭaḥ
BhP tasmin pratīpaḥ parakṛtya āste nirvāsyatām āśu purāc chvasānaḥ
BhP svayaṃ dhanur dvāri nidhāya māyāṃ bhrātuḥ puro marmasu tāḍito 'pi
BhP sa ittham atyulbaṇakarṇabāṇair gatavyatho 'yād uru mānayānaḥ
BhP sa nirgataḥ kauravapuṇyalabdho gajāhvayāt tīrthapadaḥ padāni
BhP anvākramat puṇyacikīrṣayorvyām adhiṣṭhito yāni sahasramūrtiḥ
BhP pureṣu puṇyopavanādrikuñjeṣv apaṅkatoyeṣu saritsaraḥsu
BhP anantaliṅgaiḥ samalaṅkṛteṣu cacāra tīrthāyataneṣv ananyaḥ
BhP gāṃ paryaṭan medhyaviviktavṛttiḥ sadāpluto 'dhaḥ śayano 'vadhūtaḥ
BhP alakṣitaḥ svair avadhūtaveṣo vratāni cere haritoṣaṇāni
BhP itthaṃ vrajan bhāratam eva varṣaṃ kālena yāvad gatavān prabhāsam
BhP tāvac chaśāsa kṣitim eka cakrāml ekātapatrām ajitena pārthaḥ
BhP tatrātha śuśrāva suhṛdvinaṣṭiṃ vanaṃ yathā veṇujavahnisaṃśrayam
BhP saṃspardhayā dagdham athānuśocan sarasvatīṃ pratyag iyāya tūṣṇīm
BhP tasyāṃ tritasyośanaso manoś ca pṛthor athāgner asitasya vāyoḥ
BhP tīrthaṃ sudāsasya gavāṃ guhasya yac chrāddhadevasya sa āsiṣeve
BhP anyāni ceha dvijadevadevaiḥ kṛtāni nānāyatanāni viṣṇoḥ
BhP pratyaṅgamukhyāṅkitamandirāṇi yaddarśanāt kṛṣṇam anusmaranti
BhP tatas tv ativrajya surāṣṭram ṛddhaṃ sauvīramatsyān kurujāṅgalāṃś ca
BhP kālena tāvad yamunām upetya tatroddhavaṃ bhāgavataṃ dadarśa
BhP sa vāsudevānucaraṃ praśāntaṃ bṛhaspateḥ prāk tanayaṃ pratītam
BhP āliṅgya gāḍhaṃ praṇayena bhadraṃ svānām apṛcchad bhagavatprajānām
BhP kaccit purāṇau puruṣau svanābhya pādmānuvṛttyeha kilāvatīrṇau
BhP āsāta urvyāḥ kuśalaṃ vidhāya kṛtakṣaṇau kuśalaṃ śūragehe
BhP kaccit kurūṇāṃ paramaḥ suhṛn no bhāmaḥ sa āste sukham aṅga śauriḥ
BhP yo vai svasṇāṃ pitṛvad dadāti varān vadānyo varatarpaṇena
BhP kaccid varūthādhipatir yadūnāṃ pradyumna āste sukham aṅga vīraḥ
BhP yaṃ rukmiṇī bhagavato 'bhilebhe ārādhya viprān smaram ādisarge
BhP kaccit sukhaṃ sātvatavṛṣṇibhoja dāśārhakāṇām adhipaḥ sa āste
BhP yam abhyaṣiñcac chatapatranetro nṛpāsanāśāṃ parihṛtya dūrāt
BhP kaccid dhareḥ saumya sutaḥ sadṛkṣa āste 'graṇī rathināṃ sādhu sāmbaḥ
BhP asūta yaṃ jāmbavatī vratāḍhyā devaṃ guhaṃ yo 'mbikayā dhṛto 'gre
BhP kṣemaṃ sa kaccid yuyudhāna āste yaḥ phālgunāl labdhadhanūrahasyaḥ
BhP lebhe 'ñjasādhokṣajasevayaiva gatiṃ tadīyāṃ yatibhir durāpām
BhP kaccid budhaḥ svasty anamīva āste śvaphalkaputro bhagavatprapannaḥ
BhP yaḥ kṛṣṇapādāṅkitamārgapāṃsuṣv aceṣṭata premavibhinnadhairyaḥ
BhP kaccic chivaṃ devakabhojaputryā viṣṇuprajāyā iva devamātuḥ
BhP yā vai svagarbheṇa dadhāra devaṃ trayī yathā yajñavitānam artham
BhP apisvid āste bhagavān sukhaṃ vo yaḥ sātvatāṃ kāmadugho 'niruddhaḥ
BhP yam āmananti sma hi śabdayoniṃ manomayaṃ sattvaturīyatattvam
BhP apisvid anye ca nijātmadaivam ananyavṛttyā samanuvratā ye
BhP hṛdīkasatyātmajacārudeṣṇa gadādayaḥ svasti caranti saumya
BhP api svadorbhyāṃ vijayācyutābhyāṃ dharmeṇa dharmaḥ paripāti setum
BhP duryodhano 'tapyata yatsabhāyāṃ sāmrājyalakṣmyā vijayānuvṛttyā
BhP kiṃ vā kṛtāgheṣv agham atyamarṣī bhīmo 'hivad dīrghatamaṃ vyamuñcat
BhP yasyāṅghripātaṃ raṇabhūr na sehe mārgaṃ gadāyāś carato vicitram
BhP kaccid yaśodhā rathayūthapānāṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvoparatārir āste
BhP alakṣito yaccharakūṭagūḍho māyākirāto giriśas tutoṣa
BhP yamāv utasvit tanayau pṛthāyāḥ pārthair vṛtau pakṣmabhir akṣiṇīva
BhP remāta uddāya mṛdhe svarikthaṃ parāt suparṇāv iva vajrivaktrāt
BhP aho pṛthāpi dhriyate 'rbhakārthe rājarṣivaryeṇa vināpi tena
BhP yas tv ekavīro 'dhiratho vijigye dhanur dvitīyaḥ kakubhaś catasraḥ
BhP saumyānuśoce tam adhaḥpatantaṃ bhrātre paretāya vidudruhe yaḥ
BhP niryāpito yena suhṛt svapuryā ahaṃ svaputrān samanuvratena
BhP so 'haṃ harer martyaviḍambanena dṛśo nṛṇāṃ cālayato vidhātuḥ
BhP nānyopalakṣyaḥ padavīṃ prasādāc carāmi paśyan gatavismayo 'tra
BhP nūnaṃ nṛpāṇāṃ trimadotpathānāṃ mahīṃ muhuś cālayatāṃ camūbhiḥ
BhP vadhāt prapannārtijihīrṣayeśo 'py upaikṣatāghaṃ bhagavān kurūṇām
BhP ajasya janmotpathanāśanāya karmāṇy akartur grahaṇāya puṃsām
BhP nanv anyathā ko 'rhati dehayogaṃ paro guṇānām uta karmatantram
BhP tasya prapannākhilalokapānām avasthitānām anuśāsane sve
BhP arthāya jātasya yaduṣv ajasya vārtāṃ sakhe kīrtaya tīrthakīrteḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti bhāgavataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṣattrā vārtāṃ priyāśrayām
BhP prativaktuṃ na cotseha autkaṇṭhyāt smāriteśvaraḥ
BhP yaḥ pañcahāyano mātrā prātarāśāya yācitaḥ
BhP tan naicchad racayan yasya saparyāṃ bālalīlayā
BhP sa kathaṃ sevayā tasya kālena jarasaṃ gataḥ
BhP pṛṣṭo vārtāṃ pratibrūyād bhartuḥ pādāv anusmaran
BhP sa muhūrtam abhūt tūṣṇīṃ kṛṣṇāṅghrisudhayā bhṛśam
BhP tīvreṇa bhaktiyogena nimagnaḥ sādhu nirvṛtaḥ
BhP pulakodbhinnasarvāṅgo muñcan mīladdṛśā śucaḥ
BhP pūrṇārtho lakṣitas tena snehaprasarasamplutaḥ
BhP śanakair bhagavallokān nṛlokaṃ punar āgataḥ
BhP vimṛjya netre viduraṃ prītyāhoddhava utsmayan
BhP uddhava uvāca
BhP kṛṣṇadyumaṇi nimloce gīrṇeṣv ajagareṇa ha
BhP kiṃ nu naḥ kuśalaṃ brūyāṃ gataśrīṣu gṛheṣv aham
BhP durbhago bata loko 'yaṃ yadavo nitarām api
BhP ye saṃvasanto na vidur hariṃ mīnā ivoḍupam
BhP iṅgitajñāḥ puruprauḍhā ekārāmāś ca sātvatāḥ
BhP sātvatām ṛṣabhaṃ sarve bhūtāvāsam amaṃsata
BhP devasya māyayā spṛṣṭā ye cānyad asadāśritāḥ
BhP bhrāmyate dhīr na tadvākyair ātmany uptātmano harau
BhP pradarśyātaptatapasām avitṛptadṛśāṃ nṛṇām
BhP ādāyāntar adhād yas tu svabimbaṃ lokalocanam
BhP yan martyalīlaupayikaṃ svayoga māyābalaṃ darśayatā gṛhītam
BhP vismāpanaṃ svasya ca saubhagarddheḥ paraṃ padaṃ bhūṣaṇabhūṣaṇāṅgam
BhP yad dharmasūnor bata rājasūye nirīkṣya dṛksvastyayanaṃ trilokaḥ
BhP kārtsnyena cādyeha gataṃ vidhātur arvāksṛtau kauśalam ity amanyata
BhP yasyānurāgaplutahāsarāsa līlāvalokapratilabdhamānāḥ
BhP vrajastriyo dṛgbhir anupravṛtta dhiyo 'vatasthuḥ kila kṛtyaśeṣāḥ
BhP svaśāntarūpeṣv itaraiḥ svarūpair abhyardyamāneṣv anukampitātmā
BhP parāvareśo mahadaṃśayukto hy ajo 'pi jāto bhagavān yathāgniḥ
BhP māṃ khedayaty etad ajasya janma viḍambanaṃ yad vasudevagehe
BhP vraje ca vāso 'ribhayād iva svayaṃ purād vyavātsīd yadanantavīryaḥ
BhP dunoti cetaḥ smarato mamaitad yad āha pādāv abhivandya pitroḥ
BhP tātāmba kaṃsād uruśaṅkitānāṃ prasīdataṃ no 'kṛtaniṣkṛtīnām
BhP ko vā amuṣyāṅghrisarojareṇuṃ vismartum īśīta pumān vijighran
BhP yo visphuradbhrūviṭapena bhūmer bhāraṃ kṛtāntena tiraścakāra
BhP dṛṣṭā bhavadbhir nanu rājasūye caidyasya kṛṣṇaṃ dviṣato 'pi siddhiḥ
BhP yāṃ yoginaḥ saṃspṛhayanti samyag yogena kas tadvirahaṃ saheta
BhP tathaiva cānye naralokavīrā ya āhave kṛṣṇamukhāravindam
BhP netraiḥ pibanto nayanābhirāmaṃ pārthāstrapūtaḥ padam āpur asya
BhP svayaṃ tv asāmyātiśayas tryadhīśaḥ svārājyalakṣmyāptasamastakāmaḥ
BhP baliṃ haradbhiś ciralokapālaiḥ kirīṭakoṭyeḍitapādapīṭhaḥ
BhP tat tasya kaiṅkaryam alaṃ bhṛtān no viglāpayaty aṅga yad ugrasenam
BhP tiṣṭhan niṣaṇṇaṃ parameṣṭhidhiṣṇye nyabodhayad deva nidhārayeti
BhP aho bakī yaṃ stanakālakūṭaṃ jighāṃsayāpāyayad apy asādhvī
BhP lebhe gatiṃ dhātryucitāṃ tato 'nyaṃ kaṃ vā dayāluṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajema
BhP manye 'surān bhāgavatāṃs tryadhīśe saṃrambhamārgābhiniviṣṭacittān
BhP ye saṃyuge 'cakṣata tārkṣyaputram aṃse sunābhāyudham āpatantam
BhP vasudevasya devakyāṃ jāto bhojendrabandhane
BhP cikīrṣur bhagavān asyāḥ śam ajenābhiyācitaḥ
BhP tato nandavrajam itaḥ pitrā kaṃsād vibibhyatā
BhP ekādaśa samās tatra gūḍhārciḥ sabalo 'vasat
BhP parīto vatsapair vatsāṃś cārayan vyaharad vibhuḥ
BhP yamunopavane kūjad dvijasaṅkulitāṅghripe
BhP kaumārīṃ darśayaṃś ceṣṭāṃ prekṣaṇīyāṃ vrajaukasām
BhP rudann iva hasan mugdha bālasiṃhāvalokanaḥ
BhP sa eva godhanaṃ lakṣmyā niketaṃ sitagovṛṣam
BhP cārayann anugān gopān raṇadveṇur arīramat
BhP prayuktān bhojarājena māyinaḥ kāmarūpiṇaḥ
BhP līlayā vyanudat tāṃs tān bālaḥ krīḍanakān iva
BhP vipannān viṣapānena nigṛhya bhujagādhipam
BhP utthāpyāpāyayad gāvas tat toyaṃ prakṛtisthitam
BhP ayājayad gosavena goparājaṃ dvijottamaiḥ
BhP vittasya corubhārasya cikīrṣan sadvyayaṃ vibhuḥ
BhP varṣatīndre vrajaḥ kopād bhagnamāne 'tivihvalaḥ
BhP gotralīlātapatreṇa trāto bhadrānugṛhṇatā
BhP śaracchaśikarair mṛṣṭaṃ mānayan rajanīmukham
BhP gāyan kalapadaṃ reme strīṇāṃ maṇḍalamaṇḍanaḥ
BhP uddhava uvāca
BhP tataḥ sa āgatya puraṃ svapitroś cikīrṣayā śaṃ baladevasaṃyutaḥ
BhP nipātya tuṅgād ripuyūthanāthaṃ hataṃ vyakarṣad vyasum ojasorvyām
BhP sāndīpaneḥ sakṛt proktaṃ brahmādhītya savistaram
BhP tasmai prādād varaṃ putraṃ mṛtaṃ pañcajanodarāt
BhP samāhutā bhīṣmakakanyayā ye śriyaḥ savarṇena bubhūṣayaiṣām
BhP gāndharvavṛttyā miṣatāṃ svabhāgaṃ jahre padaṃ mūrdhni dadhat suparṇaḥ
BhP kakudmino 'viddhanaso damitvā svayaṃvare nāgnajitīm uvāha
BhP tadbhagnamānān api gṛdhyato 'jñāñ jaghne 'kṣataḥ śastrabhṛtaḥ svaśastraiḥ
BhP priyaṃ prabhur grāmya iva priyāyā vidhitsur ārcchad dyutaruṃ yadarthe
BhP vajry ādravat taṃ sagaṇo ruṣāndhaḥ krīḍāmṛgo nūnam ayaṃ vadhūnām
BhP sutaṃ mṛdhe khaṃ vapuṣā grasantaṃ dṛṣṭvā sunābhonmathitaṃ dharitryā
BhP āmantritas tattanayāya śeṣaṃ dattvā tadantaḥpuram āviveśa
BhP tatrāhṛtās tā naradevakanyāḥ kujena dṛṣṭvā harim ārtabandhum
BhP utthāya sadyo jagṛhuḥ praharṣa vrīḍānurāgaprahitāvalokaiḥ
BhP āsāṃ muhūrta ekasmin nānāgāreṣu yoṣitām
BhP savidhaṃ jagṛhe pāṇīn anurūpaḥ svamāyayā
BhP tāsv apatyāny ajanayad ātmatulyāni sarvataḥ
BhP ekaikasyāṃ daśa daśa prakṛter vibubhūṣayā
BhP kālamāgadhaśālvādīn anīkai rundhataḥ puram
BhP ajīghanat svayaṃ divyaṃ svapuṃsāṃ teja ādiśat
BhP śambaraṃ dvividaṃ bāṇaṃ muraṃ balvalam eva ca
BhP anyāṃś ca dantavakrādīn avadhīt kāṃś ca ghātayat
BhP atha te bhrātṛputrāṇāṃ pakṣayoḥ patitān nṛpān
BhP cacāla bhūḥ kurukṣetraṃ yeṣām āpatatāṃ balaiḥ
BhP sa karṇaduḥśāsanasaubalānāṃ kumantrapākena hataśriyāyuṣam
BhP suyodhanaṃ sānucaraṃ śayānaṃ bhagnorum ūrvyāṃ na nananda paśyan
BhP kiyān bhuvo 'yaṃ kṣapitorubhāro yad droṇabhīṣmārjunabhīmamūlaiḥ
BhP aṣṭādaśākṣauhiṇiko madaṃśair āste balaṃ durviṣahaṃ yadūnām
BhP mitho yadaiṣāṃ bhavitā vivādo madhvāmadātāmravilocanānām
BhP naiṣāṃ vadhopāya iyān ato 'nyo mayy udyate 'ntardadhate svayaṃ sma
BhP evaṃ sañcintya bhagavān svarājye sthāpya dharmajam
BhP nandayām āsa suhṛdaḥ sādhūnāṃ vartma darśayan
BhP uttarāyāṃ dhṛtaḥ pūror vaṃśaḥ sādhvabhimanyunā
BhP sa vai drauṇyastrasampluṣṭaḥ punar bhagavatā dhṛtaḥ
BhP ayājayad dharmasutam aśvamedhais tribhir vibhuḥ
BhP so 'pi kṣmām anujai rakṣan reme kṛṣṇam anuvrataḥ
BhP bhagavān api viśvātmā lokavedapathānugaḥ
BhP kāmān siṣeve dvārvatyām asaktaḥ sāṅkhyam āsthitaḥ
BhP snigdhasmitāvalokena vācā pīyūṣakalpayā
BhP caritreṇānavadyena śrīniketena cātmanā
BhP imaṃ lokam amuṃ caiva ramayan sutarāṃ yadūn
BhP reme kṣaṇadayā datta kṣaṇastrīkṣaṇasauhṛdaḥ
BhP tasyaivaṃ ramamāṇasya saṃvatsaragaṇān bahūn
BhP gṛhamedheṣu yogeṣu virāgaḥ samajāyata
BhP daivādhīneṣu kāmeṣu daivādhīnaḥ svayaṃ pumān
BhP ko viśrambheta yogena yogeśvaram anuvrataḥ
BhP puryāṃ kadācit krīḍadbhir yadubhojakumārakaiḥ
BhP kopitā munayaḥ śepur bhagavanmatakovidāḥ
BhP tataḥ katipayair māsair vṛṣṇibhojāndhakādayaḥ
BhP yayuḥ prabhāsaṃ saṃhṛṣṭā rathair devavimohitāḥ
BhP tatra snātvā pitn devān ṛṣīṃś caiva tadambhasā
BhP tarpayitvātha viprebhyo gāvo bahuguṇā daduḥ
BhP hiraṇyaṃ rajataṃ śayyāṃ vāsāṃsy ajinakambalān
BhP yānaṃ rathān ibhān kanyā dharāṃ vṛttikarīm api
BhP annaṃ corurasaṃ tebhyo dattvā bhagavadarpaṇam
BhP goviprārthāsavaḥ śūrāḥ praṇemur bhuvi mūrdhabhiḥ
BhP uddhava uvāca
BhP atha te tadanujñātā bhuktvā pītvā ca vāruṇīm
BhP tayā vibhraṃśitajñānā duruktair marma paspṛśuḥ
BhP teṣāṃ maireyadoṣeṇa viṣamīkṛtacetasām
BhP nimlocati ravāv āsīd veṇūnām iva mardanam
BhP bhagavān svātmamāyāyā gatiṃ tām avalokya saḥ
BhP sarasvatīm upaspṛśya vṛkṣamūlam upāviśat
BhP ahaṃ cokto bhagavatā prapannārtihareṇa ha
BhP badarīṃ tvaṃ prayāhīti svakulaṃ sañjihīrṣuṇā
BhP tathāpi tadabhipretaṃ jānann aham arindama
BhP pṛṣṭhato 'nvagamaṃ bhartuḥ pādaviśleṣaṇākṣamaḥ
BhP adrākṣam ekam āsīnaṃ vicinvan dayitaṃ patim
BhP śrīniketaṃ sarasvatyāṃ kṛtaketam aketanam
BhP śyāmāvadātaṃ virajaṃ praśāntāruṇalocanam
BhP dorbhiś caturbhir viditaṃ pītakauśāmbareṇa ca
BhP vāma ūrāv adhiśritya dakṣiṇāṅghrisaroruham
BhP apāśritārbhakāśvattham akṛśaṃ tyaktapippalam
BhP tasmin mahābhāgavato dvaipāyanasuhṛtsakhā
BhP lokān anucaran siddha āsasāda yadṛcchayā
BhP tasyānuraktasya muner mukundaḥ pramodabhāvānatakandharasya
BhP āśṛṇvato mām anurāgahāsa samīkṣayā viśramayann uvāca
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP vedāham antar manasīpsitaṃ te dadāmi yat tad duravāpam anyaiḥ
BhP satre purā viśvasṛjāṃ vasūnāṃ matsiddhikāmena vaso tvayeṣṭaḥ
BhP sa eṣa sādho caramo bhavānām āsāditas te madanugraho yat
BhP yan māṃ nṛlokān raha utsṛjantaṃ diṣṭyā dadṛśvān viśadānuvṛttyā
BhP purā mayā proktam ajāya nābhye padme niṣaṇṇāya mamādisarge
BhP jñānaṃ paraṃ manmahimāvabhāsaṃ yat sūrayo bhāgavataṃ vadanti
BhP ity ādṛtoktaḥ paramasya puṃsaḥ pratikṣaṇānugrahabhājano 'ham
BhP snehottharomā skhalitākṣaras taṃ muñcañ chucaḥ prāñjalir ābabhāṣe
BhP ko nv īśa te pādasarojabhājāṃ sudurlabho 'rtheṣu caturṣv apīha
BhP tathāpi nāhaṃ pravṛṇomi bhūman bhavatpadāmbhojaniṣevaṇotsukaḥ
BhP karmāṇy anīhasya bhavo 'bhavasya te durgāśrayo 'thāribhayāt palāyanam
BhP kālātmano yat pramadāyutāśramaḥ svātmanrateḥ khidyati dhīr vidām iha
BhP mantreṣu māṃ vā upahūya yat tvam akuṇṭhitākhaṇḍasadātmabodhaḥ
BhP pṛccheḥ prabho mugdha ivāpramattas tan no mano mohayatīva deva
BhP jñānaṃ paraṃ svātmarahaḥprakāśaṃ provāca kasmai bhagavān samagram
BhP api kṣamaṃ no grahaṇāya bhartar vadāñjasā yad vṛjinaṃ tarema
BhP ity āveditahārdāya mahyaṃ sa bhagavān paraḥ
BhP ādideśāravindākṣa ātmanaḥ paramāṃ sthitim
BhP sa evam ārādhitapādatīrthād adhītatattvātmavibodhamārgaḥ
BhP praṇamya pādau parivṛtya devam ihāgato 'haṃ virahāturātmā
BhP so 'haṃ taddarśanāhlāda viyogārtiyutaḥ prabho
BhP gamiṣye dayitaṃ tasya badaryāśramamaṇḍalam
BhP yatra nārāyaṇo devo naraś ca bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
BhP mṛdu tīvraṃ tapo dīrghaṃ tepāte lokabhāvanau
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity uddhavād upākarṇya suhṛdāṃ duḥsahaṃ vadham
BhP jñānenāśamayat kṣattā śokam utpatitaṃ budhaḥ
BhP sa taṃ mahābhāgavataṃ vrajantaṃ kauravarṣabhaḥ
BhP viśrambhād abhyadhattedaṃ mukhyaṃ kṛṣṇaparigrahe
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP jñānaṃ paraṃ svātmarahaḥprakāśaṃ yad āha yogeśvara īśvaras te
BhP vaktuṃ bhavān no 'rhati yad dhi viṣṇor bhṛtyāḥ svabhṛtyārthakṛtaś caranti
BhP uddhava uvāca
BhP nanu te tattvasaṃrādhya ṛṣiḥ kauṣāravo 'ntike
BhP sākṣād bhagavatādiṣṭo martyalokaṃ jihāsatā
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti saha vidureṇa viśvamūrter guṇakathayā sudhayā plāvitorutāpaḥ
BhP kṣaṇam iva puline yamasvasus tāṃ samuṣita aupagavir niśāṃ tato 'gāt
BhP rājovāca
BhP nidhanam upagateṣu vṛṣṇibhojeṣv adhirathayūthapayūthapeṣu mukhyaḥ
BhP sa tu katham avaśiṣṭa uddhavo yad dharir api tatyaja ākṛtiṃ tryadhīśaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP brahmaśāpāpadeśena kālenāmoghavāñchitaḥ
BhP saṃhṛtya svakulaṃ sphītaṃ tyakṣyan deham acintayat
BhP asmāl lokād uparate mayi jñānaṃ madāśrayam
BhP arhaty uddhava evāddhā sampraty ātmavatāṃ varaḥ
BhP noddhavo 'ṇv api mannyūno yad guṇair nārditaḥ prabhuḥ
BhP ato madvayunaṃ lokaṃ grāhayann iha tiṣṭhatu
BhP evaṃ trilokaguruṇā sandiṣṭaḥ śabdayoninā
BhP badaryāśramam āsādya harim īje samādhinā
BhP viduro 'py uddhavāc chrutvā kṛṣṇasya paramātmanaḥ
BhP krīḍayopāttadehasya karmāṇi ślāghitāni ca
BhP dehanyāsaṃ ca tasyaivaṃ dhīrāṇāṃ dhairyavardhanam
BhP anyeṣāṃ duṣkarataraṃ paśūnāṃ viklavātmanām
BhP ātmānaṃ ca kuruśreṣṭha kṛṣṇena manasekṣitam
BhP dhyāyan gate bhāgavate ruroda premavihvalaḥ
BhP kālindyāḥ katibhiḥ siddha ahobhir bharatarṣabha
BhP prāpadyata svaḥsaritaṃ yatra mitrāsuto muniḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP dvāri dyunadyā ṛṣabhaḥ kurūṇāṃ maitreyam āsīnam agādhabodham
BhP kṣattopasṛtyācyutabhāvasiddhaḥ papraccha sauśīlyaguṇābhitṛptaḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP sukhāya karmāṇi karoti loko na taiḥ sukhaṃ vānyadupāramaṃ vā
BhP vindeta bhūyas tata eva duḥkhaṃ yad atra yuktaṃ bhagavān vaden naḥ
BhP janasya kṛṣṇād vimukhasya daivād adharmaśīlasya suduḥkhitasya
BhP anugrahāyeha caranti nūnaṃ bhūtāni bhavyāni janārdanasya
BhP tat sādhuvaryādiśa vartma śaṃ naḥ saṃrādhito bhagavān yena puṃsām
BhP hṛdi sthito yacchati bhaktipūte jñānaṃ satattvādhigamaṃ purāṇam
BhP karoti karmāṇi kṛtāvatāro yāny ātmatantro bhagavāṃs tryadhīśaḥ
BhP yathā sasarjāgra idaṃ nirīhaḥ saṃsthāpya vṛttiṃ jagato vidhatte
BhP yathā punaḥ sve kha idaṃ niveśya śete guhāyāṃ sa nivṛttavṛttiḥ
BhP yogeśvarādhīśvara eka etad anupraviṣṭo bahudhā yathāsīt
BhP krīḍan vidhatte dvijagosurāṇāṃ kṣemāya karmāṇy avatārabhedaiḥ
BhP mano na tṛpyaty api śṛṇvatāṃ naḥ suślokamauleś caritāmṛtāni
BhP yais tattvabhedair adhilokanātho lokān alokān saha lokapālān
BhP acīkḷpad yatra hi sarvasattva nikāyabhedo 'dhikṛtaḥ pratītaḥ
BhP yena prajānām uta ātmakarma rūpābhidhānāṃ ca bhidāṃ vyadhatta
BhP nārāyaṇo viśvasṛg ātmayonir etac ca no varṇaya vipravarya
BhP parāvareṣāṃ bhagavan vratāni śrutāni me vyāsamukhād abhīkṣṇam
BhP atṛpnuma kṣullasukhāvahānāṃ teṣām ṛte kṛṣṇakathāmṛtaughāt
BhP kas tṛpnuyāt tīrthapado 'bhidhānāt satreṣu vaḥ sūribhir īḍyamānāt
BhP yaḥ karṇanāḍīṃ puruṣasya yāto bhavapradāṃ geharatiṃ chinatti
BhP munir vivakṣur bhagavadguṇānāṃ sakhāpi te bhāratam āha kṛṣṇaḥ
BhP yasmin nṛṇāṃ grāmyasukhānuvādair matir gṛhītā nu hareḥ kathāyām
BhP sā śraddadhānasya vivardhamānā viraktim anyatra karoti puṃsaḥ
BhP hareḥ padānusmṛtinirvṛtasya samastaduḥkhāpyayam āśu dhatte
BhP tāñ chocyaśocyān avido 'nuśoce hareḥ kathāyāṃ vimukhān aghena
BhP kṣiṇoti devo 'nimiṣas tu yeṣām āyur vṛthāvādagatismṛtīnām
BhP tad asya kauṣārava śarmadātur hareḥ kathām eva kathāsu sāram
BhP uddhṛtya puṣpebhya ivārtabandho śivāya naḥ kīrtaya tīrthakīrteḥ
BhP sa viśvajanmasthitisaṃyamārthe kṛtāvatāraḥ pragṛhītaśaktiḥ
BhP cakāra karmāṇy atipūruṣāṇi yānīśvaraḥ kīrtaya tāni mahyam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa evaṃ bhagavān pṛṣṭaḥ kṣattrā kauṣāravo muniḥ
BhP puṃsāṃ niḥśreyasārthena tam āha bahumānayan
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā sādho lokān sādhv anugṛhṇatā
BhP kīrtiṃ vitanvatā loke ātmano 'dhokṣajātmanaḥ
BhP naitac citraṃ tvayi kṣattar bādarāyaṇavīryaje
BhP gṛhīto 'nanyabhāvena yat tvayā harir īśvaraḥ
BhP māṇḍavyaśāpād bhagavān prajāsaṃyamano yamaḥ
BhP bhrātuḥ kṣetre bhujiṣyāyāṃ jātaḥ satyavatīsutāt
BhP bhavān bhagavato nityaṃ sammataḥ sānugasya ha
BhP yasya jñānopadeśāya mādiśad bhagavān vrajan
BhP atha te bhagavallīlā yogamāyorubṛṃhitāḥ
BhP viśvasthityudbhavāntārthā varṇayāmy anupūrvaśaḥ
BhP bhagavān eka āsedam agra ātmātmanāṃ vibhuḥ
BhP ātmecchānugatāv ātmā nānāmatyupalakṣaṇaḥ
BhP sa vā eṣa tadā draṣṭā nāpaśyad dṛśyam ekarāṭ
BhP mene 'santam ivātmānaṃ suptaśaktir asuptadṛk
BhP sā vā etasya saṃdraṣṭuḥ śaktiḥ sadasadātmikā
BhP māyā nāma mahābhāga yayedaṃ nirmame vibhuḥ
BhP kālavṛttyā tu māyāyāṃ guṇamayyām adhokṣajaḥ
BhP puruṣeṇātmabhūtena vīryam ādhatta vīryavān
BhP tato 'bhavan mahattattvam avyaktāt kālacoditāt
BhP vijñānātmātmadehasthaṃ viśvaṃ vyañjaṃs tamonudaḥ
BhP so 'py aṃśaguṇakālātmā bhagavaddṛṣṭigocaraḥ
BhP ātmānaṃ vyakarod ātmā viśvasyāsya sisṛkṣayā
BhP mahattattvād vikurvāṇād ahaṃtattvaṃ vyajāyata
BhP kāryakāraṇakartrātmā bhūtendriyamanomayaḥ
BhP vaikārikas taijasaś ca tāmasaś cety ahaṃ tridhā
BhP ahaṃtattvād vikurvāṇān mano vaikārikād abhūt
BhP vaikārikāś ca ye devā arthābhivyañjanaṃ yataḥ
BhP taijasānīndriyāṇy eva jñānakarmamayāni ca
BhP tāmaso bhūtasūkṣmādir yataḥ khaṃ liṅgam ātmanaḥ
BhP kālamāyāṃśayogena bhagavadvīkṣitaṃ nabhaḥ
BhP nabhaso 'nusṛtaṃ sparśaṃ vikurvan nirmame 'nilam
BhP anilo 'pi vikurvāṇo nabhasorubalānvitaḥ
BhP sasarja rūpatanmātraṃ jyotir lokasya locanam
BhP anilenānvitaṃ jyotir vikurvat paravīkṣitam
BhP ādhattāmbho rasamayaṃ kālamāyāṃśayogataḥ
BhP jyotiṣāmbho 'nusaṃsṛṣṭaṃ vikurvad brahmavīkṣitam
BhP mahīṃ gandhaguṇām ādhāt kālamāyāṃśayogataḥ
BhP bhūtānāṃ nabhaādīnāṃ yad yad bhavyāvarāvaram
BhP teṣāṃ parānusaṃsargād yathā saṅkhyaṃ guṇān viduḥ
BhP ete devāḥ kalā viṣṇoḥ kālamāyāṃśaliṅginaḥ
BhP nānātvāt svakriyānīśāḥ procuḥ prāñjalayo vibhum
BhP devā ūcuḥ
BhP namāma te deva padāravindaṃ prapannatāpopaśamātapatram
BhP yanmūlaketā yatayo 'ñjasoru saṃsāraduḥkhaṃ bahir utkṣipanti
BhP dhātar yad asmin bhava īśa jīvās tāpatrayeṇābhihatā na śarma
BhP ātman labhante bhagavaṃs tavāṅghri cchāyāṃ savidyām ata āśrayema
BhP mārganti yat te mukhapadmanīḍaiś chandaḥsuparṇair ṛṣayo vivikte
BhP yasyāghamarṣodasaridvarāyāḥ padaṃ padaṃ tīrthapadaḥ prapannāḥ
BhP yac chraddhayā śrutavatyā ca bhaktyā sammṛjyamāne hṛdaye 'vadhāya
BhP jñānena vairāgyabalena dhīrā vrajema tat te 'ṅghrisarojapīṭham
BhP viśvasya janmasthitisaṃyamārthe kṛtāvatārasya padāmbujaṃ te
BhP vrajema sarve śaraṇaṃ yad īśa smṛtaṃ prayacchaty abhayaṃ svapuṃsām
BhP yat sānubandhe 'sati dehagehe mamāham ity ūḍhadurāgrahāṇām
BhP puṃsāṃ sudūraṃ vasato 'pi puryāṃ bhajema tat te bhagavan padābjam
BhP tān vai hy asadvṛttibhir akṣibhir ye parāhṛtāntarmanasaḥ pareśa
BhP atho na paśyanty urugāya nūnaṃ ye te padanyāsavilāsalakṣyāḥ
BhP pānena te deva kathāsudhāyāḥ pravṛddhabhaktyā viśadāśayā ye
BhP vairāgyasāraṃ pratilabhya bodhaṃ yathāñjasānvīyur akuṇṭhadhiṣṇyam
BhP tathāpare cātmasamādhiyoga balena jitvā prakṛtiṃ baliṣṭhām
BhP tvām eva dhīrāḥ puruṣaṃ viśanti teṣāṃ śramaḥ syān na tu sevayā te
BhP tat te vayaṃ lokasisṛkṣayādya tvayānusṛṣṭās tribhir ātmabhiḥ sma
BhP sarve viyuktāḥ svavihāratantraṃ na śaknumas tat pratihartave te
BhP yāvad baliṃ te 'ja harāma kāle yathā vayaṃ cānnam adāma yatra
BhP yathobhayeṣāṃ ta ime hi lokā baliṃ haranto 'nnam adanty anūhāḥ
BhP tvaṃ naḥ surāṇām asi sānvayānāṃ kūṭastha ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ
BhP tvaṃ deva śaktyāṃ guṇakarmayonau retas tv ajāyāṃ kavim ādadhe 'jaḥ
BhP tato vayaṃ matpramukhā yadarthe babhūvimātman karavāma kiṃ te
BhP tvaṃ naḥ svacakṣuḥ paridehi śaktyā deva kriyārthe yadanugrahāṇām
BhP ṛṣir uvāca
BhP iti tāsāṃ svaśaktīnāṃ satīnām asametya saḥ
BhP prasuptalokatantrāṇāṃ niśāmya gatim īśvaraḥ
BhP kālasañjñāṃ tadā devīṃ bibhracchaktim urukramaḥ
BhP trayoviṃśati tattvānāṃ gaṇaṃ yugapad āviśat
BhP so 'nupraviṣṭo bhagavāṃś ceṣṭārūpeṇa taṃ gaṇam
BhP bhinnaṃ saṃyojayām āsa suptaṃ karma prabodhayan
BhP prabuddhakarma daivena trayoviṃśatiko gaṇaḥ
BhP prerito 'janayat svābhir mātrābhir adhipūruṣam
BhP pareṇa viśatā svasmin mātrayā viśvasṛggaṇaḥ
BhP cukṣobhānyonyam āsādya yasmin lokāś carācarāḥ
BhP hiraṇmayaḥ sa puruṣaḥ sahasraparivatsarān
BhP āṇḍakośa uvāsāpsu sarvasattvopabṛṃhitaḥ
BhP sa vai viśvasṛjāṃ garbho devakarmātmaśaktimān
BhP vibabhājātmanātmānam ekadhā daśadhā tridhā
BhP eṣa hy aśeṣasattvānām ātmāṃśaḥ paramātmanaḥ
BhP ādyo 'vatāro yatrāsau bhūtagrāmo vibhāvyate
BhP sādhyātmaḥ sādhidaivaś ca sādhibhūta iti tridhā
BhP virāṭ prāṇo daśavidha ekadhā hṛdayena ca
BhP smaran viśvasṛjām īśo vijñāpitam adhokṣajaḥ
BhP virājam atapat svena tejasaiṣāṃ vivṛttaye
BhP atha tasyābhitaptasya katidhāyatanāni ha
BhP nirabhidyanta devānāṃ tāni me gadataḥ śṛṇu
BhP tasyāgnir āsyaṃ nirbhinnaṃ lokapālo 'viśat padam
BhP vācā svāṃśena vaktavyaṃ yayāsau pratipadyate
BhP nirbhinnaṃ tālu varuṇo lokapālo 'viśad dhareḥ
BhP jihvayāṃśena ca rasaṃ yayāsau pratipadyate
BhP nirbhinne aśvinau nāse viṣṇor āviśatāṃ padam
BhP ghrāṇenāṃśena gandhasya pratipattir yato bhavet
BhP nirbhinne akṣiṇī tvaṣṭā lokapālo 'viśad vibhoḥ
BhP cakṣuṣāṃśena rūpāṇāṃ pratipattir yato bhavet
BhP nirbhinnāny asya carmāṇi lokapālo 'nilo 'viśat
BhP prāṇenāṃśena saṃsparśaṃ yenāsau pratipadyate
BhP karṇāv asya vinirbhinnau dhiṣṇyaṃ svaṃ viviśur diśaḥ
BhP śrotreṇāṃśena śabdasya siddhiṃ yena prapadyate
BhP tvacam asya vinirbhinnāṃ viviśur dhiṣṇyam oṣadhīḥ
BhP aṃśena romabhiḥ kaṇḍūṃ yair asau pratipadyate
BhP meḍhraṃ tasya vinirbhinnaṃ svadhiṣṇyaṃ ka upāviśat
BhP retasāṃśena yenāsāv ānandaṃ pratipadyate
BhP gudaṃ puṃso vinirbhinnaṃ mitro lokeśa āviśat
BhP pāyunāṃśena yenāsau visargaṃ pratipadyate
BhP hastāv asya vinirbhinnāv indraḥ svarpatir āviśat
BhP vārtayāṃśena puruṣo yayā vṛttiṃ prapadyate
BhP pādāv asya vinirbhinnau lokeśo viṣṇur āviśat
BhP gatyā svāṃśena puruṣo yayā prāpyaṃ prapadyate
BhP buddhiṃ cāsya vinirbhinnāṃ vāgīśo dhiṣṇyam āviśat
BhP bodhenāṃśena boddhavyam pratipattir yato bhavet
BhP hṛdayaṃ cāsya nirbhinnaṃ candramā dhiṣṇyam āviśat
BhP manasāṃśena yenāsau vikriyāṃ pratipadyate
BhP ātmānaṃ cāsya nirbhinnam abhimāno 'viśat padam
BhP karmaṇāṃśena yenāsau kartavyaṃ pratipadyate
BhP sattvaṃ cāsya vinirbhinnaṃ mahān dhiṣṇyam upāviśat
BhP cittenāṃśena yenāsau vijñānaṃ pratipadyate
BhP śīrṣṇo 'sya dyaur dharā padbhyāṃ khaṃ nābher udapadyata
BhP guṇānāṃ vṛttayo yeṣu pratīyante surādayaḥ
BhP ātyantikena sattvena divaṃ devāḥ prapedire
BhP dharāṃ rajaḥsvabhāvena paṇayo ye ca tān anu
BhP tārtīyena svabhāvena bhagavannābhim āśritāḥ
BhP ubhayor antaraṃ vyoma ye rudrapārṣadāṃ gaṇāḥ
BhP mukhato 'vartata brahma puruṣasya kurūdvaha
BhP yas tūnmukhatvād varṇānāṃ mukhyo 'bhūd brāhmaṇo guruḥ
BhP bāhubhyo 'vartata kṣatraṃ kṣatriyas tad anuvrataḥ
BhP yo jātas trāyate varṇān pauruṣaḥ kaṇṭakakṣatāt
BhP viśo 'vartanta tasyorvor lokavṛttikarīr vibhoḥ
BhP vaiśyas tadudbhavo vārtāṃ nṛṇāṃ yaḥ samavartayat
BhP padbhyāṃ bhagavato jajñe śuśrūṣā dharmasiddhaye
BhP tasyāṃ jātaḥ purā śūdro yadvṛttyā tuṣyate hariḥ
BhP ete varṇāḥ svadharmeṇa yajanti svaguruṃ harim
BhP śraddhayātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ yajjātāḥ saha vṛttibhiḥ
BhP etat kṣattar bhagavato daivakarmātmarūpiṇaḥ
BhP kaḥ śraddadhyād upākartuṃ yogamāyābalodayam
BhP tathāpi kīrtayāmy aṅga yathāmati yathāśrutam
BhP kīrtiṃ hareḥ svāṃ satkartuṃ giram anyābhidhāsatīm
BhP ekāntalābhaṃ vacaso nu puṃsāṃ suślokamauler guṇavādam āhuḥ
BhP śruteś ca vidvadbhir upākṛtāyāṃ kathāsudhāyām upasamprayogam
BhP ātmano 'vasito vatsa mahimā kavinādinā
BhP saṃvatsarasahasrānte dhiyā yogavipakkayā
BhP ato bhagavato māyā māyinām api mohinī
BhP yat svayaṃ cātmavartmātmā na veda kim utāpare
BhP yato 'prāpya nyavartanta vācaś ca manasā saha
BhP ahaṃ cānya ime devās tasmai bhagavate namaḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ maitreyaṃ dvaipāyanasuto budhaḥ
BhP prīṇayann iva bhāratyā viduraḥ pratyabhāṣata
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP brahman kathaṃ bhagavataś cinmātrasyāvikāriṇaḥ
BhP līlayā cāpi yujyeran nirguṇasya guṇāḥ kriyāḥ
BhP krīḍāyām udyamo 'rbhasya kāmaś cikrīḍiṣānyataḥ
BhP svatastṛptasya ca kathaṃ nivṛttasya sadānyataḥ
BhP asrākṣīd bhagavān viśvaṃ guṇamayyātmamāyayā
BhP tayā saṃsthāpayaty etad bhūyaḥ pratyapidhāsyati
BhP deśataḥ kālato yo 'sāv avasthātaḥ svato 'nyataḥ
BhP aviluptāvabodhātmā sa yujyetājayā katham
BhP bhagavān eka evaiṣa sarvakṣetreṣv avasthitaḥ
BhP amuṣya durbhagatvaṃ vā kleśo vā karmabhiḥ kutaḥ
BhP etasmin me mano vidvan khidyate 'jñānasaṅkaṭe
BhP tan naḥ parāṇuda vibho kaśmalaṃ mānasaṃ mahat
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa itthaṃ coditaḥ kṣattrā tattvajijñāsunā muniḥ
BhP pratyāha bhagavaccittaḥ smayann iva gatasmayaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP seyaṃ bhagavato māyā yan nayena virudhyate
BhP īśvarasya vimuktasya kārpaṇyam uta bandhanam
BhP yad arthena vināmuṣya puṃsa ātmaviparyayaḥ
BhP pratīyata upadraṣṭuḥ svaśiraś chedanādikaḥ
BhP yathā jale candramasaḥ kampādis tatkṛto guṇaḥ
BhP dṛśyate 'sann api draṣṭur ātmano 'nātmano guṇaḥ
BhP sa vai nivṛttidharmeṇa vāsudevānukampayā
BhP bhagavadbhaktiyogena tirodhatte śanair iha
BhP yadendriyoparāmo 'tha draṣṭrātmani pare harau
BhP vilīyante tadā kleśāḥ saṃsuptasyeva kṛtsnaśaḥ
BhP aśeṣasaṅkleśaśamaṃ vidhatte guṇānuvādaśravaṇaṃ murāreḥ
BhP kiṃ vā punas taccaraṇāravinda parāgasevāratir ātmalabdhā
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP sañchinnaḥ saṃśayo mahyaṃ tava sūktāsinā vibho
BhP ubhayatrāpi bhagavan mano me sampradhāvati
BhP sādhv etad vyāhṛtaṃ vidvan nātmamāyāyanaṃ hareḥ
BhP ābhāty apārthaṃ nirmūlaṃ viśvamūlaṃ na yad bahiḥ
BhP yaś ca mūḍhatamo loke yaś ca buddheḥ paraṃ gataḥ
BhP tāv ubhau sukham edhete kliśyaty antarito janaḥ
BhP arthābhāvaṃ viniścitya pratītasyāpi nātmanaḥ
BhP tāṃ cāpi yuṣmaccaraṇa sevayāhaṃ parāṇude
BhP yatsevayā bhagavataḥ kūṭasthasya madhudviṣaḥ
BhP ratirāso bhavet tīvraḥ pādayor vyasanārdanaḥ
BhP durāpā hy alpatapasaḥ sevā vaikuṇṭhavartmasu
BhP yatropagīyate nityaṃ devadevo janārdanaḥ
BhP sṛṣṭvāgre mahadādīni savikārāṇy anukramāt
BhP tebhyo virājam uddhṛtya tam anu prāviśad vibhuḥ
BhP yam āhur ādyaṃ puruṣaṃ sahasrāṅghryūrubāhukam
BhP yatra viśva ime lokāḥ savikāśaṃ ta āsate
BhP yasmin daśavidhaḥ prāṇaḥ sendriyārthendriyas trivṛt
BhP tvayerito yato varṇās tadvibhūtīr vadasva naḥ
BhP yatra putraiś ca pautraiś ca naptṛbhiḥ saha gotrajaiḥ
BhP prajā vicitrākṛtaya āsan yābhir idaṃ tatam
BhP prajāpatīnāṃ sa patiś cakḷpe kān prajāpatīn
BhP sargāṃś caivānusargāṃś ca manūn manvantarādhipān
BhP eteṣām api vedāṃś ca vaṃśānucaritāni ca
BhP upary adhaś ca ye lokā bhūmer mitrātmajāsate
BhP teṣāṃ saṃsthāṃ pramāṇaṃ ca bhūrlokasya ca varṇaya
BhP tiryaṅmānuṣadevānāṃ sarīsṛpapatattriṇām
BhP vada naḥ sargasaṃvyūhaṃ gārbhasvedadvijodbhidām
BhP guṇāvatārair viśvasya sargasthityapyayāśrayam
BhP sṛjataḥ śrīnivāsasya vyācakṣvodāravikramam
BhP varṇāśramavibhāgāṃś ca rūpaśīlasvabhāvataḥ
BhP ṛṣīṇāṃ janmakarmāṇi vedasya ca vikarṣaṇam
BhP yajñasya ca vitānāni yogasya ca pathaḥ prabho
BhP naiṣkarmyasya ca sāṅkhyasya tantraṃ vā bhagavatsmṛtam
BhP pāṣaṇḍapathavaiṣamyaṃ pratilomaniveśanam
BhP jīvasya gatayo yāś ca yāvatīr guṇakarmajāḥ
BhP dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ nimittāny avirodhataḥ
BhP vārtāyā daṇḍanīteś ca śrutasya ca vidhiṃ pṛthak
BhP śrāddhasya ca vidhiṃ brahman pitṇāṃ sargam eva ca
BhP grahanakṣatratārāṇāṃ kālāvayavasaṃsthitim
BhP dānasya tapaso vāpi yac ceṣṭāpūrtayoḥ phalam
BhP pravāsasthasya yo dharmo yaś ca puṃsa utāpadi
BhP yena vā bhagavāṃs tuṣyed dharmayonir janārdanaḥ
BhP samprasīdati vā yeṣām etad ākhyāhi me 'nagha
BhP anuvratānāṃ śiṣyāṇāṃ putrāṇāṃ ca dvijottama
BhP anāpṛṣṭam api brūyur guravo dīnavatsalāḥ
BhP tattvānāṃ bhagavaṃs teṣāṃ katidhā pratisaṅkramaḥ
BhP tatremaṃ ka upāsīran ka u svid anuśerate
BhP puruṣasya ca saṃsthānaṃ svarūpaṃ vā parasya ca
BhP jñānaṃ ca naigamaṃ yat tad guruśiṣyaprayojanam
BhP nimittāni ca tasyeha proktāny anaghasūribhiḥ
BhP svato jñānaṃ kutaḥ puṃsāṃ bhaktir vairāgyam eva vā
BhP etān me pṛcchataḥ praśnān hareḥ karmavivitsayā
BhP brūhi me 'jñasya mitratvād ajayā naṣṭacakṣuṣaḥ
BhP sarve vedāś ca yajñāś ca tapo dānāni cānagha
BhP jīvābhayapradānasya na kurvīran kalām api
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP sa ittham āpṛṣṭapurāṇakalpaḥ kurupradhānena munipradhānaḥ
BhP pravṛddhaharṣo bhagavatkathāyāṃ sañcoditas taṃ prahasann ivāha
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP satsevanīyo bata pūruvaṃśo yal lokapālo bhagavatpradhānaḥ
BhP babhūvithehājitakīrtimālāṃ pade pade nūtanayasy abhīkṣṇam
BhP so 'haṃ nṛṇāṃ kṣullasukhāya duḥkhaṃ mahad gatānāṃ viramāya tasya
BhP pravartaye bhāgavataṃ purāṇaṃ yad āha sākṣād bhagavān ṛṣibhyaḥ
BhP āsīnam urvyāṃ bhagavantam ādyaṃ saṅkarṣaṇaṃ devam akuṇṭhasattvam
BhP vivitsavas tattvam ataḥ parasya kumāramukhyā munayo 'nvapṛcchan
BhP svam eva dhiṣṇyaṃ bahu mānayantaṃ yad vāsudevābhidham āmananti
BhP pratyagdhṛtākṣāmbujakośam īṣad unmīlayantaṃ vibudhodayāya
BhP svardhunyudārdraiḥ svajaṭākalāpair upaspṛśantaś caraṇopadhānam
BhP padmaṃ yad arcanty ahirājakanyāḥ saprema nānābalibhir varārthāḥ
BhP muhur gṛṇanto vacasānurāga skhalatpadenāsya kṛtāni tajjñāḥ
BhP kirīṭasāhasramaṇipraveka pradyotitoddāmaphaṇāsahasram
BhP proktaṃ kilaitad bhagavattamena nivṛttidharmābhiratāya tena
BhP sanatkumārāya sa cāha pṛṣṭaḥ sāṅkhyāyanāyāṅga dhṛtavratāya
BhP sāṅkhyāyanaḥ pāramahaṃsyamukhyo vivakṣamāṇo bhagavadvibhūtīḥ
BhP jagāda so 'smadgurave 'nvitāya parāśarāyātha bṛhaspateś ca
BhP provāca mahyaṃ sa dayālur ukto muniḥ pulastyena purāṇam ādyam
BhP so 'haṃ tavaitat kathayāmi vatsa śraddhālave nityam anuvratāya
BhP udāplutaṃ viśvam idaṃ tadāsīd yan nidrayāmīlitadṛṅ nyamīlayat
BhP ahīndratalpe 'dhiśayāna ekaḥ kṛtakṣaṇaḥ svātmaratau nirīhaḥ
BhP so 'ntaḥ śarīre 'rpitabhūtasūkṣmaḥ kālātmikāṃ śaktim udīrayāṇaḥ
BhP uvāsa tasmin salile pade sve yathānalo dāruṇi ruddhavīryaḥ
BhP caturyugānāṃ ca sahasram apsu svapan svayodīritayā svaśaktyā
BhP kālākhyayāsāditakarmatantro lokān apītān dadṛśe svadehe
BhP tasyārthasūkṣmābhiniviṣṭadṛṣṭer antargato 'rtho rajasā tanīyān
BhP guṇena kālānugatena viddhaḥ sūṣyaṃs tadābhidyata nābhideśāt
BhP sa padmakośaḥ sahasodatiṣṭhat kālena karmapratibodhanena
BhP svarociṣā tat salilaṃ viśālaṃ vidyotayann arka ivātmayoniḥ
BhP tal lokapadmaṃ sa u eva viṣṇuḥ prāvīviśat sarvaguṇāvabhāsam
BhP tasmin svayaṃ vedamayo vidhātā svayambhuvaṃ yaṃ sma vadanti so 'bhūt
BhP tasyāṃ sa cāmbhoruhakarṇikāyām avasthito lokam apaśyamānaḥ
BhP parikraman vyomni vivṛttanetraś catvāri lebhe 'nudiśaṃ mukhāni
BhP tasmād yugāntaśvasanāvaghūrṇa jalormicakrāt salilād virūḍham
BhP upāśritaḥ kañjam u lokatattvaṃ nātmānam addhāvidad ādidevaḥ
BhP ka eṣa yo 'sāv aham abjapṛṣṭha etat kuto vābjam ananyad apsu
BhP asti hy adhastād iha kiñcanaitad adhiṣṭhitaṃ yatra satā nu bhāvyam
BhP sa ittham udvīkṣya tadabjanāla nāḍībhir antarjalam āviveśa
BhP nārvāggatas tatkharanālanāla nābhiṃ vicinvaṃs tad avindatājaḥ
BhP tamasy apāre vidurātmasargaṃ vicinvato 'bhūt sumahāṃs triṇemiḥ
BhP yo dehabhājāṃ bhayam īrayāṇaḥ parikṣiṇoty āyur ajasya hetiḥ
BhP tato nivṛtto 'pratilabdhakāmaḥ svadhiṣṇyam āsādya punaḥ sa devaḥ
BhP śanair jitaśvāsanivṛttacitto nyaṣīdad ārūḍhasamādhiyogaḥ
BhP kālena so 'jaḥ puruṣāyuṣābhi pravṛttayogena virūḍhabodhaḥ
BhP svayaṃ tad antarhṛdaye 'vabhātam apaśyatāpaśyata yan na pūrvam
BhP mṛṇālagaurāyataśeṣabhoga paryaṅka ekaṃ puruṣaṃ śayānam
BhP phaṇātapatrāyutamūrdharatna dyubhir hatadhvāntayugāntatoye
BhP prekṣāṃ kṣipantaṃ haritopalādreḥ sandhyābhranīver ururukmamūrdhnaḥ
BhP ratnodadhārauṣadhisaumanasya vanasrajo veṇubhujāṅghripāṅghreḥ
BhP āyāmato vistarataḥ svamāna dehena lokatrayasaṅgraheṇa
BhP vicitradivyābharaṇāṃśukānāṃ kṛtaśriyāpāśritaveṣadeham
BhP puṃsāṃ svakāmāya viviktamārgair abhyarcatāṃ kāmadughāṅghripadmam
BhP pradarśayantaṃ kṛpayā nakhendu mayūkhabhinnāṅgulicārupatram
BhP mukhena lokārtiharasmitena parisphuratkuṇḍalamaṇḍitena
BhP śoṇāyitenādharabimbabhāsā pratyarhayantaṃ sunasena subhrvā
BhP kadambakiñjalkapiśaṅgavāsasā svalaṅkṛtaṃ mekhalayā nitambe
BhP hāreṇa cānantadhanena vatsa śrīvatsavakṣaḥsthalavallabhena
BhP parārdhyakeyūramaṇipraveka paryastadordaṇḍasahasraśākham
BhP avyaktamūlaṃ bhuvanāṅghripendram ahīndrabhogair adhivītavalśam
BhP carācarauko bhagavanmahīdhram ahīndrabandhuṃ salilopagūḍham
BhP kirīṭasāhasrahiraṇyaśṛṅgam āvirbhavat kaustubharatnagarbham
BhP nivītam āmnāyamadhuvrataśriyā svakīrtimayyā vanamālayā harim
BhP sūryenduvāyvagnyagamaṃ tridhāmabhiḥ parikramatprādhanikair durāsadam
BhP tarhy eva tannābhisaraḥsarojam ātmānam ambhaḥ śvasanaṃ viyac ca
BhP dadarśa devo jagato vidhātā nātaḥ paraṃ lokavisargadṛṣṭiḥ
BhP sa karmabījaṃ rajasoparaktaḥ prajāḥ sisṛkṣann iyad eva dṛṣṭvā
BhP astaud visargābhimukhas tam īḍyam avyaktavartmany abhiveśitātmā
BhP brahmovāca
BhP jñāto 'si me 'dya sucirān nanu dehabhājāṃ
BhP na jñāyate bhagavato gatir ity avadyam
BhP nānyat tvad asti bhagavann api tan na śuddhaṃ
BhP māyāguṇavyatikarād yad urur vibhāsi
BhP rūpaṃ yad etad avabodharasodayena
BhP śaśvannivṛttatamasaḥ sadanugrahāya
BhP ādau gṛhītam avatāraśataikabījaṃ
BhP yannābhipadmabhavanād aham āvirāsam
BhP nātaḥ paraṃ parama yad bhavataḥ svarūpam
BhP ānandamātram avikalpam aviddhavarcaḥ
BhP paśyāmi viśvasṛjam ekam aviśvam ātman
BhP bhūtendriyātmakamadas ta upāśrito 'smi
BhP tad vā idaṃ bhuvanamaṅgala maṅgalāya
BhP dhyāne sma no darśitaṃ ta upāsakānām
BhP tasmai namo bhagavate 'nuvidhema tubhyaṃ
BhP yo 'nādṛto narakabhāgbhir asatprasaṅgaiḥ
BhP ye tu tvadīyacaraṇāmbujakośagandhaṃ
BhP jighranti karṇavivaraiḥ śrutivātanītam
BhP bhaktyā gṛhītacaraṇaḥ parayā ca teṣāṃ
BhP nāpaiṣi nātha hṛdayāmburuhāt svapuṃsām
BhP tāvad bhayaṃ draviṇadehasuhṛnnimittaṃ
BhP śokaḥ spṛhā paribhavo vipulaś ca lobhaḥ
BhP tāvan mamety asadavagraha ārtimūlaṃ
BhP yāvan na te 'ṅghrim abhayaṃ pravṛṇīta lokaḥ
BhP daivena te hatadhiyo bhavataḥ prasaṅgāt
BhP sarvāśubhopaśamanād vimukhendriyā ye
BhP kurvanti kāmasukhaleśalavāya dīnā
BhP lobhābhibhūtamanaso 'kuśalāni śaśvat
BhP kṣuttṛṭtridhātubhir imā muhur ardyamānāḥ
BhP śītoṣṇavātavaraṣair itaretarāc ca
BhP kāmāgninācyutaruṣā ca sudurbhareṇa
BhP sampaśyato mana urukrama sīdate me
BhP yāvat pṛthaktvam idam ātmana indriyārtha
BhP māyābalaṃ bhagavato jana īśa paśyet
BhP tāvan na saṃsṛtir asau pratisaṅkrameta
BhP vyarthāpi duḥkhanivahaṃ vahatī kriyārthā
BhP ahny āpṛtārtakaraṇā niśi niḥśayānā
BhP nānāmanorathadhiyā kṣaṇabhagnanidrāḥ
BhP daivāhatārtharacanā ṛṣayo 'pi deva
BhP yuṣmatprasaṅgavimukhā iha saṃsaranti
BhP tvaṃ bhaktiyogaparibhāvitahṛtsaroja
BhP āsse śrutekṣitapatho nanu nātha puṃsām
BhP yadyaddhiyā ta urugāya vibhāvayanti
BhP tattadvapuḥ praṇayase sadanugrahāya
BhP nātiprasīdati tathopacitopacārair
BhP ārādhitaḥ suragaṇair hṛdi baddhakāmaiḥ
BhP yat sarvabhūtadayayāsadalabhyayaiko
BhP nānājaneṣv avahitaḥ suhṛd antarātmā
BhP puṃsām ato vividhakarmabhir adhvarādyair
BhP dānena cogratapasā paricaryayā ca
BhP ārādhanaṃ bhagavatas tava satkriyārtho
BhP dharmo 'rpitaḥ karhicid mriyate na yatra
BhP śaśvat svarūpamahasaiva nipītabheda
BhP mohāya bodhadhiṣaṇāya namaḥ parasmai
BhP viśvodbhavasthitilayeṣu nimittalīlā
BhP rāsāya te nama idaṃ cakṛmeśvarāya
BhP yasyāvatāraguṇakarmaviḍambanāni
BhP nāmāni ye 'suvigame vivaśā gṛṇanti
BhP te 'naikajanmaśamalaṃ sahasaiva hitvā
BhP saṃyānty apāvṛtāmṛtaṃ tam ajaṃ prapadye
BhP yo vā ahaṃ ca giriśaś ca vibhuḥ svayaṃ ca
BhP sthityudbhavapralayahetava ātmamūlam
BhP bhittvā tripād vavṛdha eka uruprarohas
BhP tasmai namo bhagavate bhuvanadrumāya
BhP loko vikarmanirataḥ kuśale pramattaḥ
BhP karmaṇy ayaṃ tvadudite bhavadarcane sve
BhP yas tāvad asya balavān iha jīvitāśāṃ
BhP sadyaś chinatty animiṣāya namo 'stu tasmai
BhP yasmād bibhemy aham api dviparārdhadhiṣṇyam
BhP adhyāsitaḥ sakalalokanamaskṛtaṃ yat
BhP tepe tapo bahusavo 'varurutsamānas
BhP tasmai namo bhagavate 'dhimakhāya tubhyam
BhP tiryaṅmanuṣyavibudhādiṣu jīvayoniṣv
BhP ātmecchayātmakṛtasetuparīpsayā yaḥ
BhP reme nirastaviṣayo 'py avaruddhadehas
BhP tasmai namo bhagavate puruṣottamāya
BhP yo 'vidyayānupahato 'pi daśārdhavṛttyā
BhP nidrām uvāha jaṭharīkṛtalokayātraḥ
BhP antarjale 'hikaśipusparśānukūlāṃ
BhP bhīmormimālini janasya sukhaṃ vivṛṇvan
BhP yannābhipadmabhavanād aham āsam īḍya
BhP lokatrayopakaraṇo yadanugraheṇa
BhP tasmai namas ta udarasthabhavāya yoga
BhP nidrāvasānavikasannalinekṣaṇāya
BhP so 'yaṃ samastajagatāṃ suhṛd eka ātmā
BhP sattvena yan mṛḍayate bhagavān bhagena
BhP tenaiva me dṛśam anuspṛśatād yathāhaṃ
BhP srakṣyāmi pūrvavad idaṃ praṇatapriyo 'sau
BhP eṣa prapannavarado ramayātmaśaktyā
BhP yad yat kariṣyati gṛhītaguṇāvatāraḥ
BhP tasmin svavikramam idaṃ sṛjato 'pi ceto
BhP yuñjīta karmaśamalaṃ ca yathā vijahyām
BhP nābhihradād iha sato 'mbhasi yasya puṃso
BhP vijñānaśaktir aham āsam anantaśakteḥ
BhP rūpaṃ vicitram idam asya vivṛṇvato me
BhP mā rīriṣīṣṭa nigamasya girāṃ visargaḥ
BhP so 'sāv adabhrakaruṇo bhagavān vivṛddha
BhP premasmitena nayanāmburuhaṃ vijṛmbhan
BhP utthāya viśvavijayāya ca no viṣādaṃ
BhP mādhvyā girāpanayatāt puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP svasambhavaṃ niśāmyaivaṃ tapovidyāsamādhibhiḥ
BhP yāvan manovacaḥ stutvā virarāma sa khinnavat
BhP athābhipretam anvīkṣya brahmaṇo madhusūdanaḥ
BhP viṣaṇṇacetasaṃ tena kalpavyatikarāmbhasā
BhP lokasaṃsthānavijñāna ātmanaḥ parikhidyataḥ
BhP tam āhāgādhayā vācā kaśmalaṃ śamayann iva
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP mā vedagarbha gās tandrīṃ sarga udyamam āvaha
BhP tan mayāpāditaṃ hy agre yan māṃ prārthayate bhavān
BhP bhūyas tvaṃ tapa ātiṣṭha vidyāṃ caiva madāśrayām
BhP tābhyām antarhṛdi brahman lokān drakṣyasy apāvṛtān
BhP tata ātmani loke ca bhaktiyuktaḥ samāhitaḥ
BhP draṣṭāsi māṃ tataṃ brahman mayi lokāṃs tvam ātmanaḥ
BhP yadā tu sarvabhūteṣu dāruṣv agnim iva sthitam
BhP praticakṣīta māṃ loko jahyāt tarhy eva kaśmalam
BhP yadā rahitam ātmānaṃ bhūtendriyaguṇāśayaiḥ
BhP svarūpeṇa mayopetaṃ paśyan svārājyam ṛcchati
BhP nānākarmavitānena prajā bahvīḥ sisṛkṣataḥ
BhP nātmāvasīdaty asmiṃs te varṣīyān madanugrahaḥ
BhP ṛṣim ādyaṃ na badhnāti pāpīyāṃs tvāṃ rajoguṇaḥ
BhP yan mano mayi nirbaddhaṃ prajāḥ saṃsṛjato 'pi te
BhP jñāto 'haṃ bhavatā tv adya durvijñeyo 'pi dehinām
BhP yan māṃ tvaṃ manyase 'yuktaṃ bhūtendriyaguṇātmabhiḥ
BhP tubhyaṃ madvicikitsāyām ātmā me darśito 'bahiḥ
BhP nālena salile mūlaṃ puṣkarasya vicinvataḥ
BhP yac cakarthāṅga matstotraṃ matkathābhyudayāṅkitam
BhP yad vā tapasi te niṣṭhā sa eṣa madanugrahaḥ
BhP prīto 'ham astu bhadraṃ te lokānāṃ vijayecchayā
BhP yad astauṣīr guṇamayaṃ nirguṇaṃ mānuvarṇayan
BhP ya etena pumān nityaṃ stutvā stotreṇa māṃ bhajet
BhP tasyāśu samprasīdeyaṃ sarvakāmavareśvaraḥ
BhP pūrtena tapasā yajñair dānair yogasamādhinā
BhP rāddhaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ puṃsāṃ matprītis tattvavinmatam
BhP aham ātmātmanāṃ dhātaḥ preṣṭhaḥ san preyasām api
BhP ato mayi ratiṃ kuryād dehādir yatkṛte priyaḥ
BhP sarvavedamayenedam ātmanātmātmayoninā
BhP prajāḥ sṛja yathāpūrvaṃ yāś ca mayy anuśerate
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP tasmā evaṃ jagatsraṣṭre pradhānapuruṣeśvaraḥ
BhP vyajyedaṃ svena rūpeṇa kañjanābhas tirodadhe
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP antarhite bhagavati brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
BhP prajāḥ sasarja katidhā daihikīr mānasīr vibhuḥ
BhP ye ca me bhagavan pṛṣṭās tvayy arthā bahuvittama
BhP tān vadasvānupūrvyeṇa chindhi naḥ sarvasaṃśayān
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP evaṃ sañcoditas tena kṣattrā kauṣāravir muniḥ
BhP prītaḥ pratyāha tān praśnān hṛdisthān atha bhārgava
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP viriñco 'pi tathā cakre divyaṃ varṣaśataṃ tapaḥ
BhP ātmany ātmānam āveśya yathāha bhagavān ajaḥ
BhP tad vilokyābjasambhūto vāyunā yadadhiṣṭhitaḥ
BhP padmam ambhaś ca tatkāla kṛtavīryeṇa kampitam
BhP tapasā hy edhamānena vidyayā cātmasaṃsthayā
BhP vivṛddhavijñānabalo nyapād vāyuṃ sahāmbhasā
BhP tad vilokya viyadvyāpi puṣkaraṃ yadadhiṣṭhitam
BhP anena lokān prāglīnān kalpitāsmīty acintayat
BhP padmakośaṃ tadāviśya bhagavatkarmacoditaḥ
BhP ekaṃ vyabhāṅkṣīd urudhā tridhā bhāvyaṃ dvisaptadhā
BhP etāvāñ jīvalokasya saṃsthābhedaḥ samāhṛtaḥ
BhP dharmasya hy animittasya vipākaḥ parameṣṭhy asau
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP yathāttha bahurūpasya harer adbhutakarmaṇaḥ
BhP kālākhyaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ brahman yathā varṇaya naḥ prabho
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP guṇavyatikarākāro nirviśeṣo 'pratiṣṭhitaḥ
BhP puruṣas tadupādānam ātmānaṃ līlayāsṛjat
BhP viśvaṃ vai brahmatanmātraṃ saṃsthitaṃ viṣṇumāyayā
BhP īśvareṇa paricchinnaṃ kālenāvyaktamūrtinā
BhP yathedānīṃ tathāgre ca paścād apy etad īdṛśam
BhP sargo navavidhas tasya prākṛto vaikṛtas tu yaḥ
BhP kāladravyaguṇair asya trividhaḥ pratisaṅkramaḥ
BhP ādyas tu mahataḥ sargo guṇavaiṣamyam ātmanaḥ
BhP dvitīyas tv ahamo yatra dravyajñānakriyodayaḥ
BhP bhūtasargas tṛtīyas tu tanmātro dravyaśaktimān
BhP caturtha aindriyaḥ sargo yas tu jñānakriyātmakaḥ
BhP vaikāriko devasargaḥ pañcamo yanmayaṃ manaḥ
BhP ṣaṣṭhas tu tamasaḥ sargo yas tv abuddhikṛtaḥ prabhoḥ
BhP ṣaḍ ime prākṛtāḥ sargā vaikṛtān api me śṛṇu
BhP rajobhājo bhagavato līleyaṃ harimedhasaḥ
BhP saptamo mukhyasargas tu ṣaḍvidhas tasthuṣāṃ ca yaḥ
BhP vanaspatyoṣadhilatā tvaksārā vīrudho drumāḥ
BhP utsrotasas tamaḥprāyā antaḥsparśā viśeṣiṇaḥ
BhP tiraścām aṣṭamaḥ sargaḥ so 'ṣṭāviṃśadvidho mataḥ
BhP avido bhūritamaso ghrāṇajñā hṛdy avedinaḥ
BhP gaur ajo mahiṣaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sūkaro gavayo ruruḥ
BhP dviśaphāḥ paśavaś ceme avir uṣṭraś ca sattama
BhP kharo 'śvo 'śvataro gauraḥ śarabhaś camarī tathā
BhP ete caikaśaphāḥ kṣattaḥ śṛṇu pañcanakhān paśūn
BhP śvā sṛgālo vṛko vyāghro mārjāraḥ śaśaśallakau
BhP siṃhaḥ kapir gajaḥ kūrmo godhā ca makarādayaḥ
BhP kaṅkagṛdhrabakaśyena bhāsabhallūkabarhiṇaḥ
BhP haṃsasārasacakrāhva kākolūkādayaḥ khagāḥ
BhP arvāksrotas tu navamaḥ kṣattar ekavidho nṛṇām
BhP rajo 'dhikāḥ karmaparā duḥkhe ca sukhamāninaḥ
BhP vaikṛtās traya evaite devasargaś ca sattama
BhP vaikārikas tu yaḥ proktaḥ kaumāras tūbhayātmakaḥ
BhP devasargaś cāṣṭavidho vibudhāḥ pitaro 'surāḥ
BhP gandharvāpsarasaḥ siddhā yakṣarakṣāṃsi cāraṇāḥ
BhP bhūtapretapiśācāś ca vidyādhrāḥ kinnarādayaḥ
BhP daśaite vidurākhyātāḥ sargās te viśvasṛkkṛtāḥ
BhP ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi vaṃśān manvantarāṇi ca
BhP evaṃ rajaḥplutaḥ sraṣṭā kalpādiṣv ātmabhūr hariḥ
BhP sṛjaty amoghasaṅkalpa ātmaivātmānam ātmanā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP caramaḥ sadviśeṣāṇām aneko 'saṃyutaḥ sadā
BhP paramāṇuḥ sa vijñeyo nṛṇām aikyabhramo yataḥ
BhP sata eva padārthasya svarūpāvasthitasya yat
BhP kaivalyaṃ paramamahān aviśeṣo nirantaraḥ
BhP evaṃ kālo 'py anumitaḥ saukṣmye sthaulye ca sattama
BhP saṃsthānabhuktyā bhagavān avyakto vyaktabhug vibhuḥ
BhP sa kālaḥ paramāṇur vai yo bhuṅkte paramāṇutām
BhP sato 'viśeṣabhug yas tu sa kālaḥ paramo mahān
BhP aṇur dvau paramāṇū syāt trasareṇus trayaḥ smṛtaḥ
BhP jālārkaraśmyavagataḥ kham evānupatann agāt
BhP trasareṇutrikaṃ bhuṅkte yaḥ kālaḥ sa truṭiḥ smṛtaḥ
BhP śatabhāgas tu vedhaḥ syāt tais tribhis tu lavaḥ smṛtaḥ
BhP nimeṣas trilavo jñeya āmnātas te trayaḥ kṣaṇaḥ
BhP kṣaṇān pañca viduḥ kāṣṭhāṃ laghu tā daśa pañca ca
BhP laghūni vai samāmnātā daśa pañca ca nāḍikā
BhP te dve muhūrtaḥ praharaḥ ṣaḍ yāmaḥ sapta vā nṛṇām
BhP dvādaśārdhapalonmānaṃ caturbhiś caturaṅgulaiḥ
BhP svarṇamāṣaiḥ kṛtacchidraṃ yāvat prasthajalaplutam
BhP yāmāś catvāraś catvāro martyānām ahanī ubhe
BhP pakṣaḥ pañcadaśāhāni śuklaḥ kṛṣṇaś ca mānada
BhP tayoḥ samuccayo māsaḥ pitṝṇāṃ tad aharniśam
BhP dvau tāv ṛtuḥ ṣaḍ ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ cottaraṃ divi
BhP ayane cāhanī prāhur vatsaro dvādaśa smṛtaḥ
BhP saṃvatsaraśataṃ nṇāṃ paramāyur nirūpitam
BhP graharkṣatārācakrasthaḥ paramāṇvādinā jagat
BhP saṃvatsarāvasānena paryety animiṣo vibhuḥ
BhP saṃvatsaraḥ parivatsara iḍāvatsara eva ca
BhP anuvatsaro vatsaraś ca viduraivaṃ prabhāṣyate
BhP yaḥ sṛjyaśaktim urudhocchvasayan svaśaktyā
BhP puṃso 'bhramāya divi dhāvati bhūtabhedaḥ
BhP kālākhyayā guṇamayaṃ kratubhir vitanvaṃs
BhP tasmai baliṃ harata vatsarapañcakāya
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇām āyuḥ param idaṃ smṛtam
BhP pareṣāṃ gatim ācakṣva ye syuḥ kalpād bahir vidaḥ
BhP bhagavān veda kālasya gatiṃ bhagavato nanu
BhP viśvaṃ vicakṣate dhīrā yogarāddhena cakṣuṣā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliś ceti caturyugam
BhP divyair dvādaśabhir varṣaiḥ sāvadhānaṃ nirūpitam
BhP catvāri trīṇi dve caikaṃ kṛtādiṣu yathākramam
BhP saṅkhyātāni sahasrāṇi dviguṇāni śatāni ca
BhP sandhyāsandhyāṃśayor antar yaḥ kālaḥ śatasaṅkhyayoḥ
BhP tam evāhur yugaṃ tajjñā yatra dharmo vidhīyate
BhP dharmaś catuṣpān manujān kṛte samanuvartate
BhP sa evānyeṣv adharmeṇa vyeti pādena vardhatā
BhP trilokyā yugasāhasraṃ bahir ābrahmaṇo dinam
BhP tāvaty eva niśā tāta yan nimīlati viśvasṛk
BhP niśāvasāna ārabdho lokakalpo 'nuvartate
BhP yāvad dinaṃ bhagavato manūn bhuñjaṃś caturdaśa
BhP svaṃ svaṃ kālaṃ manur bhuṅkte sādhikāṃ hy ekasaptatim
BhP manvantareṣu manavas tadvaṃśyā ṛṣayaḥ surāḥ
BhP bhavanti caiva yugapat sureśāś cānu ye ca tān
BhP eṣa dainandinaḥ sargo brāhmas trailokyavartanaḥ
BhP tiryaṅnṛpitṛdevānāṃ sambhavo yatra karmabhiḥ
BhP manvantareṣu bhagavān bibhrat sattvaṃ svamūrtibhiḥ
BhP manvādibhir idaṃ viśvam avaty uditapauruṣaḥ
BhP tamomātrām upādāya pratisaṃruddhavikramaḥ
BhP kālenānugatāśeṣa āste tūṣṇīṃ dinātyaye
BhP tam evānv api dhīyante lokā bhūrādayas trayaḥ
BhP niśāyām anuvṛttāyāṃ nirmuktaśaśibhāskaram
BhP trilokyāṃ dahyamānāyāṃ śaktyā saṅkarṣaṇāgninā
BhP yānty ūṣmaṇā maharlokāj janaṃ bhṛgvādayo 'rditāḥ
BhP tāvat tribhuvanaṃ sadyaḥ kalpāntaidhitasindhavaḥ
BhP plāvayanty utkaṭāṭopa caṇḍavāteritormayaḥ
BhP antaḥ sa tasmin salila āste 'nantāsano hariḥ
BhP yoganidrānimīlākṣaḥ stūyamāno janālayaiḥ
BhP evaṃvidhair ahorātraiḥ kālagatyopalakṣitaiḥ
BhP apakṣitam ivāsyāpi paramāyur vayaḥśatam
BhP yad ardham āyuṣas tasya parārdham abhidhīyate
BhP pūrvaḥ parārdho 'pakrānto hy aparo 'dya pravartate
BhP pūrvasyādau parārdhasya brāhmo nāma mahān abhūt
BhP kalpo yatrābhavad brahmā śabdabrahmeti yaṃ viduḥ
BhP tasyaiva cānte kalpo 'bhūd yaṃ pādmam abhicakṣate
BhP yad dharer nābhisarasa āsīl lokasaroruham
BhP ayaṃ tu kathitaḥ kalpo dvitīyasyāpi bhārata
BhP vārāha iti vikhyāto yatrāsīc chūkaro hariḥ
BhP kālo 'yaṃ dviparārdhākhyo nimeṣa upacaryate
BhP avyākṛtasyānantasya hy anāder jagadātmanaḥ
BhP kālo 'yaṃ paramāṇvādir dviparārdhānta īśvaraḥ
BhP naiveśituṃ prabhur bhūmna īśvaro dhāmamāninām
BhP vikāraiḥ sahito yuktair viśeṣādibhir āvṛtaḥ
BhP āṇḍakośo bahir ayaṃ pañcāśatkoṭivistṛtaḥ
BhP daśottarādhikair yatra praviṣṭaḥ paramāṇuvat
BhP lakṣyate 'ntargatāś cānye koṭiśo hy aṇḍarāśayaḥ
BhP tad āhur akṣaraṃ brahma sarvakāraṇakāraṇam
BhP viṣṇor dhāma paraṃ sākṣāt puruṣasya mahātmanaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti te varṇitaḥ kṣattaḥ kālākhyaḥ paramātmanaḥ
BhP mahimā vedagarbho 'tha yathāsrākṣīn nibodha me
BhP sasarjāgre 'ndhatāmisram atha tāmisram ādikṛt
BhP mahāmohaṃ ca mohaṃ ca tamaś cājñānavṛttayaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā pāpīyasīṃ sṛṣṭiṃ nātmānaṃ bahv amanyata
BhP bhagavaddhyānapūtena manasānyāṃ tato 'sṛjat
BhP sanakaṃ ca sanandaṃ ca sanātanam athātmabhūḥ
BhP sanatkumāraṃ ca munīn niṣkriyān ūrdhvaretasaḥ
BhP tān babhāṣe svabhūḥ putrān prajāḥ sṛjata putrakāḥ
BhP tan naicchan mokṣadharmāṇo vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ
BhP so 'vadhyātaḥ sutair evaṃ pratyākhyātānuśāsanaiḥ
BhP krodhaṃ durviṣahaṃ jātaṃ niyantum upacakrame
BhP dhiyā nigṛhyamāṇo 'pi bhruvor madhyāt prajāpateḥ
BhP sadyo 'jāyata tanmanyuḥ kumāro nīlalohitaḥ
BhP sa vai ruroda devānāṃ pūrvajo bhagavān bhavaḥ
BhP nāmāni kuru me dhātaḥ sthānāni ca jagadguro
BhP iti tasya vacaḥ pādmo bhagavān paripālayan
BhP abhyadhād bhadrayā vācā mā rodīs tat karomi te
BhP yad arodīḥ suraśreṣṭha sodvega iva bālakaḥ
BhP tatas tvām abhidhāsyanti nāmnā rudra iti prajāḥ
BhP hṛd indriyāṇy asur vyoma vāyur agnir jalaṃ mahī
BhP sūryaś candras tapaś caiva sthānāny agre kṛtāni te
BhP manyur manur mahinaso mahāñ chiva ṛtadhvajaḥ
BhP ugraretā bhavaḥ kālo vāmadevo dhṛtavrataḥ
BhP dhīr dhṛtirasalomā ca niyut sarpir ilāmbikā
BhP irāvatī svadhā dīkṣā rudrāṇyo rudra te striyaḥ
BhP gṛhāṇaitāni nāmāni sthānāni ca sayoṣaṇaḥ
BhP ebhiḥ sṛja prajā bahvīḥ prajānām asi yat patiḥ
BhP ity ādiṣṭaḥ svaguruṇā bhagavān nīlalohitaḥ
BhP sattvākṛtisvabhāvena sasarjātmasamāḥ prajāḥ
BhP rudrāṇāṃ rudrasṛṣṭānāṃ samantād grasatāṃ jagat
BhP niśāmyāsaṅkhyaśo yūthān prajāpatir aśaṅkata
BhP alaṃ prajābhiḥ sṛṣṭābhir īdṛśībhiḥ surottama
BhP mayā saha dahantībhir diśaś cakṣurbhir ulbaṇaiḥ
BhP tapa ātiṣṭha bhadraṃ te sarvabhūtasukhāvaham
BhP tapasaiva yathā pūrvaṃ sraṣṭā viśvam idaṃ bhavān
BhP tapasaiva paraṃ jyotir bhagavantam adhokṣajam
BhP sarvabhūtaguhāvāsam añjasā vindate pumān
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evam ātmabhuvādiṣṭaḥ parikramya girāṃ patim
BhP bāḍham ity amum āmantrya viveśa tapase vanam
BhP athābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ daśa putrāḥ prajajñire
BhP bhagavacchaktiyuktasya lokasantānahetavaḥ
BhP marīcir atryaṅgirasau pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
BhP bhṛgur vasiṣṭho dakṣaś ca daśamas tatra nāradaḥ
BhP utsaṅgān nārado jajñe dakṣo 'ṅguṣṭhāt svayambhuvaḥ
BhP prāṇād vasiṣṭhaḥ sañjāto bhṛgus tvaci karāt kratuḥ
BhP pulaho nābhito jajñe pulastyaḥ karṇayor ṛṣiḥ
BhP aṅgirā mukhato 'kṣṇo 'trir marīcir manaso 'bhavat
BhP dharmaḥ stanād dakṣiṇato yatra nārāyaṇaḥ svayam
BhP adharmaḥ pṛṣṭhato yasmān mṛtyur lokabhayaṅkaraḥ
BhP hṛdi kāmo bhruvaḥ krodho lobhaś cādharadacchadāt
BhP āsyād vāk sindhavo meḍhrān nirṛtiḥ pāyor aghāśrayaḥ
BhP chāyāyāḥ kardamo jajñe devahūtyāḥ patiḥ prabhuḥ
BhP manaso dehataś cedaṃ jajñe viśvakṛto jagat
BhP vācaṃ duhitaraṃ tanvīṃ svayambhūr haratīṃ manaḥ
BhP akāmāṃ cakame kṣattaḥ sakāma iti naḥ śrutam
BhP tam adharme kṛtamatiṃ vilokya pitaraṃ sutāḥ
BhP marīcimukhyā munayo viśrambhāt pratyabodhayan
BhP naitat pūrvaiḥ kṛtaṃ tvad ye na kariṣyanti cāpare
BhP yas tvaṃ duhitaraṃ gaccher anigṛhyāṅgajaṃ prabhuḥ
BhP tejīyasām api hy etan na suślokyaṃ jagadguro
BhP yadvṛttam anutiṣṭhan vai lokaḥ kṣemāya kalpate
BhP tasmai namo bhagavate ya idaṃ svena rociṣā
BhP ātmasthaṃ vyañjayām āsa sa dharmaṃ pātum arhati
BhP sa itthaṃ gṛṇataḥ putrān puro dṛṣṭvā prajāpatīn
BhP prajāpatipatis tanvaṃ tatyāja vrīḍitas tadā
BhP tāṃ diśo jagṛhur ghorāṃ nīhāraṃ yad vidus tamaḥ
BhP kadācid dhyāyataḥ sraṣṭur vedā āsaṃś caturmukhāt
BhP kathaṃ srakṣyāmy ahaṃ lokān samavetān yathā purā
BhP cāturhotraṃ karmatantram upavedanayaiḥ saha
BhP dharmasya pādāś catvāras tathaivāśramavṛttayaḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP sa vai viśvasṛjām īśo vedādīn mukhato 'sṛjat
BhP yad yad yenāsṛjad devas tan me brūhi tapodhana
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvākhyān vedān pūrvādibhir mukhaiḥ
BhP śāstram ijyāṃ stutistomaṃ prāyaścittaṃ vyadhāt kramāt
BhP āyurvedaṃ dhanurvedaṃ gāndharvaṃ vedam ātmanaḥ
BhP sthāpatyaṃ cāsṛjad vedaṃ kramāt pūrvādibhir mukhaiḥ
BhP itihāsapurāṇāni pañcamaṃ vedam īśvaraḥ
BhP sarvebhya eva vaktrebhyaḥ sasṛje sarvadarśanaḥ
BhP ṣoḍaśyukthau pūrvavaktrāt purīṣyagniṣṭutāv atha
BhP āptoryāmātirātrau ca vājapeyaṃ sagosavam
BhP vidyā dānaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ dharmasyeti padāni ca
BhP āśramāṃś ca yathāsaṅkhyam asṛjat saha vṛttibhiḥ
BhP sāvitraṃ prājāpatyaṃ ca brāhmaṃ cātha bṛhat tathā
BhP vārtā sañcayaśālīna śiloñcha iti vai gṛhe
BhP vaikhānasā vālakhilyau dumbarāḥ phenapā vane
BhP nyāse kuṭīcakaḥ pūrvaṃ bahvodo haṃsaniṣkriyau
BhP ānvīkṣikī trayī vārtā daṇḍanītis tathaiva ca
BhP evaṃ vyāhṛtayaś cāsan praṇavo hy asya dahrataḥ
BhP tasyoṣṇig āsīl lomabhyo gāyatrī ca tvaco vibhoḥ
BhP triṣṭum māṃsāt snuto 'nuṣṭub jagaty asthnaḥ prajāpateḥ
BhP majjāyāḥ paṅktir utpannā bṛhatī prāṇato 'bhavat
BhP sparśas tasyābhavaj jīvaḥ svaro deha udāhṛta
BhP ūṣmāṇam indriyāṇy āhur antaḥsthā balam ātmanaḥ
BhP svarāḥ sapta vihāreṇa bhavanti sma prajāpateḥ
BhP śabdabrahmātmanas tasya vyaktāvyaktātmanaḥ paraḥ
BhP brahmāvabhāti vitato nānāśaktyupabṛṃhitaḥ
BhP tato 'parām upādāya sa sargāya mano dadhe
BhP ṛṣīṇāṃ bhūrivīryāṇām api sargam avistṛtam
BhP jñātvā tad dhṛdaye bhūyaś cintayām āsa kaurava
BhP aho adbhutam etan me vyāpṛtasyāpi nityadā
BhP na hy edhante prajā nūnaṃ daivam atra vighātakam
BhP evaṃ yuktakṛtas tasya daivaṃ cāvekṣatas tadā
BhP kasya rūpam abhūd dvedhā yat kāyam abhicakṣate
BhP tābhyāṃ rūpavibhāgābhyāṃ mithunaṃ samapadyata
BhP yas tu tatra pumān so 'bhūn manuḥ svāyambhuvaḥ svarāṭ
BhP strī yāsīc chatarūpākhyā mahiṣy asya mahātmanaḥ
BhP tadā mithunadharmeṇa prajā hy edhām babhūvire
BhP sa cāpi śatarūpāyāṃ pañcāpatyāny ajījanat
BhP priyavratottānapādau tisraḥ kanyāś ca bhārata
BhP ākūtir devahūtiś ca prasūtir iti sattama
BhP ākūtiṃ rucaye prādāt kardamāya tu madhyamām
BhP dakṣāyādāt prasūtiṃ ca yata āpūritaṃ jagat
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP niśamya vācaṃ vadato muneḥ puṇyatamāṃ nṛpa
BhP bhūyaḥ papraccha kauravyo vāsudevakathādṛtaḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP sa vai svāyambhuvaḥ samrāṭ priyaḥ putraḥ svayambhuvaḥ
BhP pratilabhya priyāṃ patnīṃ kiṃ cakāra tato mune
BhP caritaṃ tasya rājarṣer ādirājasya sattama
BhP brūhi me śraddadhānāya viṣvaksenāśrayo hy asau
BhP śrutasya puṃsāṃ suciraśramasya nanv añjasā sūribhir īḍito 'rthaḥ
BhP tattadguṇānuśravaṇaṃ mukunda pādāravindaṃ hṛdayeṣu yeṣām
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP iti bruvāṇaṃ viduraṃ vinītaṃ sahasraśīrṣṇaś caraṇopadhānam
BhP prahṛṣṭaromā bhagavatkathāyāṃ praṇīyamāno munir abhyacaṣṭa
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP yadā svabhāryayā sārdhaṃ jātaḥ svāyambhuvo manuḥ
BhP prāñjaliḥ praṇataś cedaṃ vedagarbham abhāṣata
BhP tvam ekaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ janmakṛd vṛttidaḥ pitā
BhP tathāpi naḥ prajānāṃ te śuśrūṣā kena vā bhavet
BhP tad vidhehi namas tubhyaṃ karmasv īḍyātmaśaktiṣu
BhP yat kṛtveha yaśo viṣvag amutra ca bhaved gatiḥ
BhP brahmovāca
BhP prītas tubhyam ahaṃ tāta svasti stād vāṃ kṣitīśvara
BhP yan nirvyalīkena hṛdā śādhi mety ātmanārpitam
BhP etāvaty ātmajair vīra kāryā hy apacitir gurau
BhP śaktyāpramattair gṛhyeta sādaraṃ gatamatsaraiḥ
BhP sa tvam asyām apatyāni sadṛśāny ātmano guṇaiḥ
BhP utpādya śāsa dharmeṇa gāṃ yajñaiḥ puruṣaṃ yaja
BhP paraṃ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ mahyaṃ syāt prajārakṣayā nṛpa
BhP bhagavāṃs te prajābhartur hṛṣīkeśo 'nutuṣyati
BhP yeṣāṃ na tuṣṭo bhagavān yajñaliṅgo janārdanaḥ
BhP teṣāṃ śramo hy apārthāya yad ātmā nādṛtaḥ svayam
BhP manur uvāca
BhP ādeśe 'haṃ bhagavato varteyāmīvasūdana
BhP sthānaṃ tv ihānujānīhi prajānāṃ mama ca prabho
BhP yad okaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ mahī magnā mahāmbhasi
BhP asyā uddharaṇe yatno deva devyā vidhīyatām
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP parameṣṭhī tv apāṃ madhye tathā sannām avekṣya gām
BhP katham enāṃ samunneṣya iti dadhyau dhiyā ciram
BhP sṛjato me kṣitir vārbhiḥ plāvyamānā rasāṃ gatā
BhP athātra kim anuṣṭheyam asmābhiḥ sargayojitaiḥ
BhP yasyāhaṃ hṛdayād āsaṃ sa īśo vidadhātu me
BhP ity abhidhyāyato nāsā vivarāt sahasānagha
BhP varāhatoko niragād aṅguṣṭhaparimāṇakaḥ
BhP tasyābhipaśyataḥ khasthaḥ kṣaṇena kila bhārata
BhP gajamātraḥ pravavṛdhe tad adbhutam abhūn mahat
BhP marīcipramukhair vipraiḥ kumārair manunā saha
BhP dṛṣṭvā tat saukaraṃ rūpaṃ tarkayām āsa citradhā
BhP kim etat sūkaravyājaṃ sattvaṃ divyam avasthitam
BhP aho batāścaryam idaṃ nāsāyā me viniḥsṛtam
BhP dṛṣṭo 'ṅguṣṭhaśiromātraḥ kṣaṇād gaṇḍaśilāsamaḥ
BhP api svid bhagavān eṣa yajño me khedayan manaḥ
BhP iti mīmāṃsatas tasya brahmaṇaḥ saha sūnubhiḥ
BhP bhagavān yajñapuruṣo jagarjāgendrasannibhaḥ
BhP brahmāṇaṃ harṣayām āsa haris tāṃś ca dvijottamān
BhP svagarjitena kakubhaḥ pratisvanayatā vibhuḥ
BhP niśamya te ghargharitaṃ svakheda kṣayiṣṇu māyāmayasūkarasya
BhP janastapaḥsatyanivāsinas te tribhiḥ pavitrair munayo 'gṛṇan sma
BhP teṣāṃ satāṃ vedavitānamūrtir brahmāvadhāryātmaguṇānuvādam
BhP vinadya bhūyo vibudhodayāya gajendralīlo jalam āviveśa
BhP utkṣiptavālaḥ khacaraḥ kaṭhoraḥ saṭā vidhunvan khararomaśatvak
BhP khurāhatābhraḥ sitadaṃṣṭra īkṣā jyotir babhāse bhagavān mahīdhraḥ
BhP ghrāṇena pṛthvyāḥ padavīṃ vijighran kroḍāpadeśaḥ svayam adhvarāṅgaḥ
BhP karāladaṃṣṭro 'py akarāladṛgbhyām udvīkṣya viprān gṛṇato 'viśat kam
BhP sa vajrakūṭāṅganipātavega viśīrṇakukṣiḥ stanayann udanvān
BhP utsṛṣṭadīrghormibhujair ivārtaś cukrośa yajñeśvara pāhi meti
BhP khuraiḥ kṣuraprair darayaṃs tad āpa utpārapāraṃ triparū rasāyām
BhP dadarśa gāṃ tatra suṣupsur agre yāṃ jīvadhānīṃ svayam abhyadhatta
BhP pātālamūleśvarabhogasaṃhatau vinyasya pādau pṛthivīṃ ca bibhrataḥ
BhP yasyopamāno na babhūva so 'cyuto mamāstu māṅgalyavivṛddhaye hariḥ
BhP svadaṃṣṭrayoddhṛtya mahīṃ nimagnāṃ sa utthitaḥ saṃruruce rasāyāḥ
BhP tatrāpi daityaṃ gadayāpatantaṃ sunābhasandīpitatīvramanyuḥ
BhP jaghāna rundhānam asahyavikramaṃ sa līlayebhaṃ mṛgarāḍ ivāmbhasi
BhP tadraktapaṅkāṅkitagaṇḍatuṇḍo yathā gajendro jagatīṃ vibhindan
BhP tamālanīlaṃ sitadantakoṭyā kṣmām utkṣipantaṃ gajalīlayāṅga
BhP prajñāya baddhāñjalayo 'nuvākair viriñcimukhyā upatasthur īśam
BhP ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
BhP jitaṃ jitaṃ te 'jita yajñabhāvana trayīṃ tanuṃ svāṃ paridhunvate namaḥ
BhP yadromagarteṣu nililyur addhayas tasmai namaḥ kāraṇasūkarāya te
BhP rūpaṃ tavaitan nanu duṣkṛtātmanāṃ durdarśanaṃ deva yad adhvarātmakam
BhP chandāṃsi yasya tvaci barhiromasv ājyaṃ dṛśi tv aṅghriṣu cāturhotram
BhP srak tuṇḍa āsīt sruva īśa nāsayor iḍodare camasāḥ karṇarandhre
BhP prāśitram āsye grasane grahās tu te yac carvaṇaṃ te bhagavann agnihotram
BhP dīkṣānujanmopasadaḥ śirodharaṃ tvaṃ prāyaṇīyodayanīyadaṃṣṭraḥ
BhP jihvā pravargyas tava śīrṣakaṃ kratoḥ satyāvasathyaṃ citayo 'savo hi te
BhP somas tu retaḥ savanāny avasthitiḥ saṃsthāvibhedās tava deva dhātavaḥ
BhP satrāṇi sarvāṇi śarīrasandhis tvaṃ sarvayajñakratur iṣṭibandhanaḥ
BhP namo namas te 'khilamantradevatā dravyāya sarvakratave kriyātmane
BhP vairāgyabhaktyātmajayānubhāvita jñānāya vidyāgurave namo namaḥ
BhP daṃṣṭrāgrakoṭyā bhagavaṃs tvayā dhṛtā virājate bhūdhara bhūḥ sabhūdharā
BhP yathā vanān niḥsarato datā dhṛtā mataṅgajendrasya sapatrapadminī
BhP trayīmayaṃ rūpam idaṃ ca saukaraṃ bhūmaṇḍalenātha datā dhṛtena te
BhP cakāsti śṛṅgoḍhaghanena bhūyasā kulācalendrasya yathaiva vibhramaḥ
BhP saṃsthāpayaināṃ jagatāṃ satasthuṣāṃ lokāya patnīm asi mātaraṃ pitā
BhP vidhema cāsyai namasā saha tvayā yasyāṃ svatejo 'gnim ivāraṇāv adhāḥ
BhP kaḥ śraddadhītānyatamas tava prabho rasāṃ gatāyā bhuva udvibarhaṇam
BhP na vismayo 'sau tvayi viśvavismaye yo māyayedaṃ sasṛje 'tivismayam
BhP vidhunvatā vedamayaṃ nijaṃ vapur janastapaḥsatyanivāsino vayam
BhP saṭāśikhoddhūtaśivāmbubindubhir vimṛjyamānā bhṛśam īśa pāvitāḥ
BhP sa vai bata bhraṣṭamatis tavaiṣate yaḥ karmaṇāṃ pāram apārakarmaṇaḥ
BhP yadyogamāyāguṇayogamohitaṃ viśvaṃ samastaṃ bhagavan vidhehi śam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ity upasthīyamāno 'sau munibhir brahmavādibhiḥ
BhP salile svakhurākrānta upādhattāvitāvanim
BhP sa itthaṃ bhagavān urvīṃ viṣvaksenaḥ prajāpatiḥ
BhP rasāyā līlayonnītām apsu nyasya yayau hariḥ
BhP ya evam etāṃ harimedhaso hareḥ kathāṃ subhadrāṃ kathanīyamāyinaḥ
BhP śṛṇvīta bhaktyā śravayeta vośatīṃ janārdano 'syāśu hṛdi prasīdati
BhP tasmin prasanne sakalāśiṣāṃ prabhau kiṃ durlabhaṃ tābhir alaṃ lavātmabhiḥ
BhP ananyadṛṣṭyā bhajatāṃ guhāśayaḥ svayaṃ vidhatte svagatiṃ paraḥ parām
BhP ko nāma loke puruṣārthasāravit purākathānāṃ bhagavatkathāsudhām
BhP āpīya karṇāñjalibhir bhavāpahām aho virajyeta vinā naretaram
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP niśamya kauṣāraviṇopavarṇitāṃ hareḥ kathāṃ kāraṇasūkarātmanaḥ
BhP punaḥ sa papraccha tam udyatāñjalir na cātitṛpto viduro dhṛtavrataḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP tenaiva tu muniśreṣṭha hariṇā yajñamūrtinā
BhP ādidaityo hiraṇyākṣo hata ity anuśuśruma
BhP tasya coddharataḥ kṣauṇīṃ svadaṃṣṭrāgreṇa līlayā
BhP daityarājasya ca brahman kasmād dhetor abhūn mṛdhaḥ
BhP śraddadhānāya bhaktāya brūhi tajjanmavistaram
BhP ṛṣe na tṛpyati manaḥ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sādhu vīra tvayā pṛṣṭam avatārakathāṃ hareḥ
BhP yat tvaṃ pṛcchasi martyānāṃ mṛtyupāśaviśātanīm
BhP yayottānapadaḥ putro muninā gītayārbhakaḥ
BhP mṛtyoḥ kṛtvaiva mūrdhny aṅghrim āruroha hareḥ padam
BhP athātrāpītihāso 'yaṃ śruto me varṇitaḥ purā
BhP brahmaṇā devadevena devānām anupṛcchatām
BhP ditir dākṣāyaṇī kṣattar mārīcaṃ kaśyapaṃ patim
BhP apatyakāmā cakame sandhyāyāṃ hṛcchayārditā
BhP iṣṭvāgnijihvaṃ payasā puruṣaṃ yajuṣāṃ patim
BhP nimlocaty arka āsīnam agnyagāre samāhitam
BhP ditir uvāca
BhP eṣa māṃ tvatkṛte vidvan kāma āttaśarāsanaḥ
BhP dunoti dīnāṃ vikramya rambhām iva mataṅgajaḥ
BhP tad bhavān dahyamānāyāṃ sapatnīnāṃ samṛddhibhiḥ
BhP prajāvatīnāṃ bhadraṃ te mayy āyuṅktām anugraham
BhP bhartary āptorumānānāṃ lokān āviśate yaśaḥ
BhP patir bhavadvidho yāsāṃ prajayā nanu jāyate
BhP purā pitā no bhagavān dakṣo duhitṛvatsalaḥ
BhP kaṃ vṛṇīta varaṃ vatsā ity apṛcchata naḥ pṛthak
BhP sa viditvātmajānāṃ no bhāvaṃ santānabhāvanaḥ
BhP trayodaśādadāt tāsāṃ yās te śīlam anuvratāḥ
BhP atha me kuru kalyāṇaṃ kāmaṃ kamalalocana
BhP ārtopasarpaṇaṃ bhūmann amoghaṃ hi mahīyasi
BhP iti tāṃ vīra mārīcaḥ kṛpaṇāṃ bahubhāṣiṇīm
BhP pratyāhānunayan vācā pravṛddhānaṅgakaśmalām
BhP eṣa te 'haṃ vidhāsyāmi priyaṃ bhīru yad icchasi
BhP tasyāḥ kāmaṃ na kaḥ kuryāt siddhis traivargikī yataḥ
BhP sarvāśramān upādāya svāśrameṇa kalatravān
BhP vyasanārṇavam atyeti jalayānair yathārṇavam
BhP yām āhur ātmano hy ardhaṃ śreyaskāmasya mānini
BhP yasyāṃ svadhuram adhyasya pumāṃś carati vijvaraḥ
BhP yām āśrityendriyārātīn durjayān itarāśramaiḥ
BhP vayaṃ jayema helābhir dasyūn durgapatir yathā
BhP na vayaṃ prabhavas tāṃ tvām anukartuṃ gṛheśvari
BhP apy āyuṣā vā kārtsnyena ye cānye guṇagṛdhnavaḥ
BhP athāpi kāmam etaṃ te prajātyai karavāṇy alam
BhP yathā māṃ nātirocanti muhūrtaṃ pratipālaya
BhP eṣā ghoratamā velā ghorāṇāṃ ghoradarśanā
BhP caranti yasyāṃ bhūtāni bhūteśānucarāṇi ha
BhP etasyāṃ sādhvi sandhyāyāṃ bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ
BhP parīto bhūtaparṣadbhir vṛṣeṇāṭati bhūtarāṭ
BhP śmaśānacakrāniladhūlidhūmra vikīrṇavidyotajaṭākalāpaḥ
BhP bhasmāvaguṇṭhāmalarukmadeho devas tribhiḥ paśyati devaras te
BhP na yasya loke svajanaḥ paro vā nātyādṛto nota kaścid vigarhyaḥ
BhP vayaṃ vratair yaccaraṇāpaviddhām āśāsmahe 'jāṃ bata bhuktabhogām
BhP yasyānavadyācaritaṃ manīṣiṇo gṛṇanty avidyāpaṭalaṃ bibhitsavaḥ
BhP nirastasāmyātiśayo 'pi yat svayaṃ piśācacaryām acarad gatiḥ satām
BhP hasanti yasyācaritaṃ hi durbhagāḥ svātmanratasyāviduṣaḥ samīhitam
BhP yair vastramālyābharaṇānulepanaiḥ śvabhojanaṃ svātmatayopalālitam
BhP brahmādayo yatkṛtasetupālā yatkāraṇaṃ viśvam idaṃ ca māyā
BhP ājñākarī yasya piśācacaryā aho vibhūmnaś caritaṃ viḍambanam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP saivaṃ saṃvidite bhartrā manmathonmathitendriyā
BhP jagrāha vāso brahmarṣer vṛṣalīva gatatrapā
BhP sa viditvātha bhāryāyās taṃ nirbandhaṃ vikarmaṇi
BhP natvā diṣṭāya rahasi tayāthopaviveśa hi
BhP athopaspṛśya salilaṃ prāṇān āyamya vāgyataḥ
BhP dhyāyañ jajāpa virajaṃ brahma jyotiḥ sanātanam
BhP ditis tu vrīḍitā tena karmāvadyena bhārata
BhP upasaṅgamya viprarṣim adhomukhy abhyabhāṣata
BhP ditir uvāca
BhP na me garbham imaṃ brahman bhūtānām ṛṣabho 'vadhīt
BhP rudraḥ patir hi bhūtānāṃ yasyākaravam aṃhasam
BhP namo rudrāya mahate devāyogrāya mīḍhuṣe
BhP śivāya nyastadaṇḍāya dhṛtadaṇḍāya manyave
BhP sa naḥ prasīdatāṃ bhāmo bhagavān urvanugrahaḥ
BhP vyādhasyāpy anukampyānāṃ strīṇāṃ devaḥ satīpatiḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP svasargasyāśiṣaṃ lokyām āśāsānāṃ pravepatīm
BhP nivṛttasandhyāniyamo bhāryām āha prajāpatiḥ
BhP kaśyapa uvāca
BhP aprāyatyād ātmanas te doṣān mauhūrtikād uta
BhP mannideśāticāreṇa devānāṃ cātihelanāt
BhP bhaviṣyatas tavābhadrāv abhadre jāṭharādhamau
BhP lokān sapālāṃs trīṃś caṇḍi muhur ākrandayiṣyataḥ
BhP prāṇināṃ hanyamānānāṃ dīnānām akṛtāgasām
BhP strīṇāṃ nigṛhyamāṇānāṃ kopiteṣu mahātmasu
BhP tadā viśveśvaraḥ kruddho bhagavāl lokabhāvanaḥ
BhP haniṣyaty avatīryāsau yathādrīn śataparvadhṛk
BhP ditir uvāca
BhP vadhaṃ bhagavatā sākṣāt sunābhodārabāhunā
BhP āśāse putrayor mahyaṃ mā kruddhād brāhmaṇād prabho
BhP na brahmadaṇḍadagdhasya na bhūtabhayadasya ca
BhP nārakāś cānugṛhṇanti yāṃ yāṃ yonim asau gataḥ
BhP kaśyapa uvāca
BhP kṛtaśokānutāpena sadyaḥ pratyavamarśanāt
BhP bhagavaty urumānāc ca bhave mayy api cādarāt
BhP putrasyaiva ca putrāṇāṃ bhavitaikaḥ satāṃ mataḥ
BhP gāsyanti yadyaśaḥ śuddhaṃ bhagavadyaśasā samam
BhP yogair hemeva durvarṇaṃ bhāvayiṣyanti sādhavaḥ
BhP nirvairādibhir ātmānaṃ yacchīlam anuvartitum
BhP yatprasādād idaṃ viśvaṃ prasīdati yadātmakam
BhP sa svadṛg bhagavān yasya toṣyate 'nanyayā dṛśā
BhP sa vai mahābhāgavato mahātmā mahānubhāvo mahatāṃ mahiṣṭhaḥ
BhP pravṛddhabhaktyā hy anubhāvitāśaye niveśya vaikuṇṭham imaṃ vihāsyati
BhP alampaṭaḥ śīladharo guṇākaro hṛṣṭaḥ pararddhyā vyathito duḥkhiteṣu
BhP abhūtaśatrur jagataḥ śokahartā naidāghikaṃ tāpam ivoḍurājaḥ
BhP antar bahiś cāmalam abjanetraṃ svapūruṣecchānugṛhītarūpam
BhP pautras tava śrīlalanālalāmaṃ draṣṭā sphuratkuṇḍalamaṇḍitānanam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP śrutvā bhāgavataṃ pautram amodata ditir bhṛśam
BhP putrayoś ca vadhaṃ kṛṣṇād viditvāsīn mahāmanāḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP prājāpatyaṃ tu tat tejaḥ paratejohanaṃ ditiḥ
BhP dadhāra varṣāṇi śataṃ śaṅkamānā surārdanāt
BhP loke tenāhatāloke lokapālā hataujasaḥ
BhP nyavedayan viśvasṛje dhvāntavyatikaraṃ diśām
BhP devā ūcuḥ
BhP tama etad vibho vettha saṃvignā yad vayaṃ bhṛśam
BhP na hy avyaktaṃ bhagavataḥ kālenāspṛṣṭavartmanaḥ
BhP devadeva jagaddhātar lokanāthaśikhāmaṇe
BhP pareṣām apareṣāṃ tvaṃ bhūtānām asi bhāvavit
BhP namo vijñānavīryāya māyayedam upeyuṣe
BhP gṛhītaguṇabhedāya namas te 'vyaktayonaye
BhP ye tvānanyena bhāvena bhāvayanty ātmabhāvanam
BhP ātmani protabhuvanaṃ paraṃ sadasadātmakam
BhP teṣāṃ supakvayogānāṃ jitaśvāsendriyātmanām
BhP labdhayuṣmatprasādānāṃ na kutaścit parābhavaḥ
BhP yasya vācā prajāḥ sarvā gāvas tantyeva yantritāḥ
BhP haranti balim āyattās tasmai mukhyāya te namaḥ
BhP sa tvaṃ vidhatsva śaṃ bhūmaṃs tamasā luptakarmaṇām
BhP adabhradayayā dṛṣṭyā āpannān arhasīkṣitum
BhP eṣa deva diter garbha ojaḥ kāśyapam arpitam
BhP diśas timirayan sarvā vardhate 'gnir ivaidhasi
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sa prahasya mahābāho bhagavān śabdagocaraḥ
BhP pratyācaṣṭātmabhūr devān prīṇan rucirayā girā
BhP brahmovāca
BhP mānasā me sutā yuṣmat pūrvajāḥ sanakādayaḥ
BhP cerur vihāyasā lokāl lokeṣu vigataspṛhāḥ
BhP ta ekadā bhagavato vaikuṇṭhasyāmalātmanaḥ
BhP yayur vaikuṇṭhanilayaṃ sarvalokanamaskṛtam
BhP vasanti yatra puruṣāḥ sarve vaikuṇṭhamūrtayaḥ
BhP ye 'nimittanimittena dharmeṇārādhayan harim
BhP yatra cādyaḥ pumān āste bhagavān śabdagocaraḥ
BhP sattvaṃ viṣṭabhya virajaṃ svānāṃ no mṛḍayan vṛṣaḥ
BhP yatra naiḥśreyasaṃ nāma vanaṃ kāmadughair drumaiḥ
BhP sarvartuśrībhir vibhrājat kaivalyam iva mūrtimat
BhP vaimānikāḥ salalanāś caritāni śaśvad
BhP gāyanti yatra śamalakṣapaṇāni bhartuḥ
BhP antarjale 'nuvikasanmadhumādhavīnāṃ
BhP gandhena khaṇḍitadhiyo 'py anilaṃ kṣipantaḥ
BhP pārāvatānyabhṛtasārasacakravāka
BhP dātyūhahaṃsaśukatittiribarhiṇāṃ yaḥ
BhP kolāhalo viramate 'ciramātram uccair
BhP bhṛṅgādhipe harikathām iva gāyamāne
BhP mandārakundakurabotpalacampakārṇa
BhP punnāganāgabakulāmbujapārijātāḥ
BhP gandhe 'rcite tulasikābharaṇena tasyā
BhP yasmiṃs tapaḥ sumanaso bahu mānayanti
BhP yat saṅkulaṃ haripadānatimātradṛṣṭair
BhP vaidūryamārakatahemamayair vimānaiḥ
BhP yeṣāṃ bṛhatkaṭitaṭāḥ smitaśobhimukhyaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇātmanāṃ na raja ādadhur utsmayādyaiḥ
BhP śrī rūpiṇī kvaṇayatī caraṇāravindaṃ
BhP līlāmbujena harisadmani muktadoṣā
BhP saṃlakṣyate sphaṭikakuḍya upetahemni
BhP sammārjatīva yadanugrahaṇe 'nyayatnaḥ
BhP vāpīṣu vidrumataṭāsv amalāmṛtāpsu
BhP preṣyānvitā nijavane tulasībhir īśam
BhP abhyarcatī svalakam unnasam īkṣya vaktram
BhP uccheṣitaṃ bhagavatety amatāṅga yacchrīḥ
BhP yan na vrajanty aghabhido racanānuvādāc
BhP chṛṇvanti ye 'nyaviṣayāḥ kukathā matighnīḥ
BhP yās tu śrutā hatabhagair nṛbhir āttasārās
BhP tāṃs tān kṣipanty aśaraṇeṣu tamaḥsu hanta
BhP ye 'bhyarthitām api ca no nṛgatiṃ prapannā
BhP jñānaṃ ca tattvaviṣayaṃ sahadharmaṃ yatra
BhP nārādhanaṃ bhagavato vitaranty amuṣya
BhP sammohitā vitatayā bata māyayā te
BhP yac ca vrajanty animiṣām ṛṣabhānuvṛttyā
BhP dūre yamā hy upari naḥ spṛhaṇīyaśīlāḥ
BhP bhartur mithaḥ suyaśasaḥ kathanānurāga
BhP vaiklavyabāṣpakalayā pulakīkṛtāṅgāḥ
BhP tad viśvagurvadhikṛtaṃ bhuvanaikavandyaṃ
BhP divyaṃ vicitravibudhāgryavimānaśociḥ
BhP āpuḥ parāṃ mudam apūrvam upetya yoga
BhP māyābalena munayas tad atho vikuṇṭham
BhP tasminn atītya munayaḥ ṣaḍ asajjamānāḥ
BhP kakṣāḥ samānavayasāv atha saptamāyām
BhP devāv acakṣata gṛhītagadau parārdhya
BhP keyūrakuṇḍalakirīṭaviṭaṅkaveṣau
BhP mattadvirephavanamālikayā nivītau
BhP vinyastayāsitacatuṣṭayabāhumadhye
BhP vaktraṃ bhruvā kuṭilayā sphuṭanirgamābhyāṃ
BhP raktekṣaṇena ca manāg rabhasaṃ dadhānau
BhP dvāry etayor niviviśur miṣator apṛṣṭvā
BhP pūrvā yathā puraṭavajrakapāṭikā yāḥ
BhP sarvatra te 'viṣamayā munayaḥ svadṛṣṭyā
BhP ye sañcaranty avihatā vigatābhiśaṅkāḥ
BhP tān vīkṣya vātaraśanāṃś caturaḥ kumārān
BhP vṛddhān daśārdhavayaso viditātmatattvān
BhP vetreṇa cāskhalayatām atadarhaṇāṃs tau
BhP tejo vihasya bhagavatpratikūlaśīlau
BhP tābhyāṃ miṣatsv animiṣeṣu niṣidhyamānāḥ
BhP svarhattamā hy api hareḥ pratihārapābhyām
BhP ūcuḥ suhṛttamadidṛkṣitabhaṅga īṣat
BhP kāmānujena sahasā ta upaplutākṣāḥ
BhP munaya ūcuḥ
BhP ko vām ihaitya bhagavatparicaryayoccais
BhP taddharmiṇāṃ nivasatāṃ viṣamaḥ svabhāvaḥ
BhP tasmin praśāntapuruṣe gatavigrahe vāṃ
BhP ko vātmavat kuhakayoḥ pariśaṅkanīyaḥ
BhP na hy antaraṃ bhagavatīha samastakukṣāv
BhP ātmānam ātmani nabho nabhasīva dhīrāḥ
BhP paśyanti yatra yuvayoḥ suraliṅginoḥ kiṃ
BhP vyutpāditaṃ hy udarabhedi bhayaṃ yato 'sya
BhP tad vām amuṣya paramasya vikuṇṭhabhartuḥ
BhP kartuṃ prakṛṣṭam iha dhīmahi mandadhībhyām
BhP lokān ito vrajatam antarabhāvadṛṣṭyā
BhP pāpīyasas traya ime ripavo 'sya yatra
BhP teṣām itīritam ubhāv avadhārya ghoraṃ
BhP taṃ brahmadaṇḍam anivāraṇam astrapūgaiḥ
BhP sadyo harer anucarāv uru bibhyatas tat
BhP pādagrahāv apatatām atikātareṇa
BhP bhūyād aghoni bhagavadbhir akāri daṇḍo
BhP yo nau hareta surahelanam apy aśeṣam
BhP mā vo 'nutāpakalayā bhagavatsmṛtighno
BhP moho bhaved iha tu nau vrajator adho 'dhaḥ
BhP evaṃ tadaiva bhagavān aravindanābhaḥ
BhP svānāṃ vibudhya sadatikramam āryahṛdyaḥ
BhP tasmin yayau paramahaṃsamahāmunīnām
BhP anveṣaṇīyacaraṇau calayan sahaśrīḥ
BhP taṃ tv āgataṃ pratihṛtaupayikaṃ svapumbhis
BhP te 'cakṣatākṣaviṣayaṃ svasamādhibhāgyam
BhP haṃsaśriyor vyajanayoḥ śivavāyulolac
BhP chubhrātapatraśaśikesaraśīkarāmbum
BhP kṛtsnaprasādasumukhaṃ spṛhaṇīyadhāma
BhP snehāvalokakalayā hṛdi saṃspṛśantam
BhP śyāme pṛthāv urasi śobhitayā śriyā svaś
BhP cūḍāmaṇiṃ subhagayantam ivātmadhiṣṇyam
BhP pītāṃśuke pṛthunitambini visphurantyā
BhP kāñcyālibhir virutayā vanamālayā ca
BhP valguprakoṣṭhavalayaṃ vinatāsutāṃse
BhP vinyastahastam itareṇa dhunānam abjam
BhP vidyutkṣipanmakarakuṇḍalamaṇḍanārha
BhP gaṇḍasthalonnasamukhaṃ maṇimatkirīṭam
BhP dordaṇḍaṣaṇḍavivare haratā parārdhya
BhP hāreṇa kandharagatena ca kaustubhena
BhP atropasṛṣṭam iti cotsmitam indirāyāḥ
BhP svānāṃ dhiyā viracitaṃ bahusauṣṭhavāḍhyam
BhP mahyaṃ bhavasya bhavatāṃ ca bhajantam aṅgaṃ
BhP nemur nirīkṣya na vitṛptadṛśo mudā kaiḥ
BhP tasyāravindanayanasya padāravinda
BhP kiñjalkamiśratulasīmakarandavāyuḥ
BhP antargataḥ svavivareṇa cakāra teṣāṃ
BhP saṅkṣobham akṣarajuṣām api cittatanvoḥ
BhP te vā amuṣya vadanāsitapadmakośam
BhP udvīkṣya sundaratarādharakundahāsam
BhP labdhāśiṣaḥ punar avekṣya tadīyam aṅghri
BhP dvandvaṃ nakhāruṇamaṇiśrayaṇaṃ nidadhyuḥ
BhP puṃsāṃ gatiṃ mṛgayatām iha yogamārgair
BhP dhyānāspadaṃ bahumataṃ nayanābhirāmam
BhP pauṃsnaṃ vapur darśayānam ananyasiddhair
BhP autpattikaiḥ samagṛṇan yutam aṣṭabhogaiḥ
BhP kumārā ūcuḥ
BhP yo 'ntarhito hṛdi gato 'pi durātmanāṃ tvaṃ
BhP so 'dyaiva no nayanamūlam ananta rāddhaḥ
BhP yarhy eva karṇavivareṇa guhāṃ gato naḥ
BhP pitrānuvarṇitarahā bhavadudbhavena
BhP taṃ tvāṃ vidāma bhagavan param ātmatattvaṃ
BhP sattvena samprati ratiṃ racayantam eṣām
BhP yat te 'nutāpaviditair dṛḍhabhaktiyogair
BhP udgranthayo hṛdi vidur munayo virāgāḥ
BhP nātyantikaṃ vigaṇayanty api te prasādaṃ
BhP kimv anyad arpitabhayaṃ bhruva unnayais te
BhP ye 'ṅga tvadaṅghriśaraṇā bhavataḥ kathāyāḥ
BhP kīrtanyatīrthayaśasaḥ kuśalā rasajñāḥ
BhP kāmaṃ bhavaḥ svavṛjinair nirayeṣu naḥ stāc
BhP ceto 'livad yadi nu te padayo rameta
BhP vācaś ca nas tulasivad yadi te 'ṅghriśobhāḥ
BhP pūryeta te guṇagaṇair yadi karṇarandhraḥ
BhP prāduścakartha yad idaṃ puruhūta rūpaṃ
BhP teneśa nirvṛtim avāpur alaṃ dṛśo naḥ
BhP tasmā idaṃ bhagavate nama id vidhema
BhP yo 'nātmanāṃ durudayo bhagavān pratītaḥ
BhP brahmovāca
BhP iti tad gṛṇatāṃ teṣāṃ munīnāṃ yogadharmiṇām
BhP pratinandya jagādedaṃ vikuṇṭhanilayo vibhuḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP etau tau pārṣadau mahyaṃ jayo vijaya eva ca
BhP kadarthīkṛtya māṃ yad vo bahv akrātām atikramam
BhP yas tv etayor dhṛto daṇḍo bhavadbhir mām anuvrataiḥ
BhP sa evānumato 'smābhir munayo devahelanāt
BhP tad vaḥ prasādayāmy adya brahma daivaṃ paraṃ hi me
BhP tad dhīty ātmakṛtaṃ manye yat svapumbhir asatkṛtāḥ
BhP yannāmāni ca gṛhṇāti loko bhṛtye kṛtāgasi
BhP so 'sādhuvādas tatkīrtiṃ hanti tvacam ivāmayaḥ
BhP yasyāmṛtāmalayaśaḥśravaṇāvagāhaḥ
BhP sadyaḥ punāti jagad āśvapacād vikuṇṭhaḥ
BhP so 'haṃ bhavadbhya upalabdhasutīrthakīrtiś
BhP chindyāṃ svabāhum api vaḥ pratikūlavṛttim
BhP yatsevayā caraṇapadmapavitrareṇuṃ
BhP sadyaḥ kṣatākhilamalaṃ pratilabdhaśīlam
BhP na śrīr viraktam api māṃ vijahāti yasyāḥ
BhP prekṣālavārtha itare niyamān vahanti
BhP nāhaṃ tathādmi yajamānahavir vitāne
BhP ścyotadghṛtaplutam adan hutabhuṅmukhena
BhP yad brāhmaṇasya mukhataś carato 'nughāsaṃ
BhP tuṣṭasya mayy avahitair nijakarmapākaiḥ
BhP yeṣāṃ bibharmy aham akhaṇḍavikuṇṭhayoga
BhP māyāvibhūtir amalāṅghrirajaḥ kirīṭaiḥ
BhP viprāṃs tu ko na viṣaheta yadarhaṇāmbhaḥ
BhP sadyaḥ punāti sahacandralalāmalokān
BhP ye me tanūr dvijavarān duhatīr madīyā
BhP bhūtāny alabdhaśaraṇāni ca bhedabuddhyā
BhP drakṣyanty aghakṣatadṛśo hy ahimanyavas tān
BhP gṛdhrā ruṣā mama kuṣanty adhidaṇḍanetuḥ
BhP ye brāhmaṇān mayi dhiyā kṣipato 'rcayantas
BhP tuṣyaddhṛdaḥ smitasudhokṣitapadmavaktrāḥ
BhP vāṇyānurāgakalayātmajavad gṛṇantaḥ
BhP sambodhayanty aham ivāham upāhṛtas taiḥ
BhP tan me svabhartur avasāyam alakṣamāṇau
BhP yuṣmadvyatikramagatiṃ pratipadya sadyaḥ
BhP bhūyo mamāntikam itāṃ tad anugraho me
BhP yat kalpatām acirato bhṛtayor vivāsaḥ
BhP brahmovāca
BhP atha tasyośatīṃ devīm ṛṣikulyāṃ sarasvatīm
BhP nāsvādya manyudaṣṭānāṃ teṣām ātmāpy atṛpyata
BhP satīṃ vyādāya śṛṇvanto laghvīṃ gurvarthagahvarām
BhP vigāhyāgādhagambhīrāṃ na vidus taccikīrṣitam
BhP te yogamāyayārabdha pārameṣṭhyamahodayam
BhP procuḥ prāñjalayo viprāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ kṣubhitatvacaḥ
BhP ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
BhP na vayaṃ bhagavan vidmas tava deva cikīrṣitam
BhP kṛto me 'nugrahaś ceti yad adhyakṣaḥ prabhāṣase
BhP brahmaṇyasya paraṃ daivaṃ brāhmaṇāḥ kila te prabho
BhP viprāṇāṃ devadevānāṃ bhagavān ātmadaivatam
BhP tvattaḥ sanātano dharmo rakṣyate tanubhis tava
BhP dharmasya paramo guhyo nirvikāro bhavān mataḥ
BhP taranti hy añjasā mṛtyuṃ nivṛttā yadanugrahāt
BhP yoginaḥ sa bhavān kiṃ svid anugṛhyeta yat paraiḥ
BhP yaṃ vai vibhūtir upayāty anuvelam anyair
BhP arthārthibhiḥ svaśirasā dhṛtapādareṇuḥ
BhP dhanyārpitāṅghritulasīnavadāmadhāmno
BhP lokaṃ madhuvratapater iva kāmayānā
BhP yas tāṃ viviktacaritair anuvartamānāṃ
BhP nātyādriyat paramabhāgavataprasaṅgaḥ
BhP sa tvaṃ dvijānupathapuṇyarajaḥpunītaḥ
BhP śrīvatsalakṣma kim agā bhagabhājanas tvam
BhP dharmasya te bhagavatas triyuga tribhiḥ svaiḥ
BhP padbhiś carācaram idaṃ dvijadevatārtham
BhP nūnaṃ bhṛtaṃ tadabhighāti rajas tamaś ca
BhP sattvena no varadayā tanuvā nirasya
BhP na tvaṃ dvijottamakulaṃ yadi hātmagopaṃ
BhP goptā vṛṣaḥ svarhaṇena sasūnṛtena
BhP tarhy eva naṅkṣyati śivas tava deva panthā
BhP loko 'grahīṣyad ṛṣabhasya hi tat pramāṇam
BhP tat te 'nabhīṣṭam iva sattvanidher vidhitsoḥ
BhP kṣemaṃ janāya nijaśaktibhir uddhṛtāreḥ
BhP naitāvatā tryadhipater bata viśvabhartus
BhP tejaḥ kṣataṃ tv avanatasya sa te vinodaḥ
BhP yaṃ vānayor damam adhīśa bhavān vidhatte
BhP vṛttiṃ nu vā tad anumanmahi nirvyalīkam
BhP asmāsu vā ya ucito dhriyatāṃ sa daṇḍo
BhP ye 'nāgasau vayam ayuṅkṣmahi kilbiṣeṇa
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP etau suretaragatiṃ pratipadya sadyaḥ
BhP saṃrambhasambhṛtasamādhyanubaddhayogau
BhP bhūyaḥ sakāśam upayāsyata āśu yo vaḥ
BhP śāpo mayaiva nimitas tad aveta viprāḥ
BhP brahmovāca
BhP atha te munayo dṛṣṭvā nayanānandabhājanam
BhP vaikuṇṭhaṃ tadadhiṣṭhānaṃ vikuṇṭhaṃ ca svayaṃprabham
BhP bhagavantaṃ parikramya praṇipatyānumānya ca
BhP pratijagmuḥ pramuditāḥ śaṃsanto vaiṣṇavīṃ śriyam
BhP bhagavān anugāv āha yātaṃ mā bhaiṣṭam astu śam
BhP brahmatejaḥ samartho 'pi hantuṃ necche mataṃ tu me
BhP etat puraiva nirdiṣṭaṃ ramayā kruddhayā yadā
BhP purāpavāritā dvāri viśantī mayy upārate
BhP mayi saṃrambhayogena nistīrya brahmahelanam
BhP pratyeṣyataṃ nikāśaṃ me kālenālpīyasā punaḥ
BhP dvāḥsthāv ādiśya bhagavān vimānaśreṇibhūṣaṇam
BhP sarvātiśayayā lakṣmyā juṣṭaṃ svaṃ dhiṣṇyam āviśat
BhP tau tu gīrvāṇaṛṣabhau dustarād dharilokataḥ
BhP hataśriyau brahmaśāpād abhūtāṃ vigatasmayau
BhP tadā vikuṇṭhadhiṣaṇāt tayor nipatamānayoḥ
BhP hāhākāro mahān āsīd vimānāgryeṣu putrakāḥ
BhP tāv eva hy adhunā prāptau pārṣadapravarau hareḥ
BhP diter jaṭharanirviṣṭaṃ kāśyapaṃ teja ulbaṇam
BhP tayor asurayor adya tejasā yamayor hi vaḥ
BhP ākṣiptaṃ teja etarhi bhagavāṃs tad vidhitsati
BhP viśvasya yaḥ sthitilayodbhavahetur ādyo
BhP yogeśvarair api duratyayayogamāyaḥ
BhP kṣemaṃ vidhāsyati sa no bhagavāṃs tryadhīśas
BhP tatrāsmadīyavimṛśena kiyān ihārthaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP niśamyātmabhuvā gītaṃ kāraṇaṃ śaṅkayojjhitāḥ
BhP tataḥ sarve nyavartanta tridivāya divaukasaḥ
BhP ditis tu bhartur ādeśād apatyapariśaṅkinī
BhP pūrṇe varṣaśate sādhvī putrau prasuṣuve yamau
BhP utpātā bahavas tatra nipetur jāyamānayoḥ
BhP divi bhuvy antarikṣe ca lokasyorubhayāvahāḥ
BhP sahācalā bhuvaś celur diśaḥ sarvāḥ prajajvaluḥ
BhP solkāś cāśanayaḥ petuḥ ketavaś cārtihetavaḥ
BhP vavau vāyuḥ suduḥsparśaḥ phūtkārān īrayan muhuḥ
BhP unmūlayan nagapatīn vātyānīko rajodhvajaḥ
BhP uddhasattaḍidambhoda ghaṭayā naṣṭabhāgaṇe
BhP vyomni praviṣṭatamasā na sma vyādṛśyate padam
BhP cukrośa vimanā vārdhir udūrmiḥ kṣubhitodaraḥ
BhP sodapānāś ca saritaś cukṣubhuḥ śuṣkapaṅkajāḥ
BhP muhuḥ paridhayo 'bhūvan sarāhvoḥ śaśisūryayoḥ
BhP nirghātā rathanirhrādā vivarebhyaḥ prajajñire
BhP antargrāmeṣu mukhato vamantyo vahnim ulbaṇam
BhP sṛgālolūkaṭaṅkāraiḥ praṇedur aśivaṃ śivāḥ
BhP saṅgītavad rodanavad unnamayya śirodharām
BhP vyamuñcan vividhā vāco grāmasiṃhās tatas tataḥ
BhP kharāś ca karkaśaiḥ kṣattaḥ khurair ghnanto dharātalam
