BhP khārkārarabhasā mattāḥ paryadhāvan varūthaśaḥ
BhP rudanto rāsabhatrastā nīḍād udapatan khagāḥ
BhP ghoṣe 'raṇye ca paśavaḥ śakṛnmūtram akurvata
BhP gāvo 'trasann asṛgdohās toyadāḥ pūyavarṣiṇaḥ
BhP vyarudan devaliṅgāni drumāḥ petur vinānilam
BhP grahān puṇyatamān anye bhagaṇāṃś cāpi dīpitāḥ
BhP aticerur vakragatyā yuyudhuś ca parasparam
BhP dṛṣṭvānyāṃś ca mahotpātān atattattvavidaḥ prajāḥ
BhP brahmaputrān ṛte bhītā menire viśvasamplavam
BhP tāv ādidaityau sahasā vyajyamānātmapauruṣau
BhP vavṛdhāte 'śmasāreṇa kāyenādripatī iva
BhP divispṛśau hemakirīṭakoṭibhir niruddhakāṣṭhau sphuradaṅgadābhujau
BhP gāṃ kampayantau caraṇaiḥ pade pade kaṭyā sukāñcyārkam atītya tasthatuḥ
BhP prajāpatir nāma tayor akārṣīd yaḥ prāk svadehād yamayor ajāyata
BhP taṃ vai hiraṇyakaśipuṃ viduḥ prajā yaṃ taṃ hiraṇyākṣam asūta sāgrataḥ
BhP cakre hiraṇyakaśipur dorbhyāṃ brahmavareṇa ca
BhP vaśe sapālān lokāṃs trīn akutomṛtyur uddhataḥ
BhP hiraṇyākṣo 'nujas tasya priyaḥ prītikṛd anvaham
BhP gadāpāṇir divaṃ yāto yuyutsur mṛgayan raṇam
BhP taṃ vīkṣya duḥsahajavaṃ raṇatkāñcananūpuram
BhP vaijayantyā srajā juṣṭam aṃsanyastamahāgadam
BhP manovīryavarotsiktam asṛṇyam akutobhayam
BhP bhītā nililyire devās tārkṣyatrastā ivāhayaḥ
BhP sa vai tirohitān dṛṣṭvā mahasā svena daityarāṭ
BhP sendrān devagaṇān kṣībān apaśyan vyanadad bhṛśam
BhP tato nivṛttaḥ krīḍiṣyan gambhīraṃ bhīmanisvanam
BhP vijagāhe mahāsattvo vārdhiṃ matta iva dvipaḥ
BhP tasmin praviṣṭe varuṇasya sainikā yādogaṇāḥ sannadhiyaḥ sasādhvasāḥ
BhP ahanyamānā api tasya varcasā pradharṣitā dūrataraṃ pradudruvuḥ
BhP sa varṣapūgān udadhau mahābalaś caran mahormīñ chvasaneritān muhuḥ
BhP maurvyābhijaghne gadayā vibhāvarīm āsedivāṃs tāta purīṃ pracetasaḥ
BhP tatropalabhyāsuralokapālakaṃ yādogaṇānām ṛṣabhaṃ pracetasam
BhP smayan pralabdhuṃ praṇipatya nīcavaj jagāda me dehy adhirāja saṃyugam
BhP tvaṃ lokapālo 'dhipatir bṛhacchravā vīryāpaho durmadavīramāninām
BhP vijitya loke 'khiladaityadānavān yad rājasūyena purāyajat prabho
BhP sa evam utsiktamadena vidviṣā dṛḍhaṃ pralabdho bhagavān apāṃ patiḥ
BhP roṣaṃ samutthaṃ śamayan svayā dhiyā vyavocad aṅgopaśamaṃ gatā vayam
BhP paśyāmi nānyaṃ puruṣāt purātanād yaḥ saṃyuge tvāṃ raṇamārgakovidam
BhP ārādhayiṣyaty asurarṣabhehi taṃ manasvino yaṃ gṛṇate bhavādṛśāḥ
BhP taṃ vīram ārād abhipadya vismayaḥ śayiṣyase vīraśaye śvabhir vṛtaḥ
BhP yas tvadvidhānām asatāṃ praśāntaye rūpāṇi dhatte sadanugrahecchayā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP tad evam ākarṇya jaleśabhāṣitaṃ mahāmanās tad vigaṇayya durmadaḥ
BhP harer viditvā gatim aṅga nāradād rasātalaṃ nirviviśe tvarānvitaḥ
BhP dadarśa tatrābhijitaṃ dharādharaṃ pronnīyamānāvanim agradaṃṣṭrayā
BhP muṣṇantam akṣṇā svaruco 'ruṇaśriyā jahāsa cāho vanagocaro mṛgaḥ
BhP āhainam ehy ajña mahīṃ vimuñca no rasaukasāṃ viśvasṛjeyam arpitā
BhP na svasti yāsyasy anayā mamekṣataḥ surādhamāsāditasūkarākṛte
BhP tvaṃ naḥ sapatnair abhavāya kiṃ bhṛto yo māyayā hanty asurān parokṣajit
BhP tvāṃ yogamāyābalam alpapauruṣaṃ saṃsthāpya mūḍha pramṛje suhṛcchucaḥ
BhP tvayi saṃsthite gadayā śīrṇaśīrṣaṇy asmadbhujacyutayā ye ca tubhyam
BhP baliṃ haranty ṛṣayo ye ca devāḥ svayaṃ sarve na bhaviṣyanty amūlāḥ
BhP sa tudyamāno 'riduruktatomarair daṃṣṭrāgragāṃ gām upalakṣya bhītām
BhP todaṃ mṛṣan niragād ambumadhyād grāhāhataḥ sakareṇur yathebhaḥ
BhP taṃ niḥsarantaṃ salilād anudruto hiraṇyakeśo dviradaṃ yathā jhaṣaḥ
BhP karāladaṃṣṭro 'śaninisvano 'bravīd gatahriyāṃ kiṃ tv asatāṃ vigarhitam
BhP sa gām udastāt salilasya gocare vinyasya tasyām adadhāt svasattvam
BhP abhiṣṭuto viśvasṛjā prasūnair āpūryamāṇo vibudhaiḥ paśyato 'reḥ
BhP parānuṣaktaṃ tapanīyopakalpaṃ mahāgadaṃ kāñcanacitradaṃśam
BhP marmāṇy abhīkṣṇaṃ pratudantaṃ duruktaiḥ pracaṇḍamanyuḥ prahasaṃs taṃ babhāṣe
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP satyaṃ vayaṃ bho vanagocarā mṛgā yuṣmadvidhān mṛgaye grāmasiṃhān
BhP na mṛtyupāśaiḥ pratimuktasya vīrā vikatthanaṃ tava gṛhṇanty abhadra
BhP ete vayaṃ nyāsaharā rasaukasāṃ gatahriyo gadayā drāvitās te
BhP tiṣṭhāmahe 'thāpi kathañcid ājau stheyaṃ kva yāmo balinotpādya vairam
BhP tvaṃ padrathānāṃ kila yūthapādhipo ghaṭasva no 'svastaya āśv anūhaḥ
BhP saṃsthāpya cāsmān pramṛjāśru svakānāṃ yaḥ svāṃ pratijñāṃ nātipiparty asabhyaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP so 'dhikṣipto bhagavatā pralabdhaś ca ruṣā bhṛśam
BhP ājahārolbaṇaṃ krodhaṃ krīḍyamāno 'hirāḍ iva
BhP sṛjann amarṣitaḥ śvāsān manyupracalitendriyaḥ
BhP āsādya tarasā daityo gadayā nyahanad dharim
BhP bhagavāṃs tu gadāvegaṃ visṛṣṭaṃ ripuṇorasi
BhP avañcayat tiraścīno yogārūḍha ivāntakam
BhP punar gadāṃ svām ādāya bhrāmayantam abhīkṣṇaśaḥ
BhP abhyadhāvad dhariḥ kruddhaḥ saṃrambhād daṣṭadacchadam
BhP tataś ca gadayārātiṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ bhruvi prabhuḥ
BhP ājaghne sa tu tāṃ saumya gadayā kovido 'hanat
BhP evaṃ gadābhyāṃ gurvībhyāṃ haryakṣo harir eva ca
BhP jigīṣayā susaṃrabdhāv anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ
BhP tayoḥ spṛdhos tigmagadāhatāṅgayoḥ kṣatāsravaghrāṇavivṛddhamanyvoḥ
BhP vicitramārgāṃś carator jigīṣayā vyabhād ilāyām iva śuṣmiṇor mṛdhaḥ
BhP daityasya yajñāvayavasya māyā gṛhītavārāhatanor mahātmanaḥ
BhP kauravya mahyāṃ dviṣator vimardanaṃ didṛkṣur āgād ṛṣibhir vṛtaḥ svarāṭ
BhP āsannaśauṇḍīram apetasādhvasaṃ kṛtapratīkāram ahāryavikramam
BhP vilakṣya daityaṃ bhagavān sahasraṇīr jagāda nārāyaṇam ādisūkaram
BhP brahmovāca
BhP eṣa te deva devānām aṅghrimūlam upeyuṣām
BhP viprāṇāṃ saurabheyīṇāṃ bhūtānām apy anāgasām
BhP āgaskṛd bhayakṛd duṣkṛd asmadrāddhavaro 'suraḥ
BhP anveṣann apratiratho lokān aṭati kaṇṭakaḥ
BhP mainaṃ māyāvinaṃ dṛptaṃ niraṅkuśam asattamam
BhP ākrīḍa bālavad deva yathāśīviṣam utthitam
BhP na yāvad eṣa vardheta svāṃ velāṃ prāpya dāruṇaḥ
BhP svāṃ deva māyām āsthāya tāvaj jahy agham acyuta
BhP eṣā ghoratamā sandhyā lokacchambaṭkarī prabho
BhP upasarpati sarvātman surāṇāṃ jayam āvaha
BhP adhunaiṣo 'bhijin nāma yogo mauhūrtiko hy agāt
BhP śivāya nas tvaṃ suhṛdām āśu nistara dustaram
BhP diṣṭyā tvāṃ vihitaṃ mṛtyum ayam āsāditaḥ svayam
BhP vikramyainaṃ mṛdhe hatvā lokān ādhehi śarmaṇi
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP avadhārya viriñcasya nirvyalīkāmṛtaṃ vacaḥ
BhP prahasya premagarbheṇa tad apāṅgena so 'grahīt
BhP tataḥ sapatnaṃ mukhataś carantam akutobhayam
BhP jaghānotpatya gadayā hanāv asuram akṣajaḥ
BhP sā hatā tena gadayā vihatā bhagavatkarāt
BhP vighūrṇitāpatad reje tad adbhutam ivābhavat
BhP sa tadā labdhatīrtho 'pi na babādhe nirāyudham
BhP mānayan sa mṛdhe dharmaṃ viṣvaksenaṃ prakopayan
BhP gadāyām apaviddhāyāṃ hāhākāre vinirgate
BhP mānayām āsa taddharmaṃ sunābhaṃ cāsmarad vibhuḥ
BhP taṃ vyagracakraṃ ditiputrādhamena svapārṣadamukhyena viṣajjamānam
BhP citrā vāco 'tadvidāṃ khecarāṇāṃ tatra smāsan svasti te 'muṃ jahīti
BhP sa taṃ niśāmyāttarathāṅgam agrato vyavasthitaṃ padmapalāśalocanam
BhP vilokya cāmarṣapariplutendriyo ruṣā svadantacchadam ādaśac chvasan
BhP karāladaṃṣṭraś cakṣurbhyāṃ sañcakṣāṇo dahann iva
BhP abhiplutya svagadayā hato 'sīty āhanad dharim
BhP padā savyena tāṃ sādho bhagavān yajñasūkaraḥ
BhP līlayā miṣataḥ śatroḥ prāharad vātaraṃhasam
BhP āha cāyudham ādhatsva ghaṭasva tvaṃ jigīṣasi
BhP ity uktaḥ sa tadā bhūyas tāḍayan vyanadad bhṛśam
BhP tāṃ sa āpatatīṃ vīkṣya bhagavān samavasthitaḥ
BhP jagrāha līlayā prāptāṃ garutmān iva pannagīm
BhP svapauruṣe pratihate hatamāno mahāsuraḥ
BhP naicchad gadāṃ dīyamānāṃ hariṇā vigataprabhaḥ
BhP jagrāha triśikhaṃ śūlaṃ jvalajjvalanalolupam
BhP yajñāya dhṛtarūpāya viprāyābhicaran yathā
BhP tad ojasā daityamahābhaṭārpitaṃ cakāsad antaḥkha udīrṇadīdhiti
BhP cakreṇa ciccheda niśātaneminā harir yathā tārkṣyapatatram ujjhitam
BhP vṛkṇe svaśūle bahudhāriṇā hareḥ pratyetya vistīrṇam uro vibhūtimat
BhP pravṛddharoṣaḥ sa kaṭhoramuṣṭinā nadan prahṛtyāntaradhīyatāsuraḥ
BhP tenettham āhataḥ kṣattar bhagavān ādisūkaraḥ
BhP nākampata manāk kvāpi srajā hata iva dvipaḥ
BhP athorudhāsṛjan māyāṃ yogamāyeśvare harau
BhP yāṃ vilokya prajās trastā menire 'syopasaṃyamam
BhP pravavur vāyavaś caṇḍās tamaḥ pāṃsavam airayan
BhP digbhyo nipetur grāvāṇaḥ kṣepaṇaiḥ prahitā iva
BhP dyaur naṣṭabhagaṇābhraughaiḥ savidyutstanayitnubhiḥ
BhP varṣadbhiḥ pūyakeśāsṛg viṇmūtrāsthīni cāsakṛt
BhP girayaḥ pratyadṛśyanta nānāyudhamuco 'nagha
BhP digvāsaso yātudhānyaḥ śūlinyo muktamūrdhajāḥ
BhP bahubhir yakṣarakṣobhiḥ pattyaśvarathakuñjaraiḥ
BhP ātatāyibhir utsṛṣṭā hiṃsrā vāco 'tivaiśasāḥ
BhP prāduṣkṛtānāṃ māyānām āsurīṇāṃ vināśayat
BhP sudarśanāstraṃ bhagavān prāyuṅkta dayitaṃ tripāt
BhP tadā diteḥ samabhavat sahasā hṛdi vepathuḥ
BhP smarantyā bhartur ādeśaṃ stanāc cāsṛk prasusruve
BhP vinaṣṭāsu svamāyāsu bhūyaś cāvrajya keśavam
BhP ruṣopagūhamāno 'muṃ dadṛśe 'vasthitaṃ bahiḥ
BhP taṃ muṣṭibhir vinighnantaṃ vajrasārair adhokṣajaḥ
BhP kareṇa karṇamūle 'han yathā tvāṣṭraṃ marutpatiḥ
BhP sa āhato viśvajitā hy avajñayā paribhramadgātra udastalocanaḥ
BhP viśīrṇabāhvaṅghriśiroruho 'patad yathā nagendro lulito nabhasvatā
BhP kṣitau śayānaṃ tam akuṇṭhavarcasaṃ karāladaṃṣṭraṃ paridaṣṭadacchadam
BhP ajādayo vīkṣya śaśaṃsur āgatā aho imaṃ ko nu labheta saṃsthitim
BhP yaṃ yogino yogasamādhinā raho dhyāyanti liṅgād asato mumukṣayā
BhP tasyaiṣa daityaṛṣabhaḥ padāhato mukhaṃ prapaśyaṃs tanum utsasarja ha
BhP etau tau pārṣadāv asya śāpād yātāv asadgatim
BhP punaḥ katipayaiḥ sthānaṃ prapatsyete ha janmabhiḥ
BhP devā ūcuḥ
BhP namo namas te 'khilayajñatantave sthitau gṛhītāmalasattvamūrtaye
BhP diṣṭyā hato 'yaṃ jagatām aruntudas tvatpādabhaktyā vayam īśa nirvṛtāḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ hiraṇyākṣam asahyavikramaṃ sa sādayitvā harir ādisūkaraḥ
BhP jagāma lokaṃ svam akhaṇḍitotsavaṃ samīḍitaḥ puṣkaraviṣṭarādibhiḥ
BhP mayā yathānūktam avādi te hareḥ kṛtāvatārasya sumitra ceṣṭitam
BhP yathā hiraṇyākṣa udāravikramo mahāmṛdhe krīḍanavan nirākṛtaḥ
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP iti kauṣāravākhyātām āśrutya bhagavatkathām
BhP kṣattānandaṃ paraṃ lebhe mahābhāgavato dvija
BhP anyeṣāṃ puṇyaślokānām uddāmayaśasāṃ satām
BhP upaśrutya bhaven modaḥ śrīvatsāṅkasya kiṃ punaḥ
BhP yo gajendraṃ jhaṣagrastaṃ dhyāyantaṃ caraṇāmbujam
BhP krośantīnāṃ kareṇūnāṃ kṛcchrato 'mocayad drutam
BhP taṃ sukhārādhyam ṛjubhir ananyaśaraṇair nṛbhiḥ
BhP kṛtajñaḥ ko na seveta durārādhyam asādhubhiḥ
BhP yo vai hiraṇyākṣavadhaṃ mahādbhutaṃ vikrīḍitaṃ kāraṇasūkarātmanaḥ
BhP śṛṇoti gāyaty anumodate 'ñjasā vimucyate brahmavadhād api dvijāḥ
BhP etan mahāpuṇyam alaṃ pavitraṃ dhanyaṃ yaśasyaṃ padam āyurāśiṣām
BhP prāṇendriyāṇāṃ yudhi śauryavardhanaṃ nārāyaṇo 'nte gatir aṅga śṛṇvatām
BhP śaunaka uvāca
BhP mahīṃ pratiṣṭhām adhyasya saute svāyambhuvo manuḥ
BhP kāny anvatiṣṭhad dvārāṇi mārgāyāvarajanmanām
BhP kṣattā mahābhāgavataḥ kṛṣṇasyaikāntikaḥ suhṛt
BhP yas tatyājāgrajaṃ kṛṣṇe sāpatyam aghavān iti
BhP dvaipāyanād anavaro mahitve tasya dehajaḥ
BhP sarvātmanā śritaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ tatparāṃś cāpy anuvrataḥ
BhP kim anvapṛcchan maitreyaṃ virajās tīrthasevayā
BhP upagamya kuśāvarta āsīnaṃ tattvavittamam
BhP tayoḥ saṃvadatoḥ sūta pravṛttā hy amalāḥ kathāḥ
BhP āpo gāṅgā ivāghaghnīr hareḥ pādāmbujāśrayāḥ
BhP tā naḥ kīrtaya bhadraṃ te kīrtanyodārakarmaṇaḥ
BhP rasajñaḥ ko nu tṛpyeta harilīlāmṛtaṃ piban
BhP evam ugraśravāḥ pṛṣṭa ṛṣibhir naimiṣāyanaiḥ
BhP bhagavaty arpitādhyātmas tān āha śrūyatām iti
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP harer dhṛtakroḍatanoḥ svamāyayā niśamya gor uddharaṇaṃ rasātalāt
BhP līlāṃ hiraṇyākṣam avajñayā hataṃ sañjātaharṣo munim āha bhārataḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP prajāpatipatiḥ sṛṣṭvā prajāsarge prajāpatīn
BhP kim ārabhata me brahman prabrūhy avyaktamārgavit
BhP ye marīcyādayo viprā yas tu svāyambhuvo manuḥ
BhP te vai brahmaṇa ādeśāt katham etad abhāvayan
BhP sadvitīyāḥ kim asṛjan svatantrā uta karmasu
BhP āho svit saṃhatāḥ sarva idaṃ sma samakalpayan
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP daivena durvitarkyeṇa pareṇānimiṣeṇa ca
BhP jātakṣobhād bhagavato mahān āsīd guṇatrayāt
BhP rajaḥpradhānān mahatas triliṅgo daivacoditāt
BhP jātaḥ sasarja bhūtādir viyadādīni pañcaśaḥ
BhP tāni caikaikaśaḥ sraṣṭum asamarthāni bhautikam
BhP saṃhatya daivayogena haimam aṇḍam avāsṛjan
BhP so 'śayiṣṭābdhisalile āṇḍakośo nirātmakaḥ
BhP sāgraṃ vai varṣasāhasram anvavātsīt tam īśvaraḥ
BhP tasya nābher abhūt padmaṃ sahasrārkorudīdhiti
BhP sarvajīvanikāyauko yatra svayam abhūt svarāṭ
BhP so 'nuviṣṭo bhagavatā yaḥ śete salilāśaye
BhP lokasaṃsthāṃ yathā pūrvaṃ nirmame saṃsthayā svayā
BhP sasarja cchāyayāvidyāṃ pañcaparvāṇam agrataḥ
BhP tāmisram andhatāmisraṃ tamo moho mahātamaḥ
BhP visasarjātmanaḥ kāyaṃ nābhinandaṃs tamomayam
BhP jagṛhur yakṣarakṣāṃsi rātriṃ kṣuttṛṭsamudbhavām
BhP kṣuttṛḍbhyām upasṛṣṭās te taṃ jagdhum abhidudruvuḥ
BhP mā rakṣatainaṃ jakṣadhvam ity ūcuḥ kṣuttṛḍarditāḥ
BhP devas tān āha saṃvigno mā māṃ jakṣata rakṣata
BhP aho me yakṣarakṣāṃsi prajā yūyaṃ babhūvitha
BhP devatāḥ prabhayā yā yā dīvyan pramukhato 'sṛjat
BhP te ahārṣur devayanto visṛṣṭāṃ tāṃ prabhām ahaḥ
BhP devo 'devāñ jaghanataḥ sṛjati smātilolupān
BhP ta enaṃ lolupatayā maithunāyābhipedire
BhP tato hasan sa bhagavān asurair nirapatrapaiḥ
BhP anvīyamānas tarasā kruddho bhītaḥ parāpatat
BhP sa upavrajya varadaṃ prapannārtiharaṃ harim
BhP anugrahāya bhaktānām anurūpātmadarśanam
BhP pāhi māṃ paramātmaṃs te preṣaṇenāsṛjaṃ prajāḥ
BhP tā imā yabhituṃ pāpā upākrāmanti māṃ prabho
BhP tvam ekaḥ kila lokānāṃ kliṣṭānāṃ kleśanāśanaḥ
BhP tvam ekaḥ kleśadas teṣām anāsannapadāṃ tava
BhP so 'vadhāryāsya kārpaṇyaṃ viviktādhyātmadarśanaḥ
BhP vimuñcātmatanuṃ ghorām ity ukto vimumoca ha
BhP tāṃ kvaṇaccaraṇāmbhojāṃ madavihvalalocanām
BhP kāñcīkalāpavilasad dukūlacchannarodhasam
BhP anyonyaśleṣayottuṅga nirantarapayodharām
BhP sunāsāṃ sudvijāṃ snigdha hāsalīlāvalokanām
BhP gūhantīṃ vrīḍayātmānaṃ nīlālakavarūthinīm
BhP upalabhyāsurā dharma sarve sammumuhuḥ striyam
BhP aho rūpam aho dhairyam aho asyā navaṃ vayaḥ
BhP madhye kāmayamānānām akāmeva visarpati
BhP vitarkayanto bahudhā tāṃ sandhyāṃ pramadākṛtim
BhP abhisambhāvya viśrambhāt paryapṛcchan kumedhasaḥ
BhP kāsi kasyāsi rambhoru ko vārthas te 'tra bhāmini
BhP rūpadraviṇapaṇyena durbhagān no vibādhase
BhP yā vā kācit tvam abale diṣṭyā sandarśanaṃ tava
BhP utsunoṣīkṣamāṇānāṃ kandukakrīḍayā manaḥ
BhP naikatra te jayati śālini pādapadmaṃ
BhP ghnantyā muhuḥ karatalena patatpataṅgam
BhP madhyaṃ viṣīdati bṛhatstanabhārabhītaṃ
BhP śānteva dṛṣṭir amalā suśikhāsamūhaḥ
BhP iti sāyantanīṃ sandhyām asurāḥ pramadāyatīm
BhP pralobhayantīṃ jagṛhur matvā mūḍhadhiyaḥ striyam
BhP prahasya bhāvagambhīraṃ jighrantyātmānam ātmanā
BhP kāntyā sasarja bhagavān gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇān
BhP visasarja tanuṃ tāṃ vai jyotsnāṃ kāntimatīṃ priyām
BhP ta eva cādaduḥ prītyā viśvāvasupurogamāḥ
BhP sṛṣṭvā bhūtapiśācāṃś ca bhagavān ātmatandriṇā
BhP digvāsaso muktakeśān vīkṣya cāmīlayad dṛśau
BhP jagṛhus tadvisṛṣṭāṃ tāṃ jṛmbhaṇākhyāṃ tanuṃ prabhoḥ
BhP nidrām indriyavikledo yayā bhūteṣu dṛśyate
BhP yenocchiṣṭān dharṣayanti tam unmādaṃ pracakṣate
BhP ūrjasvantaṃ manyamāna ātmānaṃ bhagavān ajaḥ
BhP sādhyān gaṇān pitṛgaṇān parokṣeṇāsṛjat prabhuḥ
BhP ta ātmasargaṃ taṃ kāyaṃ pitaraḥ pratipedire
BhP sādhyebhyaś ca pitṛbhyaś ca kavayo yad vitanvate
BhP siddhān vidyādharāṃś caiva tirodhānena so 'sṛjat
BhP tebhyo 'dadāt tam ātmānam antardhānākhyam adbhutam
BhP sa kinnarān kimpuruṣān pratyātmyenāsṛjat prabhuḥ
BhP mānayann ātmanātmānam ātmābhāsaṃ vilokayan
BhP te tu taj jagṛhū rūpaṃ tyaktaṃ yat parameṣṭhinā
BhP mithunībhūya gāyantas tam evoṣasi karmabhiḥ
BhP dehena vai bhogavatā śayāno bahucintayā
BhP sarge 'nupacite krodhād utsasarja ha tad vapuḥ
BhP ye 'hīyantāmutaḥ keśā ahayas te 'ṅga jajñire
BhP sarpāḥ prasarpataḥ krūrā nāgā bhogorukandharāḥ
BhP sa ātmānaṃ manyamānaḥ kṛtakṛtyam ivātmabhūḥ
BhP tadā manūn sasarjānte manasā lokabhāvanān
BhP tebhyaḥ so 'sṛjat svīyaṃ puraṃ puruṣam ātmavān
BhP tān dṛṣṭvā ye purā sṛṣṭāḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ prajāpatim
BhP aho etaj jagatsraṣṭaḥ sukṛtaṃ bata te kṛtam
BhP pratiṣṭhitāḥ kriyā yasmin sākam annam adāma he
BhP tapasā vidyayā yukto yogena susamādhinā
BhP ṛṣīn ṛṣir hṛṣīkeśaḥ sasarjābhimatāḥ prajāḥ
BhP tebhyaś caikaikaśaḥ svasya dehasyāṃśam adād ajaḥ
BhP yat tat samādhiyogarddhi tapovidyāviraktimat
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP svāyambhuvasya ca manor aṃśaḥ paramasammataḥ
BhP kathyatāṃ bhagavan yatra maithunenaidhire prajāḥ
BhP priyavratottānapādau sutau svāyambhuvasya vai
BhP yathādharmaṃ jugupatuḥ saptadvīpavatīṃ mahīm
BhP tasya vai duhitā brahman devahūtīti viśrutā
BhP patnī prajāpater uktā kardamasya tvayānagha
BhP tasyāṃ sa vai mahāyogī yuktāyāṃ yogalakṣaṇaiḥ
BhP sasarja katidhā vīryaṃ tan me śuśrūṣave vada
BhP rucir yo bhagavān brahman dakṣo vā brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ
BhP yathā sasarja bhūtāni labdhvā bhāryāṃ ca mānavīm
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP prajāḥ sṛjeti bhagavān kardamo brahmaṇoditaḥ
BhP sarasvatyāṃ tapas tepe sahasrāṇāṃ samā daśa
BhP tataḥ samādhiyuktena kriyāyogena kardamaḥ
BhP samprapede hariṃ bhaktyā prapannavaradāśuṣam
BhP tāvat prasanno bhagavān puṣkarākṣaḥ kṛte yuge
BhP darśayām āsa taṃ kṣattaḥ śābdaṃ brahma dadhad vapuḥ
BhP sa taṃ virajam arkābhaṃ sitapadmotpalasrajam
BhP snigdhanīlālakavrāta vaktrābjaṃ virajo 'mbaram
BhP kirīṭinaṃ kuṇḍalinaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam
BhP śvetotpalakrīḍanakaṃ manaḥsparśasmitekṣaṇam
BhP vinyastacaraṇāmbhojam aṃsadeśe garutmataḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā khe 'vasthitaṃ vakṣaḥ śriyaṃ kaustubhakandharam
BhP jātaharṣo 'patan mūrdhnā kṣitau labdhamanorathaḥ
BhP gīrbhis tv abhyagṛṇāt prīti svabhāvātmā kṛtāñjaliḥ
BhP ṛṣir uvāca
BhP juṣṭaṃ batādyākhilasattvarāśeḥ sāṃsiddhyam akṣṇos tava darśanān naḥ
BhP yaddarśanaṃ janmabhir īḍya sadbhir āśāsate yogino rūḍhayogāḥ
BhP ye māyayā te hatamedhasas tvat pādāravindaṃ bhavasindhupotam
BhP upāsate kāmalavāya teṣāṃ rāsīśa kāmān niraye 'pi ye syuḥ
BhP tathā sa cāhaṃ parivoḍhukāmaḥ samānaśīlāṃ gṛhamedhadhenum
BhP upeyivān mūlam aśeṣamūlaṃ durāśayaḥ kāmadughāṅghripasya
BhP prajāpates te vacasādhīśa tantyā lokaḥ kilāyaṃ kāmahato 'nubaddhaḥ
BhP ahaṃ ca lokānugato vahāmi baliṃ ca śuklānimiṣāya tubhyam
BhP lokāṃś ca lokānugatān paśūṃś ca hitvā śritās te caraṇātapatram
BhP parasparaṃ tvadguṇavādasīdhu pīyūṣaniryāpitadehadharmāḥ
BhP na te 'jarākṣabhramir āyur eṣāṃ trayodaśāraṃ triśataṃ ṣaṣṭiparva
BhP ṣaṇnemy anantacchadi yat triṇābhi karālasroto jagad ācchidya dhāvat
BhP ekaḥ svayaṃ san jagataḥ sisṛkṣayā dvitīyayātmann adhiyogamāyayā
BhP sṛjasy adaḥ pāsi punar grasiṣyase yathorṇanābhir bhagavan svaśaktibhiḥ
BhP naitad batādhīśa padaṃ tavepsitaṃ yan māyayā nas tanuṣe bhūtasūkṣmam
BhP anugrahāyāstv api yarhi māyayā lasattulasyā bhagavān vilakṣitaḥ
BhP taṃ tvānubhūtyoparatakriyārthaṃ svamāyayā vartitalokatantram
BhP namāmy abhīkṣṇaṃ namanīyapāda sarojam alpīyasi kāmavarṣam
BhP ṛṣir uvāca
BhP ity avyalīkaṃ praṇuto 'bjanābhas tam ābabhāṣe vacasāmṛtena
BhP suparṇapakṣopari rocamānaḥ premasmitodvīkṣaṇavibhramadbhrūḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP viditvā tava caityaṃ me puraiva samayoji tat
BhP yadartham ātmaniyamais tvayaivāhaṃ samarcitaḥ
BhP na vai jātu mṛṣaiva syāt prajādhyakṣa madarhaṇam
BhP bhavadvidheṣv atitarāṃ mayi saṅgṛbhitātmanām
BhP prajāpatisutaḥ samrāṇ manur vikhyātamaṅgalaḥ
BhP brahmāvartaṃ yo 'dhivasan śāsti saptārṇavāṃ mahīm
BhP sa ceha vipra rājarṣir mahiṣyā śatarūpayā
BhP āyāsyati didṛkṣus tvāṃ paraśvo dharmakovidaḥ
BhP ātmajām asitāpāṅgīṃ vayaḥśīlaguṇānvitām
BhP mṛgayantīṃ patiṃ dāsyaty anurūpāya te prabho
BhP samāhitaṃ te hṛdayaṃ yatremān parivatsarān
BhP sā tvāṃ brahman nṛpavadhūḥ kāmam āśu bhajiṣyati
BhP yā ta ātmabhṛtaṃ vīryaṃ navadhā prasaviṣyati
BhP vīrye tvadīye ṛṣaya ādhāsyanty añjasātmanaḥ
BhP tvaṃ ca samyag anuṣṭhāya nideśaṃ ma uśattamaḥ
BhP mayi tīrthīkṛtāśeṣa kriyārtho māṃ prapatsyase
BhP kṛtvā dayāṃ ca jīveṣu dattvā cābhayam ātmavān
BhP mayy ātmānaṃ saha jagad drakṣyasy ātmani cāpi mām
BhP sahāhaṃ svāṃśakalayā tvadvīryeṇa mahāmune
BhP tava kṣetre devahūtyāṃ praṇeṣye tattvasaṃhitām
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ tam anubhāṣyātha bhagavān pratyagakṣajaḥ
BhP jagāma bindusarasaḥ sarasvatyā pariśritāt
BhP nirīkṣatas tasya yayāv aśeṣa siddheśvarābhiṣṭutasiddhamārgaḥ
BhP ākarṇayan patrarathendrapakṣair uccāritaṃ stomam udīrṇasāma
BhP atha samprasthite śukle kardamo bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
BhP āste sma bindusarasi taṃ kālaṃ pratipālayan
BhP manuḥ syandanam āsthāya śātakaumbhaparicchadam
BhP āropya svāṃ duhitaraṃ sabhāryaḥ paryaṭan mahīm
BhP tasmin sudhanvann ahani bhagavān yat samādiśat
BhP upāyād āśramapadaṃ muneḥ śāntavratasya tat
BhP yasmin bhagavato netrān nyapatann aśrubindavaḥ
BhP kṛpayā samparītasya prapanne 'rpitayā bhṛśam
BhP tad vai bindusaro nāma sarasvatyā pariplutam
BhP puṇyaṃ śivāmṛtajalaṃ maharṣigaṇasevitam
BhP puṇyadrumalatājālaiḥ kūjatpuṇyamṛgadvijaiḥ
BhP sarvartuphalapuṣpāḍhyaṃ vanarājiśriyānvitam
BhP mattadvijagaṇair ghuṣṭaṃ mattabhramaravibhramam
BhP mattabarhinaṭāṭopam āhvayanmattakokilam
BhP kadambacampakāśoka karañjabakulāsanaiḥ
BhP kundamandārakuṭajaiś cūtapotair alaṅkṛtam
BhP kāraṇḍavaiḥ plavair haṃsaiḥ kurarair jalakukkuṭaiḥ
BhP sārasaiś cakravākaiś ca cakorair valgu kūjitam
BhP tathaiva hariṇaiḥ kroḍaiḥ śvāvidgavayakuñjaraiḥ
BhP gopucchair haribhir markair nakulair nābhibhir vṛtam
BhP praviśya tat tīrthavaram ādirājaḥ sahātmajaḥ
BhP dadarśa munim āsīnaṃ tasmin hutahutāśanam
BhP vidyotamānaṃ vapuṣā tapasy ugrayujā ciram
BhP nātikṣāmaṃ bhagavataḥ snigdhāpāṅgāvalokanāt
BhP tadvyāhṛtāmṛtakalā pīyūṣaśravaṇena ca
BhP prāṃśuṃ padmapalāśākṣaṃ jaṭilaṃ cīravāsasam
BhP upasaṃśritya malinaṃ yathārhaṇam asaṃskṛtam
BhP athoṭajam upāyātaṃ nṛdevaṃ praṇataṃ puraḥ
BhP saparyayā paryagṛhṇāt pratinandyānurūpayā
BhP gṛhītārhaṇam āsīnaṃ saṃyataṃ prīṇayan muniḥ
BhP smaran bhagavadādeśam ity āha ślakṣṇayā girā
BhP nūnaṃ caṅkramaṇaṃ deva satāṃ saṃrakṣaṇāya te
BhP vadhāya cāsatāṃ yas tvaṃ hareḥ śaktir hi pālinī
BhP yo 'rkendvagnīndravāyūnāṃ yamadharmapracetasām
BhP rūpāṇi sthāna ādhatse tasmai śuklāya te namaḥ
BhP na yadā ratham āsthāya jaitraṃ maṇigaṇārpitam
BhP visphūrjaccaṇḍakodaṇḍo rathena trāsayann aghān
BhP svasainyacaraṇakṣuṇṇaṃ vepayan maṇḍalaṃ bhuvaḥ
BhP vikarṣan bṛhatīṃ senāṃ paryaṭasy aṃśumān iva
BhP tadaiva setavaḥ sarve varṇāśramanibandhanāḥ
BhP bhagavadracitā rājan bhidyeran bata dasyubhiḥ
BhP adharmaś ca samedheta lolupair vyaṅkuśair nṛbhiḥ
BhP śayāne tvayi loko 'yaṃ dasyugrasto vinaṅkṣyati
BhP athāpi pṛcche tvāṃ vīra yadarthaṃ tvam ihāgataḥ
BhP tad vayaṃ nirvyalīkena pratipadyāmahe hṛdā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evam āviṣkṛtāśeṣa guṇakarmodayo munim
BhP savrīḍa iva taṃ samrāḍ upāratam uvāca ha
BhP manur uvāca
BhP brahmāsṛjat svamukhato yuṣmān ātmaparīpsayā
BhP chandomayas tapovidyā yogayuktān alampaṭān
BhP tattrāṇāyāsṛjac cāsmān doḥsahasrāt sahasrapāt
BhP hṛdayaṃ tasya hi brahma kṣatram aṅgaṃ pracakṣate
BhP ato hy anyonyam ātmānaṃ brahma kṣatraṃ ca rakṣataḥ
BhP rakṣati smāvyayo devaḥ sa yaḥ sadasadātmakaḥ
BhP tava sandarśanād eva cchinnā me sarvasaṃśayāḥ
BhP yat svayaṃ bhagavān prītyā dharmam āha rirakṣiṣoḥ
BhP diṣṭyā me bhagavān dṛṣṭo durdarśo yo 'kṛtātmanām
BhP diṣṭyā pādarajaḥ spṛṣṭaṃ śīrṣṇā me bhavataḥ śivam
BhP diṣṭyā tvayānuśiṣṭo 'haṃ kṛtaś cānugraho mahān
BhP apāvṛtaiḥ karṇarandhrair juṣṭā diṣṭyośatīr giraḥ
BhP sa bhavān duhitṛsneha parikliṣṭātmano mama
BhP śrotum arhasi dīnasya śrāvitaṃ kṛpayā mune
BhP priyavratottānapadoḥ svaseyaṃ duhitā mama
BhP anvicchati patiṃ yuktaṃ vayaḥśīlaguṇādibhiḥ
BhP yadā tu bhavataḥ śīla śrutarūpavayoguṇān
BhP aśṛṇon nāradād eṣā tvayy āsīt kṛtaniścayā
BhP tat pratīccha dvijāgryemāṃ śraddhayopahṛtāṃ mayā
BhP sarvātmanānurūpāṃ te gṛhamedhiṣu karmasu
BhP udyatasya hi kāmasya prativādo na śasyate
BhP api nirmuktasaṅgasya kāmaraktasya kiṃ punaḥ
BhP ya udyatam anādṛtya kīnāśam abhiyācate
BhP kṣīyate tadyaśaḥ sphītaṃ mānaś cāvajñayā hataḥ
BhP ahaṃ tvāśṛṇavaṃ vidvan vivāhārthaṃ samudyatam
BhP atas tvam upakurvāṇaḥ prattāṃ pratigṛhāṇa me
BhP ṛṣir uvāca
BhP bāḍham udvoḍhukāmo 'ham aprattā ca tavātmajā
BhP āvayor anurūpo 'sāv ādyo vaivāhiko vidhiḥ
BhP kāmaḥ sa bhūyān naradeva te 'syāḥ putryāḥ samāmnāyavidhau pratītaḥ
BhP ka eva te tanayāṃ nādriyeta svayaiva kāntyā kṣipatīm iva śriyam
BhP yāṃ harmyapṛṣṭhe kvaṇadaṅghriśobhāṃ vikrīḍatīṃ kandukavihvalākṣīm
BhP viśvāvasur nyapatat svād vimānād vilokya sammohavimūḍhacetāḥ
BhP tāṃ prārthayantīṃ lalanālalāmam asevitaśrīcaraṇair adṛṣṭām
BhP vatsāṃ manor uccapadaḥ svasāraṃ ko nānumanyeta budho 'bhiyātām
BhP ato bhajiṣye samayena sādhvīṃ yāvat tejo bibhṛyād ātmano me
BhP ato dharmān pāramahaṃsyamukhyān śuklaproktān bahu manye 'vihiṃsrān
BhP yato 'bhavad viśvam idaṃ vicitraṃ saṃsthāsyate yatra ca vāvatiṣṭhate
BhP prajāpatīnāṃ patir eṣa mahyaṃ paraṃ pramāṇaṃ bhagavān anantaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sa ugradhanvann iyad evābabhāṣe āsīc ca tūṣṇīm aravindanābham
BhP dhiyopagṛhṇan smitaśobhitena mukhena ceto lulubhe devahūtyāḥ
BhP so 'nu jñātvā vyavasitaṃ mahiṣyā duhituḥ sphuṭam
BhP tasmai guṇagaṇāḍhyāya dadau tulyāṃ praharṣitaḥ
BhP śatarūpā mahārājñī pāribarhān mahādhanān
BhP dampatyoḥ paryadāt prītyā bhūṣāvāsaḥ paricchadān
BhP prattāṃ duhitaraṃ samrāṭ sadṛkṣāya gatavyathaḥ
BhP upaguhya ca bāhubhyām autkaṇṭhyonmathitāśayaḥ
BhP aśaknuvaṃs tadvirahaṃ muñcan bāṣpakalāṃ muhuḥ
BhP āsiñcad amba vatseti netrodair duhituḥ śikhāḥ
BhP āmantrya taṃ munivaram anujñātaḥ sahānugaḥ
BhP pratasthe ratham āruhya sabhāryaḥ svapuraṃ nṛpaḥ
BhP ubhayor ṛṣikulyāyāḥ sarasvatyāḥ surodhasoḥ
BhP ṛṣīṇām upaśāntānāṃ paśyann āśramasampadaḥ
BhP tam āyāntam abhipretya brahmāvartāt prajāḥ patim
BhP gītasaṃstutivāditraiḥ pratyudīyuḥ praharṣitāḥ
BhP barhiṣmatī nāma purī sarvasampatsamanvitā
BhP nyapatan yatra romāṇi yajñasyāṅgaṃ vidhunvataḥ
BhP kuśāḥ kāśās ta evāsan śaśvaddharitavarcasaḥ
BhP ṛṣayo yaiḥ parābhāvya yajñaghnān yajñam ījire
BhP kuśakāśamayaṃ barhir āstīrya bhagavān manuḥ
BhP ayajad yajñapuruṣaṃ labdhā sthānaṃ yato bhuvam
BhP barhiṣmatīṃ nāma vibhur yāṃ nirviśya samāvasat
BhP tasyāṃ praviṣṭo bhavanaṃ tāpatrayavināśanam
BhP sabhāryaḥ saprajaḥ kāmān bubhuje 'nyāvirodhataḥ
BhP saṅgīyamānasatkīrtiḥ sastrībhiḥ suragāyakaiḥ
BhP pratyūṣeṣv anubaddhena hṛdā śṛṇvan hareḥ kathāḥ
BhP niṣṇātaṃ yogamāyāsu muniṃ svāyambhuvaṃ manum
BhP yad ābhraṃśayituṃ bhogā na śekur bhagavatparam
BhP ayātayāmās tasyāsan yāmāḥ svāntarayāpanāḥ
BhP śṛṇvato dhyāyato viṣṇoḥ kurvato bruvataḥ kathāḥ
BhP sa evaṃ svāntaraṃ ninye yugānām ekasaptatim
BhP vāsudevaprasaṅgena paribhūtagatitrayaḥ
BhP śārīrā mānasā divyā vaiyāse ye ca mānuṣāḥ
BhP bhautikāś ca kathaṃ kleśā bādhante harisaṃśrayam
BhP yaḥ pṛṣṭo munibhiḥ prāha dharmān nānāvidhān chubhān
BhP nṛṇāṃ varṇāśramāṇāṃ ca sarvabhūtahitaḥ sadā
BhP etat ta ādirājasya manoś caritam adbhutam
BhP varṇitaṃ varṇanīyasya tadapatyodayaṃ śṛṇu
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP pitṛbhyāṃ prasthite sādhvī patim iṅgitakovidā
BhP nityaṃ paryacarat prītyā bhavānīva bhavaṃ prabhum
BhP viśrambheṇātmaśaucena gauraveṇa damena ca
BhP śuśrūṣayā sauhṛdena vācā madhurayā ca bhoḥ
BhP visṛjya kāmaṃ dambhaṃ ca dveṣaṃ lobham aghaṃ madam
BhP apramattodyatā nityaṃ tejīyāṃsam atoṣayat
BhP sa vai devarṣivaryas tāṃ mānavīṃ samanuvratām
BhP daivād garīyasaḥ patyur āśāsānāṃ mahāśiṣaḥ
BhP kālena bhūyasā kṣāmāṃ karśitāṃ vratacaryayā
BhP premagadgadayā vācā pīḍitaḥ kṛpayābravīt
BhP kardama uvāca
BhP tuṣṭo 'ham adya tava mānavi mānadāyāḥ
BhP śuśrūṣayā paramayā parayā ca bhaktyā
BhP yo dehinām ayam atīva suhṛt sa deho
BhP nāvekṣitaḥ samucitaḥ kṣapituṃ madarthe
BhP ye me svadharmaniratasya tapaḥsamādhi
BhP vidyātmayogavijitā bhagavatprasādāḥ
BhP tān eva te madanusevanayāvaruddhān
BhP dṛṣṭiṃ prapaśya vitarāmy abhayān aśokān
BhP anye punar bhagavato bhruva udvijṛmbha
BhP vibhraṃśitārtharacanāḥ kim urukramasya
BhP siddhāsi bhuṅkṣva vibhavān nijadharmadohān
BhP divyān narair duradhigān nṛpavikriyābhiḥ
BhP evaṃ bruvāṇam abalākhilayogamāyā
BhP vidyāvicakṣaṇam avekṣya gatādhir āsīt
BhP sampraśrayapraṇayavihvalayā gireṣad
BhP vrīḍāvalokavilasaddhasitānanāha
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP rāddhaṃ bata dvijavṛṣaitad amoghayoga
BhP māyādhipe tvayi vibho tad avaimi bhartaḥ
BhP yas te 'bhyadhāyi samayaḥ sakṛd aṅgasaṅgo
BhP bhūyād garīyasi guṇaḥ prasavaḥ satīnām
BhP tatretikṛtyam upaśikṣa yathopadeśaṃ
BhP yenaiṣa me karśito 'tiriraṃsayātmā
BhP siddhyeta te kṛtamanobhavadharṣitāyā
BhP dīnas tad īśa bhavanaṃ sadṛśaṃ vicakṣva
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP priyāyāḥ priyam anvicchan kardamo yogam āsthitaḥ
BhP vimānaṃ kāmagaṃ kṣattas tarhy evāviracīkarat
BhP sarvakāmadughaṃ divyaṃ sarvaratnasamanvitam
BhP sarvarddhyupacayodarkaṃ maṇistambhair upaskṛtam
BhP divyopakaraṇopetaṃ sarvakālasukhāvaham
BhP paṭṭikābhiḥ patākābhir vicitrābhir alaṅkṛtam
BhP sragbhir vicitramālyābhir mañjuśiñjatṣaḍaṅghribhiḥ
BhP dukūlakṣaumakauśeyair nānāvastrair virājitam
BhP upary upari vinyasta nilayeṣu pṛthak pṛthak
BhP kṣiptaiḥ kaśipubhiḥ kāntaṃ paryaṅkavyajanāsanaiḥ
BhP tatra tatra vinikṣipta nānāśilpopaśobhitam
BhP mahāmarakatasthalyā juṣṭaṃ vidrumavedibhiḥ
BhP dvāḥsu vidrumadehalyā bhātaṃ vajrakapāṭavat
BhP śikhareṣv indranīleṣu hemakumbhair adhiśritam
BhP cakṣuṣmat padmarāgāgryair vajrabhittiṣu nirmitaiḥ
BhP juṣṭaṃ vicitravaitānair mahārhair hematoraṇaiḥ
BhP haṃsapārāvatavrātais tatra tatra nikūjitam
BhP kṛtrimān manyamānaiḥ svān adhiruhyādhiruhya ca
BhP vihārasthānaviśrāma saṃveśaprāṅgaṇājiraiḥ
BhP yathopajoṣaṃ racitair vismāpanam ivātmanaḥ
BhP īdṛg gṛhaṃ tat paśyantīṃ nātiprītena cetasā
BhP sarvabhūtāśayābhijñaḥ prāvocat kardamaḥ svayam
BhP nimajjyāsmin hrade bhīru vimānam idam āruha
BhP idaṃ śuklakṛtaṃ tīrtham āśiṣāṃ yāpakaṃ nṛṇām
BhP sā tad bhartuḥ samādāya vacaḥ kuvalayekṣaṇā
BhP sarajaṃ bibhratī vāso veṇībhūtāṃś ca mūrdhajān
BhP aṅgaṃ ca malapaṅkena sañchannaṃ śabalastanam
BhP āviveśa sarasvatyāḥ saraḥ śivajalāśayam
BhP sāntaḥ sarasi veśmasthāḥ śatāni daśa kanyakāḥ
BhP sarvāḥ kiśoravayaso dadarśotpalagandhayaḥ
BhP tāṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya procuḥ prāñjalayaḥ striyaḥ
BhP vayaṃ karmakarīs tubhyaṃ śādhi naḥ karavāma kim
BhP snānena tāṃ mahārheṇa snāpayitvā manasvinīm
BhP dukūle nirmale nūtne dadur asyai ca mānadāḥ
BhP bhūṣaṇāni parārdhyāni varīyāṃsi dyumanti ca
BhP annaṃ sarvaguṇopetaṃ pānaṃ caivāmṛtāsavam
BhP athādarśe svam ātmānaṃ sragviṇaṃ virajāmbaram
BhP virajaṃ kṛtasvastyayanaṃ kanyābhir bahumānitam
BhP snātaṃ kṛtaśiraḥsnānaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
BhP niṣkagrīvaṃ valayinaṃ kūjatkāñcananūpuram
BhP śroṇyor adhyastayā kāñcyā kāñcanyā bahuratnayā
BhP hāreṇa ca mahārheṇa rucakena ca bhūṣitam
BhP sudatā subhruvā ślakṣṇa snigdhāpāṅgena cakṣuṣā
BhP padmakośaspṛdhā nīlair alakaiś ca lasanmukham
BhP yadā sasmāra ṛṣabham ṛṣīṇāṃ dayitaṃ patim
BhP tatra cāste saha strībhir yatrāste sa prajāpatiḥ
BhP bhartuḥ purastād ātmānaṃ strīsahasravṛtaṃ tadā
BhP niśāmya tadyogagatiṃ saṃśayaṃ pratyapadyata
BhP sa tāṃ kṛtamalasnānāṃ vibhrājantīm apūrvavat
BhP ātmano bibhratīṃ rūpaṃ saṃvītarucirastanīm
BhP vidyādharīsahasreṇa sevyamānāṃ suvāsasam
BhP jātabhāvo vimānaṃ tad ārohayad amitrahan
BhP tasminn aluptamahimā priyayānurakto
BhP vidyādharībhir upacīrṇavapur vimāne
BhP babhrāja utkacakumudgaṇavān apīcyas
BhP tārābhir āvṛta ivoḍupatir nabhaḥsthaḥ
BhP tenāṣṭalokapavihārakulācalendra
BhP droṇīṣv anaṅgasakhamārutasaubhagāsu
BhP siddhair nuto dyudhunipātaśivasvanāsu
BhP reme ciraṃ dhanadavallalanāvarūthī
BhP vaiśrambhake surasane nandane puṣpabhadrake
BhP mānase caitrarathye ca sa reme rāmayā rataḥ
BhP bhrājiṣṇunā vimānena kāmagena mahīyasā
BhP vaimānikān atyaśeta caral lokān yathānilaḥ
BhP kiṃ durāpādanaṃ teṣāṃ puṃsām uddāmacetasām
BhP yair āśritas tīrthapadaś caraṇo vyasanātyayaḥ
BhP prekṣayitvā bhuvo golaṃ patnyai yāvān svasaṃsthayā
BhP bahvāścaryaṃ mahāyogī svāśramāya nyavartata
BhP vibhajya navadhātmānaṃ mānavīṃ suratotsukām
BhP rāmāṃ niramayan reme varṣapūgān muhūrtavat
BhP tasmin vimāna utkṛṣṭāṃ śayyāṃ ratikarīṃ śritā
BhP na cābudhyata taṃ kālaṃ patyāpīcyena saṅgatā
BhP evaṃ yogānubhāvena dampatyo ramamāṇayoḥ
BhP śataṃ vyatīyuḥ śaradaḥ kāmalālasayor manāk
BhP tasyām ādhatta retas tāṃ bhāvayann ātmanātmavit
BhP nodhā vidhāya rūpaṃ svaṃ sarvasaṅkalpavid vibhuḥ
BhP ataḥ sā suṣuve sadyo devahūtiḥ striyaḥ prajāḥ
BhP sarvās tāś cārusarvāṅgyo lohitotpalagandhayaḥ
BhP patiṃ sā pravrajiṣyantaṃ tadālakṣyośatī bahiḥ
BhP smayamānā viklavena hṛdayena vidūyatā
BhP likhanty adhomukhī bhūmiṃ padā nakhamaṇiśriyā
BhP uvāca lalitāṃ vācaṃ nirudhyāśrukalāṃ śanaiḥ
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP sarvaṃ tad bhagavān mahyam upovāha pratiśrutam
BhP athāpi me prapannāyā abhayaṃ dātum arhasi
BhP brahman duhitṛbhis tubhyaṃ vimṛgyāḥ patayaḥ samāḥ
BhP kaścit syān me viśokāya tvayi pravrajite vanam
BhP etāvatālaṃ kālena vyatikrāntena me prabho
BhP indriyārthaprasaṅgena parityaktaparātmanaḥ
BhP indriyārtheṣu sajjantyā prasaṅgas tvayi me kṛtaḥ
BhP ajānantyā paraṃ bhāvaṃ tathāpy astv abhayāya me
BhP saṅgo yaḥ saṃsṛter hetur asatsu vihito 'dhiyā
BhP sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto niḥsaṅgatvāya kalpate
BhP neha yat karma dharmāya na virāgāya kalpate
BhP na tīrthapadasevāyai jīvann api mṛto hi saḥ
BhP sāhaṃ bhagavato nūnaṃ vañcitā māyayā dṛḍham
BhP yat tvāṃ vimuktidaṃ prāpya na mumukṣeya bandhanāt
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP nirvedavādinīm evaṃ manor duhitaraṃ muniḥ
BhP dayāluḥ śālinīm āha śuklābhivyāhṛtaṃ smaran
BhP ṛṣir uvāca
BhP mā khido rājaputrīttham ātmānaṃ praty anindite
BhP bhagavāṃs te 'kṣaro garbham adūrāt samprapatsyate
BhP dhṛtavratāsi bhadraṃ te damena niyamena ca
BhP tapodraviṇadānaiś ca śraddhayā ceśvaraṃ bhaja
BhP sa tvayārādhitaḥ śuklo vitanvan māmakaṃ yaśaḥ
BhP chettā te hṛdayagranthim audaryo brahmabhāvanaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP devahūty api sandeśaṃ gauraveṇa prajāpateḥ
BhP samyak śraddhāya puruṣaṃ kūṭastham abhajad gurum
BhP tasyāṃ bahutithe kāle bhagavān madhusūdanaḥ
BhP kārdamaṃ vīryam āpanno jajñe 'gnir iva dāruṇi
BhP avādayaṃs tadā vyomni vāditrāṇi ghanāghanāḥ
BhP gāyanti taṃ sma gandharvā nṛtyanty apsaraso mudā
BhP petuḥ sumanaso divyāḥ khecarair apavarjitāḥ
BhP praseduś ca diśaḥ sarvā ambhāṃsi ca manāṃsi ca
BhP tat kardamāśramapadaṃ sarasvatyā pariśritam
BhP svayambhūḥ sākam ṛṣibhir marīcyādibhir abhyayāt
BhP bhagavantaṃ paraṃ brahma sattvenāṃśena śatruhan
BhP tattvasaṅkhyānavijñaptyai jātaṃ vidvān ajaḥ svarāṭ
BhP sabhājayan viśuddhena cetasā taccikīrṣitam
BhP prahṛṣyamāṇair asubhiḥ kardamaṃ cedam abhyadhāt
BhP brahmovāca
BhP tvayā me 'pacitis tāta kalpitā nirvyalīkataḥ
BhP yan me sañjagṛhe vākyaṃ bhavān mānada mānayan
BhP etāvaty eva śuśrūṣā kāryā pitari putrakaiḥ
BhP bāḍham ity anumanyeta gauraveṇa guror vacaḥ
BhP imā duhitaraḥ satyas tava vatsa sumadhyamāḥ
BhP sargam etaṃ prabhāvaiḥ svair bṛṃhayiṣyanty anekadhā
BhP atas tvam ṛṣimukhyebhyo yathāśīlaṃ yathāruci
BhP ātmajāḥ paridehy adya vistṛṇīhi yaśo bhuvi
BhP vedāham ādyaṃ puruṣam avatīrṇaṃ svamāyayā
BhP bhūtānāṃ śevadhiṃ dehaṃ bibhrāṇaṃ kapilaṃ mune
BhP jñānavijñānayogena karmaṇām uddharan jaṭāḥ
BhP hiraṇyakeśaḥ padmākṣaḥ padmamudrāpadāmbujaḥ
BhP eṣa mānavi te garbhaṃ praviṣṭaḥ kaiṭabhārdanaḥ
BhP avidyāsaṃśayagranthiṃ chittvā gāṃ vicariṣyati
BhP ayaṃ siddhagaṇādhīśaḥ sāṅkhyācāryaiḥ susammataḥ
BhP loke kapila ity ākhyāṃ gantā te kīrtivardhanaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP tāv āśvāsya jagatsraṣṭā kumāraiḥ sahanāradaḥ
BhP haṃso haṃsena yānena tridhāmaparamaṃ yayau
BhP gate śatadhṛtau kṣattaḥ kardamas tena coditaḥ
BhP yathoditaṃ svaduhitḥ prādād viśvasṛjāṃ tataḥ
BhP marīcaye kalāṃ prādād anasūyām athātraye
BhP śraddhām aṅgirase 'yacchat pulastyāya havirbhuvam
BhP pulahāya gatiṃ yuktāṃ kratave ca kriyāṃ satīm
BhP khyātiṃ ca bhṛgave 'yacchad vasiṣṭhāyāpy arundhatīm
BhP atharvaṇe 'dadāc chāntiṃ yayā yajño vitanyate
BhP viprarṣabhān kṛtodvāhān sadārān samalālayat
BhP tatas ta ṛṣayaḥ kṣattaḥ kṛtadārā nimantrya tam
BhP prātiṣṭhan nandim āpannāḥ svaṃ svam āśramamaṇḍalam
BhP sa cāvatīrṇaṃ triyugam ājñāya vibudharṣabham
BhP vivikta upasaṅgamya praṇamya samabhāṣata
BhP aho pāpacyamānānāṃ niraye svair amaṅgalaiḥ
BhP kālena bhūyasā nūnaṃ prasīdantīha devatāḥ
BhP bahujanmavipakvena samyagyogasamādhinā
BhP draṣṭuṃ yatante yatayaḥ śūnyāgāreṣu yatpadam
BhP sa eva bhagavān adya helanaṃ na gaṇayya naḥ
BhP gṛheṣu jāto grāmyāṇāṃ yaḥ svānāṃ pakṣapoṣaṇaḥ
BhP svīyaṃ vākyam ṛtaṃ kartum avatīrṇo 'si me gṛhe
BhP cikīrṣur bhagavān jñānaṃ bhaktānāṃ mānavardhanaḥ
BhP tāny eva te 'bhirūpāṇi rūpāṇi bhagavaṃs tava
BhP yāni yāni ca rocante svajanānām arūpiṇaḥ
BhP tvāṃ sūribhis tattvabubhutsayāddhā sadābhivādārhaṇapādapīṭham
BhP aiśvaryavairāgyayaśo'vabodha vīryaśriyā pūrtam ahaṃ prapadye
BhP paraṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāntaṃ kālaṃ kaviṃ trivṛtaṃ lokapālam
BhP ātmānubhūtyānugataprapañcaṃ svacchandaśaktiṃ kapilaṃ prapadye
BhP a smābhipṛcche 'dya patiṃ prajānāṃ tvayāvatīrṇarṇa utāptakāmaḥ
BhP parivrajatpadavīm āsthito 'haṃ cariṣye tvāṃ hṛdi yuñjan viśokaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP mayā proktaṃ hi lokasya pramāṇaṃ satyalaukike
BhP athājani mayā tubhyaṃ yad avocam ṛtaṃ mune
BhP etan me janma loke 'smin mumukṣūṇāṃ durāśayāt
BhP prasaṅkhyānāya tattvānāṃ sammatāyātmadarśane
BhP eṣa ātmapatho 'vyakto naṣṭaḥ kālena bhūyasā
BhP taṃ pravartayituṃ deham imaṃ viddhi mayā bhṛtam
BhP gaccha kāmaṃ mayāpṛṣṭo mayi sannyastakarmaṇā
BhP jitvā sudurjayaṃ mṛtyum amṛtatvāya māṃ bhaja
BhP mām ātmānaṃ svayaṃjyotiḥ sarvabhūtaguhāśayam
BhP ātmany evātmanā vīkṣya viśoko 'bhayam ṛcchasi
BhP mātra ādhyātmikīṃ vidyāṃ śamanīṃ sarvakarmaṇām
BhP vitariṣye yayā cāsau bhayaṃ cātitariṣyati
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ samuditas tena kapilena prajāpatiḥ
BhP dakṣiṇīkṛtya taṃ prīto vanam eva jagāma ha
BhP vrataṃ sa āsthito maunam ātmaikaśaraṇo muniḥ
BhP niḥsaṅgo vyacarat kṣoṇīm anagnir aniketanaḥ
BhP mano brahmaṇi yuñjāno yat tat sadasataḥ param
BhP guṇāvabhāse viguṇa ekabhaktyānubhāvite
BhP nirahaṅkṛtir nirmamaś ca nirdvandvaḥ samadṛk svadṛk
BhP pratyakpraśāntadhīr dhīraḥ praśāntormir ivodadhiḥ
BhP vāsudeve bhagavati sarvajñe pratyagātmani
BhP pareṇa bhaktibhāvena labdhātmā muktabandhanaḥ
BhP ātmānaṃ sarvabhūteṣu bhagavantam avasthitam
BhP apaśyat sarvabhūtāni bhagavaty api cātmani
BhP icchādveṣavihīnena sarvatra samacetasā
BhP bhagavadbhaktiyuktena prāptā bhāgavatī gatiḥ
BhP śaunaka uvāca
BhP kapilas tattvasaṅkhyātā bhagavān ātmamāyayā
BhP jātaḥ svayam ajaḥ sākṣād ātmaprajñaptaye nṛṇām
BhP na hy asya varṣmaṇaḥ puṃsāṃ varimṇaḥ sarvayoginām
BhP viśrutau śrutadevasya bhūri tṛpyanti me 'savaḥ
BhP yad yad vidhatte bhagavān svacchandātmātmamāyayā
BhP tāni me śraddadhānasya kīrtanyāny anukīrtaya
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP dvaipāyanasakhas tv evaṃ maitreyo bhagavāṃs tathā
BhP prāhedaṃ viduraṃ prīta ānvīkṣikyāṃ pracoditaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP pitari prasthite 'raṇyaṃ mātuḥ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP tasmin bindusare 'vātsīd bhagavān kapilaḥ kila
BhP tam āsīnam akarmāṇaṃ tattvamārgāgradarśanam
BhP svasutaṃ devahūty āha dhātuḥ saṃsmaratī vacaḥ
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP nirviṇṇā nitarāṃ bhūmann asadindriyatarṣaṇāt
BhP yena sambhāvyamānena prapannāndhaṃ tamaḥ prabho
BhP tasya tvaṃ tamaso 'ndhasya duṣpārasyādya pāragam
BhP saccakṣur janmanām ante labdhaṃ me tvadanugrahāt
BhP ya ādyo bhagavān puṃsām īśvaro vai bhavān kila
BhP lokasya tamasāndhasya cakṣuḥ sūrya ivoditaḥ
BhP atha me deva sammoham apākraṣṭuṃ tvam arhasi
BhP yo 'vagraho 'haṃ mametīty etasmin yojitas tvayā
BhP taṃ tvā gatāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ śaraṇyaṃ svabhṛtyasaṃsārataroḥ kuṭhāram
BhP jijñāsayāhaṃ prakṛteḥ pūruṣasya namāmi saddharmavidāṃ variṣṭham
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti svamātur niravadyam īpsitaṃ niśamya puṃsām apavargavardhanam
BhP dhiyābhinandyātmavatāṃ satāṃ gatir babhāṣa īṣatsmitaśobhitānanaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP yoga ādhyātmikaḥ puṃsāṃ mato niḥśreyasāya me
BhP atyantoparatir yatra duḥkhasya ca sukhasya ca
BhP tam imaṃ te pravakṣyāmi yam avocaṃ purānaghe
BhP ṛṣīṇāṃ śrotukāmānāṃ yogaṃ sarvāṅganaipuṇam
BhP cetaḥ khalv asya bandhāya muktaye cātmano matam
BhP guṇeṣu saktaṃ bandhāya rataṃ vā puṃsi muktaye
BhP ahaṃ mamābhimānotthaiḥ kāmalobhādibhir malaiḥ
BhP vītaṃ yadā manaḥ śuddham aduḥkham asukhaṃ samam
BhP tadā puruṣa ātmānaṃ kevalaṃ prakṛteḥ param
BhP nirantaraṃ svayaṃjyotir aṇimānam akhaṇḍitam
BhP jñānavairāgyayuktena bhaktiyuktena cātmanā
BhP paripaśyaty udāsīnaṃ prakṛtiṃ ca hataujasam
BhP na yujyamānayā bhaktyā bhagavaty akhilātmani
BhP sadṛśo 'sti śivaḥ panthā yogināṃ brahmasiddhaye
BhP prasaṅgam ajaraṃ pāśam ātmanaḥ kavayo viduḥ
BhP sa eva sādhuṣu kṛto mokṣadvāram apāvṛtam
BhP titikṣavaḥ kāruṇikāḥ suhṛdaḥ sarvadehinām
BhP ajātaśatravaḥ śāntāḥ sādhavaḥ sādhubhūṣaṇāḥ
BhP mayy ananyena bhāvena bhaktiṃ kurvanti ye dṛḍhām
BhP matkṛte tyaktakarmāṇas tyaktasvajanabāndhavāḥ
BhP madāśrayāḥ kathā mṛṣṭāḥ śṛṇvanti kathayanti ca
BhP tapanti vividhās tāpā naitān madgatacetasaḥ
BhP ta ete sādhavaḥ sādhvi sarvasaṅgavivarjitāḥ
BhP saṅgas teṣv atha te prārthyaḥ saṅgadoṣaharā hi te
BhP satāṃ prasaṅgān mama vīryasaṃvido bhavanti hṛtkarṇarasāyanāḥ kathāḥ
BhP tajjoṣaṇād āśv apavargavartmani śraddhā ratir bhaktir anukramiṣyati
BhP bhaktyā pumān jātavirāga aindriyād dṛṣṭaśrutān madracanānucintayā
BhP cittasya yatto grahaṇe yogayukto yatiṣyate ṛjubhir yogamārgaiḥ
BhP asevayāyaṃ prakṛter guṇānāṃ jñānena vairāgyavijṛmbhitena
BhP yogena mayy arpitayā ca bhaktyā māṃ pratyagātmānam ihāvarundhe
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP kācit tvayy ucitā bhaktiḥ kīdṛśī mama gocarā
BhP yayā padaṃ te nirvāṇam añjasānvāśnavā aham
BhP yo yogo bhagavadbāṇo nirvāṇātmaṃs tvayoditaḥ
BhP kīdṛśaḥ kati cāṅgāni yatas tattvāvabodhanam
BhP tad etan me vijānīhi yathāhaṃ mandadhīr hare
BhP sukhaṃ buddhyeya durbodhaṃ yoṣā bhavadanugrahāt
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP viditvārthaṃ kapilo mātur itthaṃ jātasneho yatra tanvābhijātaḥ
BhP tattvāmnāyaṃ yat pravadanti sāṅkhyaṃ provāca vai bhaktivitānayogam
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP devānāṃ guṇaliṅgānām ānuśravikakarmaṇām
BhP sattva evaikamanaso vṛttiḥ svābhāvikī tu yā
BhP animittā bhāgavatī bhaktiḥ siddher garīyasī
BhP jarayaty āśu yā kośaṃ nigīrṇam analo yathā
BhP naikātmatāṃ me spṛhayanti kecin matpādasevābhiratā madīhāḥ
BhP ye 'nyonyato bhāgavatāḥ prasajya sabhājayante mama pauruṣāṇi
BhP paśyanti te me rucirāṇy amba santaḥ prasannavaktrāruṇalocanāni
BhP rūpāṇi divyāni varapradāni sākaṃ vācaṃ spṛhaṇīyāṃ vadanti
BhP tair darśanīyāvayavair udāra vilāsahāsekṣitavāmasūktaiḥ
BhP hṛtātmano hṛtaprāṇāṃś ca bhaktir anicchato me gatim aṇvīṃ prayuṅkte
BhP atho vibhūtiṃ mama māyāvinas tām aiśvaryam aṣṭāṅgam anupravṛttam
BhP śriyaṃ bhāgavatīṃ vāspṛhayanti bhadrāṃ parasya me te 'śnuvate tu loke
BhP na karhicin matparāḥ śāntarūpe naṅkṣyanti no me 'nimiṣo leḍhi hetiḥ
BhP yeṣām ahaṃ priya ātmā sutaś ca sakhā guruḥ suhṛdo daivam iṣṭam
BhP imaṃ lokaṃ tathaivāmum ātmānam ubhayāyinam
BhP ātmānam anu ye ceha ye rāyaḥ paśavo gṛhāḥ
BhP visṛjya sarvān anyāṃś ca mām evaṃ viśvatomukham
BhP bhajanty ananyayā bhaktyā tān mṛtyor atipāraye
BhP nānyatra mad bhagavataḥ pradhānapuruṣeśvarāt
BhP ātmanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ bhayaṃ tīvraṃ nivartate
BhP madbhayād vāti vāto 'yaṃ sūryas tapati madbhayāt
BhP varṣatīndro dahaty agnir mṛtyuś carati madbhayāt
BhP jñānavairāgyayuktena bhaktiyogena yoginaḥ
BhP kṣemāya pādamūlaṃ me praviśanty akutobhayam
BhP etāvān eva loke 'smin puṃsāṃ niḥśreyasodayaḥ
BhP tīvreṇa bhaktiyogena mano mayy arpitaṃ sthiram
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP atha te sampravakṣyāmi tattvānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pṛthak
BhP yad viditvā vimucyeta puruṣaḥ prākṛtair guṇaiḥ
BhP jñānaṃ niḥśreyasārthāya puruṣasyātmadarśanam
BhP yad āhur varṇaye tat te hṛdayagranthibhedanam
BhP anādir ātmā puruṣo nirguṇaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ
BhP pratyagdhāmā svayaṃjyotir viśvaṃ yena samanvitam
BhP sa eṣa prakṛtiṃ sūkṣmāṃ daivīṃ guṇamayīṃ vibhuḥ
BhP yadṛcchayaivopagatām abhyapadyata līlayā
BhP guṇair vicitrāḥ sṛjatīṃ sarūpāḥ prakṛtiṃ prajāḥ
BhP vilokya mumuhe sadyaḥ sa iha jñānagūhayā
BhP evaṃ parābhidhyānena kartṛtvaṃ prakṛteḥ pumān
BhP karmasu kriyamāṇeṣu guṇair ātmani manyate
BhP tad asya saṃsṛtir bandhaḥ pāratantryaṃ ca tatkṛtam
BhP bhavaty akartur īśasya sākṣiṇo nirvṛtātmanaḥ
BhP kāryakāraṇakartṛtve kāraṇaṃ prakṛtiṃ viduḥ
BhP bhoktṛtve sukhaduḥkhānāṃ puruṣaṃ prakṛteḥ param
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP prakṛteḥ puruṣasyāpi lakṣaṇaṃ puruṣottama
BhP brūhi kāraṇayor asya sadasac ca yadātmakam
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP yat tat triguṇam avyaktaṃ nityaṃ sadasadātmakam
BhP pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ prāhur aviśeṣaṃ viśeṣavat
BhP pañcabhiḥ pañcabhir brahma caturbhir daśabhis tathā
BhP etac caturviṃśatikaṃ gaṇaṃ prādhānikaṃ viduḥ
BhP mahābhūtāni pañcaiva bhūr āpo 'gnir marun nabhaḥ
BhP tanmātrāṇi ca tāvanti gandhādīni matāni me
BhP indriyāṇi daśa śrotraṃ tvag dṛg rasananāsikāḥ
BhP vāk karau caraṇau meḍhraṃ pāyur daśama ucyate
BhP mano buddhir ahaṅkāraś cittam ity antarātmakam
BhP caturdhā lakṣyate bhedo vṛttyā lakṣaṇarūpayā
BhP etāvān eva saṅkhyāto brahmaṇaḥ saguṇasya ha
BhP sanniveśo mayā prokto yaḥ kālaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ
BhP prabhāvaṃ pauruṣaṃ prāhuḥ kālam eke yato bhayam
BhP ahaṅkāravimūḍhasya kartuḥ prakṛtim īyuṣaḥ
BhP prakṛter guṇasāmyasya nirviśeṣasya mānavi
BhP ceṣṭā yataḥ sa bhagavān kāla ity upalakṣitaḥ
BhP antaḥ puruṣarūpeṇa kālarūpeṇa yo bahiḥ
BhP samanvety eṣa sattvānāṃ bhagavān ātmamāyayā
BhP daivāt kṣubhitadharmiṇyāṃ svasyāṃ yonau paraḥ pumān
BhP ādhatta vīryaṃ sāsūta mahattattvaṃ hiraṇmayam
BhP viśvam ātmagataṃ vyañjan kūṭastho jagadaṅkuraḥ
BhP svatejasāpibat tīvram ātmaprasvāpanaṃ tamaḥ
BhP yat tat sattvaguṇaṃ svacchaṃ śāntaṃ bhagavataḥ padam
BhP yad āhur vāsudevākhyaṃ cittaṃ tan mahadātmakam
BhP svacchatvam avikāritvaṃ śāntatvam iti cetasaḥ
BhP vṛttibhir lakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yathāpāṃ prakṛtiḥ parā
BhP mahattattvād vikurvāṇād bhagavadvīryasambhavāt
BhP kriyāśaktir ahaṅkāras trividhaḥ samapadyata
BhP vaikārikas taijasaś ca tāmasaś ca yato bhavaḥ
BhP manasaś cendriyāṇāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ mahatām api
BhP sahasraśirasaṃ sākṣād yam anantaṃ pracakṣate
BhP saṅkarṣaṇākhyaṃ puruṣaṃ bhūtendriyamanomayam
BhP kartṛtvaṃ karaṇatvaṃ ca kāryatvaṃ ceti lakṣaṇam
BhP śāntaghoravimūḍhatvam iti vā syād ahaṅkṛteḥ
BhP vaikārikād vikurvāṇān manastattvam ajāyata
BhP yatsaṅkalpavikalpābhyāṃ vartate kāmasambhavaḥ
BhP yad vidur hy aniruddhākhyaṃ hṛṣīkāṇām adhīśvaram
BhP śāradendīvaraśyāmaṃ saṃrādhyaṃ yogibhiḥ śanaiḥ
BhP taijasāt tu vikurvāṇād buddhitattvam abhūt sati
BhP dravyasphuraṇavijñānam indriyāṇām anugrahaḥ
BhP saṃśayo 'tha viparyāso niścayaḥ smṛtir eva ca
BhP svāpa ity ucyate buddher lakṣaṇaṃ vṛttitaḥ pṛthak
BhP taijasānīndriyāṇy eva kriyājñānavibhāgaśaḥ
BhP prāṇasya hi kriyāśaktir buddher vijñānaśaktitā
BhP tāmasāc ca vikurvāṇād bhagavadvīryacoditāt
BhP śabdamātram abhūt tasmān nabhaḥ śrotraṃ tu śabdagam
BhP arthāśrayatvaṃ śabdasya draṣṭur liṅgatvam eva ca
BhP tanmātratvaṃ ca nabhaso lakṣaṇaṃ kavayo viduḥ
BhP bhūtānāṃ chidradātṛtvaṃ bahir antaram eva ca
BhP prāṇendriyātmadhiṣṇyatvaṃ nabhaso vṛttilakṣaṇam
BhP nabhasaḥ śabdatanmātrāt kālagatyā vikurvataḥ
BhP sparśo 'bhavat tato vāyus tvak sparśasya ca saṅgrahaḥ
BhP mṛdutvaṃ kaṭhinatvaṃ ca śaityam uṣṇatvam eva ca
BhP etat sparśasya sparśatvaṃ tanmātratvaṃ nabhasvataḥ
BhP cālanaṃ vyūhanaṃ prāptir netṛtvaṃ dravyaśabdayoḥ
BhP sarvendriyāṇām ātmatvaṃ vāyoḥ karmābhilakṣaṇam
BhP vāyoś ca sparśatanmātrād rūpaṃ daiveritād abhūt
BhP samutthitaṃ tatas tejaś cakṣū rūpopalambhanam
BhP dravyākṛtitvaṃ guṇatā vyaktisaṃsthātvam eva ca
BhP tejastvaṃ tejasaḥ sādhvi rūpamātrasya vṛttayaḥ
BhP dyotanaṃ pacanaṃ pānam adanaṃ himamardanam
BhP tejaso vṛttayas tv etāḥ śoṣaṇaṃ kṣut tṛḍ eva ca
BhP rūpamātrād vikurvāṇāt tejaso daivacoditāt
BhP rasamātram abhūt tasmād ambho jihvā rasagrahaḥ
BhP kaṣāyo madhuras tiktaḥ kaṭv amla iti naikadhā
BhP bhautikānāṃ vikāreṇa rasa eko vibhidyate
BhP kledanaṃ piṇḍanaṃ tṛptiḥ prāṇanāpyāyanondanam
BhP tāpāpanodo bhūyastvam ambhaso vṛttayas tv imāḥ
BhP rasamātrād vikurvāṇād ambhaso daivacoditāt
BhP gandhamātram abhūt tasmāt pṛthvī ghrāṇas tu gandhagaḥ
BhP karambhapūtisaurabhya śāntogrāmlādibhiḥ pṛthak
BhP dravyāvayavavaiṣamyād gandha eko vibhidyate
BhP bhāvanaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sthānaṃ dhāraṇaṃ sadviśeṣaṇam
BhP sarvasattvaguṇodbhedaḥ pṛthivīvṛttilakṣaṇam
BhP nabhoguṇaviśeṣo 'rtho yasya tac chrotram ucyate
BhP vāyor guṇaviśeṣo 'rtho yasya tat sparśanaṃ viduḥ
BhP tejoguṇaviśeṣo 'rtho yasya tac cakṣur ucyate
BhP ambhoguṇaviśeṣo 'rtho yasya tad rasanaṃ viduḥ
BhP bhūmer guṇaviśeṣo 'rtho yasya sa ghrāṇa ucyate
BhP parasya dṛśyate dharmo hy aparasmin samanvayāt
BhP ato viśeṣo bhāvānāṃ bhūmāv evopalakṣyate
BhP etāny asaṃhatya yadā mahadādīni sapta vai
BhP kālakarmaguṇopeto jagadādir upāviśat
BhP tatas tenānuviddhebhyo yuktebhyo 'ṇḍam acetanam
BhP utthitaṃ puruṣo yasmād udatiṣṭhad asau virāṭ
BhP etad aṇḍaṃ viśeṣākhyaṃ kramavṛddhair daśottaraiḥ
BhP toyādibhiḥ parivṛtaṃ pradhānenāvṛtair bahiḥ
BhP yatra lokavitāno 'yaṃ rūpaṃ bhagavato hareḥ
BhP hiraṇmayād aṇḍakośād utthāya salile śayāt
BhP tam āviśya mahādevo bahudhā nirbibheda kham
BhP nirabhidyatāsya prathamaṃ mukhaṃ vāṇī tato 'bhavat
BhP vāṇyā vahnir atho nāse prāṇoto ghrāṇa etayoḥ
BhP ghrāṇād vāyur abhidyetām akṣiṇī cakṣur etayoḥ
BhP tasmāt sūryo nyabhidyetāṃ karṇau śrotraṃ tato diśaḥ
BhP nirbibheda virājas tvag romaśmaśrvādayas tataḥ
BhP tata oṣadhayaś cāsan śiśnaṃ nirbibhide tataḥ
BhP retas tasmād āpa āsan nirabhidyata vai gudam
BhP gudād apāno 'pānāc ca mṛtyur lokabhayaṅkaraḥ
BhP hastau ca nirabhidyetāṃ balaṃ tābhyāṃ tataḥ svarāṭ
BhP pādau ca nirabhidyetāṃ gatis tābhyāṃ tato hariḥ
BhP nāḍyo 'sya nirabhidyanta tābhyo lohitam ābhṛtam
BhP nadyas tataḥ samabhavann udaraṃ nirabhidyata
BhP kṣutpipāse tataḥ syātāṃ samudras tv etayor abhūt
BhP athāsya hṛdayaṃ bhinnaṃ hṛdayān mana utthitam
BhP manasaś candramā jāto buddhir buddher girāṃ patiḥ
BhP ahaṅkāras tato rudraś cittaṃ caityas tato 'bhavat
BhP ete hy abhyutthitā devā naivāsyotthāpane 'śakan
BhP punar āviviśuḥ khāni tam utthāpayituṃ kramāt
BhP vahnir vācā mukhaṃ bheje nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP ghrāṇena nāsike vāyur nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP akṣiṇī cakṣuṣādityo nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP śrotreṇa karṇau ca diśo nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP tvacaṃ romabhir oṣadhyo nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP retasā śiśnam āpas tu nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP gudaṃ mṛtyur apānena nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP hastāv indro balenaiva nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP viṣṇur gatyaiva caraṇau nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP nāḍīr nadyo lohitena nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP kṣuttṛḍbhyām udaraṃ sindhur nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP hṛdayaṃ manasā candro nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP buddhyā brahmāpi hṛdayaṃ nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP rudro 'bhimatyā hṛdayaṃ nodatiṣṭhat tadā virāṭ
BhP cittena hṛdayaṃ caityaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ prāviśad yadā
BhP virāṭ tadaiva puruṣaḥ salilād udatiṣṭhata
BhP yathā prasuptaṃ puruṣaṃ prāṇendriyamanodhiyaḥ
BhP prabhavanti vinā yena notthāpayitum ojasā
BhP tam asmin pratyagātmānaṃ dhiyā yogapravṛttayā
BhP bhaktyā viraktyā jñānena vivicyātmani cintayet
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP prakṛtistho 'pi puruṣo nājyate prākṛtair guṇaiḥ
BhP avikārād akartṛtvān nirguṇatvāj jalārkavat
BhP sa eṣa yarhi prakṛter guṇeṣv abhiviṣajjate
BhP ahaṅkriyāvimūḍhātmā kartāsmīty abhimanyate
BhP tena saṃsārapadavīm avaśo 'bhyety anirvṛtaḥ
BhP prāsaṅgikaiḥ karmadoṣaiḥ sadasanmiśrayoniṣu
BhP arthe hy avidyamāne 'pi saṃsṛtir na nivartate
BhP dhyāyato viṣayān asya svapne 'narthāgamo yathā
BhP ata eva śanaiś cittaṃ prasaktam asatāṃ pathi
BhP bhaktiyogena tīvreṇa viraktyā ca nayed vaśam
BhP yamādibhir yogapathair abhyasañ śraddhayānvitaḥ
BhP mayi bhāvena satyena matkathāśravaṇena ca
BhP sarvabhūtasamatvena nirvaireṇāprasaṅgataḥ
BhP brahmacaryeṇa maunena svadharmeṇa balīyasā
BhP yadṛcchayopalabdhena santuṣṭo mitabhuṅ muniḥ
BhP viviktaśaraṇaḥ śānto maitraḥ karuṇa ātmavān
BhP sānubandhe ca dehe 'sminn akurvann asadāgraham
BhP jñānena dṛṣṭatattvena prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca
BhP nivṛttabuddhyavasthāno dūrībhūtānyadarśanaḥ
BhP upalabhyātmanātmānaṃ cakṣuṣevārkam ātmadṛk
BhP muktaliṅgaṃ sadābhāsam asati pratipadyate
BhP sato bandhum asaccakṣuḥ sarvānusyūtam advayam
BhP yathā jalastha ābhāsaḥ sthalasthenāvadṛśyate
BhP svābhāsena tathā sūryo jalasthena divi sthitaḥ
BhP evaṃ trivṛdahaṅkāro bhūtendriyamanomayaiḥ
BhP svābhāsair lakṣito 'nena sadābhāsena satyadṛk
BhP bhūtasūkṣmendriyamano buddhyādiṣv iha nidrayā
BhP līneṣv asati yas tatra vinidro nirahaṅkriyaḥ
BhP manyamānas tadātmānam anaṣṭo naṣṭavan mṛṣā
BhP naṣṭe 'haṅkaraṇe draṣṭā naṣṭavitta ivāturaḥ
BhP evaṃ pratyavamṛśyāsāv ātmānaṃ pratipadyate
BhP sāhaṅkārasya dravyasya yo 'vasthānam anugrahaḥ
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP puruṣaṃ prakṛtir brahman na vimuñcati karhicit
BhP anyonyāpāśrayatvāc ca nityatvād anayoḥ prabho
BhP yathā gandhasya bhūmeś ca na bhāvo vyatirekataḥ
BhP apāṃ rasasya ca yathā tathā buddheḥ parasya ca
BhP akartuḥ karmabandho 'yaṃ puruṣasya yadāśrayaḥ
BhP guṇeṣu satsu prakṛteḥ kaivalyaṃ teṣv ataḥ katham
BhP kvacit tattvāvamarśena nivṛttaṃ bhayam ulbaṇam
BhP anivṛttanimittatvāt punaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhate
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP animittanimittena svadharmeṇāmalātmanā
BhP tīvrayā mayi bhaktyā ca śrutasambhṛtayā ciram
BhP jñānena dṛṣṭatattvena vairāgyeṇa balīyasā
BhP tapoyuktena yogena tīvreṇātmasamādhinā
BhP prakṛtiḥ puruṣasyeha dahyamānā tv aharniśam
BhP tirobhavitrī śanakair agner yonir ivāraṇiḥ
BhP bhuktabhogā parityaktā dṛṣṭadoṣā ca nityaśaḥ
BhP neśvarasyāśubhaṃ dhatte sve mahimni sthitasya ca
BhP yathā hy apratibuddhasya prasvāpo bahvanarthabhṛt
BhP sa eva pratibuddhasya na vai mohāya kalpate
BhP evaṃ viditatattvasya prakṛtir mayi mānasam
BhP yuñjato nāpakuruta ātmārāmasya karhicit
BhP yadaivam adhyātmarataḥ kālena bahujanmanā
BhP sarvatra jātavairāgya ābrahmabhuvanān muniḥ
BhP madbhaktaḥ pratibuddhārtho matprasādena bhūyasā
BhP niḥśreyasaṃ svasaṃsthānaṃ kaivalyākhyaṃ madāśrayam
BhP prāpnotīhāñjasā dhīraḥ svadṛśā cchinnasaṃśayaḥ
BhP yad gatvā na nivarteta yogī liṅgād vinirgame
BhP yadā na yogopacitāsu ceto māyāsu siddhasya viṣajjate 'ṅga
BhP ananyahetuṣv atha me gatiḥ syād ātyantikī yatra na mṛtyuhāsaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP yogasya lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye sabījasya nṛpātmaje
BhP mano yenaiva vidhinā prasannaṃ yāti satpatham
BhP svadharmācaraṇaṃ śaktyā vidharmāc ca nivartanam
BhP daivāl labdhena santoṣa ātmaviccaraṇārcanam
BhP grāmyadharmanivṛttiś ca mokṣadharmaratis tathā
BhP mitamedhyādanaṃ śaśvad viviktakṣemasevanam
BhP ahiṃsā satyam asteyaṃ yāvadarthaparigrahaḥ
BhP brahmacaryaṃ tapaḥ śaucaṃ svādhyāyaḥ puruṣārcanam
BhP maunaṃ sadāsanajayaḥ sthairyaṃ prāṇajayaḥ śanaiḥ
BhP pratyāhāraś cendriyāṇāṃ viṣayān manasā hṛdi
BhP svadhiṣṇyānām ekadeśe manasā prāṇadhāraṇam
BhP vaikuṇṭhalīlābhidhyānaṃ samādhānaṃ tathātmanaḥ
BhP etair anyaiś ca pathibhir mano duṣṭam asatpatham
BhP buddhyā yuñjīta śanakair jitaprāṇo hy atandritaḥ
BhP śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya vijitāsana āsanam
BhP tasmin svasti samāsīna ṛjukāyaḥ samabhyaset
BhP prāṇasya śodhayen mārgaṃ pūrakumbhakarecakaiḥ
BhP pratikūlena vā cittaṃ yathā sthiram acañcalam
BhP mano 'cirāt syād virajaṃ jitaśvāsasya yoginaḥ
BhP vāyvagnibhyāṃ yathā lohaṃ dhmātaṃ tyajati vai malam
BhP prāṇāyāmair dahed doṣān dhāraṇābhiś ca kilbiṣān
BhP pratyāhāreṇa saṃsargān dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān
BhP yadā manaḥ svaṃ virajaṃ yogena susamāhitam
BhP kāṣṭhāṃ bhagavato dhyāyet svanāsāgrāvalokanaḥ
BhP prasannavadanāmbhojaṃ padmagarbhāruṇekṣaṇam
BhP nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam
BhP lasatpaṅkajakiñjalka pītakauśeyavāsasam
BhP śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ bhrājat kaustubhāmuktakandharam
BhP mattadvirephakalayā parītaṃ vanamālayā
BhP parārdhyahāravalaya kirīṭāṅgadanūpuram
BhP kāñcīguṇollasacchroṇiṃ hṛdayāmbhojaviṣṭaram
BhP darśanīyatamaṃ śāntaṃ manonayanavardhanam
BhP apīcyadarśanaṃ śaśvat sarvalokanamaskṛtam
BhP santaṃ vayasi kaiśore bhṛtyānugrahakātaram
BhP kīrtanyatīrthayaśasaṃ puṇyaślokayaśaskaram
BhP dhyāyed devaṃ samagrāṅgaṃ yāvan na cyavate manaḥ
BhP sthitaṃ vrajantam āsīnaṃ śayānaṃ vā guhāśayam
BhP prekṣaṇīyehitaṃ dhyāyec chuddhabhāvena cetasā
BhP tasmin labdhapadaṃ cittaṃ sarvāvayavasaṃsthitam
BhP vilakṣyaikatra saṃyujyād aṅge bhagavato muniḥ
BhP sañcintayed bhagavataś caraṇāravindaṃ
BhP vajrāṅkuśadhvajasaroruhalāñchanāḍhyam
BhP uttuṅgaraktavilasannakhacakravāla
BhP jyotsnābhir āhatamahaddhṛdayāndhakāram
BhP yacchaucaniḥsṛtasaritpravarodakena
BhP tīrthena mūrdhny adhikṛtena śivaḥ śivo 'bhūt
BhP dhyātur manaḥśamalaśailanisṛṣṭavajraṃ
BhP dhyāyec ciraṃ bhagavataś caraṇāravindam
BhP jānudvayaṃ jalajalocanayā jananyā
BhP lakṣmyākhilasya suravanditayā vidhātuḥ
BhP ūrvor nidhāya karapallavarociṣā yat
BhP saṃlālitaṃ hṛdi vibhor abhavasya kuryāt
BhP ūrū suparṇabhujayor adhi śobhamānāv
BhP ojonidhī atasikākusumāvabhāsau
BhP vyālambipītavaravāsasi vartamāna
BhP kāñcīkalāpaparirambhi nitambabimbam
BhP nābhihradaṃ bhuvanakośaguhodarasthaṃ
BhP yatrātmayonidhiṣaṇākhilalokapadmam
BhP vyūḍhaṃ harinmaṇivṛṣastanayor amuṣya
BhP dhyāyed dvayaṃ viśadahāramayūkhagauram
BhP vakṣo 'dhivāsam ṛṣabhasya mahāvibhūteḥ
BhP puṃsāṃ manonayananirvṛtim ādadhānam
BhP kaṇṭhaṃ ca kaustubhamaṇer adhibhūṣaṇārthaṃ
BhP kuryān manasy akhilalokanamaskṛtasya
BhP bāhūṃś ca mandaragireḥ parivartanena
BhP nirṇiktabāhuvalayān adhilokapālān
BhP sañcintayed daśaśatāram asahyatejaḥ
BhP śaṅkhaṃ ca tatkarasaroruharājahaṃsam
BhP kaumodakīṃ bhagavato dayitāṃ smareta
BhP digdhām arātibhaṭaśoṇitakardamena
BhP mālāṃ madhuvratavarūthagiropaghuṣṭāṃ
BhP caityasya tattvam amalaṃ maṇim asya kaṇṭhe
BhP bhṛtyānukampitadhiyeha gṛhītamūrteḥ
BhP sañcintayed bhagavato vadanāravindam
BhP yad visphuranmakarakuṇḍalavalgitena
BhP vidyotitāmalakapolam udāranāsam
BhP yac chrīniketam alibhiḥ parisevyamānaṃ
BhP bhūtyā svayā kuṭilakuntalavṛndajuṣṭam
BhP mīnadvayāśrayam adhikṣipad abjanetraṃ
BhP dhyāyen manomayam atandrita ullasadbhru
BhP tasyāvalokam adhikaṃ kṛpayātighora
BhP tāpatrayopaśamanāya nisṛṣṭam akṣṇoḥ
BhP snigdhasmitānuguṇitaṃ vipulaprasādaṃ
BhP dhyāyec ciraṃ vipulabhāvanayā guhāyām
BhP hāsaṃ harer avanatākhilalokatīvra
BhP śokāśrusāgaraviśoṣaṇam atyudāram
BhP sammohanāya racitaṃ nijamāyayāsya
BhP bhrūmaṇḍalaṃ munikṛte makaradhvajasya
BhP dhyānāyanaṃ prahasitaṃ bahulādharoṣṭha
BhP bhāsāruṇāyitatanudvijakundapaṅkti
BhP dhyāyet svadehakuhare 'vasitasya viṣṇor
BhP bhaktyārdrayārpitamanā na pṛthag didṛkṣet
BhP evaṃ harau bhagavati pratilabdhabhāvo
BhP bhaktyā dravaddhṛdaya utpulakaḥ pramodāt
BhP autkaṇṭhyabāṣpakalayā muhur ardyamānas
BhP tac cāpi cittabaḍiśaṃ śanakair viyuṅkte
BhP muktāśrayaṃ yarhi nirviṣayaṃ viraktaṃ
BhP nirvāṇam ṛcchati manaḥ sahasā yathārciḥ
BhP ātmānam atra puruṣo 'vyavadhānam ekam
BhP anvīkṣate pratinivṛttaguṇapravāhaḥ
BhP so 'py etayā caramayā manaso nivṛttyā
BhP tasmin mahimny avasitaḥ sukhaduḥkhabāhye
BhP hetutvam apy asati kartari duḥkhayor yat
BhP svātman vidhatta upalabdhaparātmakāṣṭhaḥ
BhP dehaṃ ca taṃ na caramaḥ sthitam utthitaṃ vā
BhP siddho vipaśyati yato 'dhyagamat svarūpam
BhP daivād upetam atha daivavaśād apetaṃ
BhP vāso yathā parikṛtaṃ madirāmadāndhaḥ
BhP deho 'pi daivavaśagaḥ khalu karma yāvat
BhP svārambhakaṃ pratisamīkṣata eva sāsuḥ
BhP taṃ saprapañcam adhirūḍhasamādhiyogaḥ
BhP svāpnaṃ punar na bhajate pratibuddhavastuḥ
BhP yathā putrāc ca vittāc ca pṛthaṅ martyaḥ pratīyate
BhP apy ātmatvenābhimatād dehādeḥ puruṣas tathā
BhP yatholmukād visphuliṅgād dhūmād vāpi svasambhavāt
BhP apy ātmatvenābhimatād yathāgniḥ pṛthag ulmukāt
BhP bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇāt pradhānāj jīvasaṃjñitāt
BhP ātmā tathā pṛthag draṣṭā bhagavān brahmasaṃjñitaḥ
BhP sarvabhūteṣu cātmānaṃ sarvabhūtāni cātmani
BhP īkṣetānanyabhāvena bhūteṣv iva tadātmatām
BhP svayoniṣu yathā jyotir ekaṃ nānā pratīyate

BhP tasmād imāṃ svāṃ prakṛtiṃ daivīṃ sadasadātmikām
BhP durvibhāvyāṃ parābhāvya svarūpeṇāvatiṣṭhate
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP lakṣaṇaṃ mahadādīnāṃ prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca
BhP svarūpaṃ lakṣyate 'mīṣāṃ yena tatpāramārthikam
BhP yathā sāṅkhyeṣu kathitaṃ yanmūlaṃ tat pracakṣate
BhP bhaktiyogasya me mārgaṃ brūhi vistaraśaḥ prabho
BhP virāgo yena puruṣo bhagavan sarvato bhavet
BhP ācakṣva jīvalokasya vividhā mama saṃsṛtīḥ
BhP kālasyeśvararūpasya pareṣāṃ ca parasya te
BhP svarūpaṃ bata kurvanti yaddhetoḥ kuśalaṃ janāḥ
BhP lokasya mithyābhimater acakṣuṣaś ciraṃ prasuptasya tamasy anāśraye
BhP śrāntasya karmasv anuviddhayā dhiyā tvam āvirāsīḥ kila yogabhāskaraḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti mātur vacaḥ ślakṣṇaṃ pratinandya mahāmuniḥ
BhP ābabhāṣe kuruśreṣṭha prītas tāṃ karuṇārditaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP bhaktiyogo bahuvidho mārgair bhāmini bhāvyate
BhP svabhāvaguṇamārgeṇa puṃsāṃ bhāvo vibhidyate
BhP abhisandhāya yo hiṃsāṃ dambhaṃ mātsaryam eva vā
BhP saṃrambhī bhinnadṛg bhāvaṃ mayi kuryāt sa tāmasaḥ
BhP viṣayān abhisandhāya yaśa aiśvaryam eva vā
BhP arcādāv arcayed yo māṃ pṛthagbhāvaḥ sa rājasaḥ
BhP karmanirhāram uddiśya parasmin vā tadarpaṇam
BhP yajed yaṣṭavyam iti vā pṛthagbhāvaḥ sa sāttvikaḥ
BhP madguṇaśrutimātreṇa mayi sarvaguhāśaye
BhP manogatir avicchinnā yathā gaṅgāmbhaso 'mbudhau
BhP lakṣaṇaṃ bhaktiyogasya nirguṇasya hy udāhṛtam
BhP ahaituky avyavahitā yā bhaktiḥ puruṣottame
BhP sālokyasārṣṭisāmīpya sārūpyaikatvam apy uta
BhP dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā matsevanaṃ janāḥ
BhP sa eva bhaktiyogākhya ātyantika udāhṛtaḥ
BhP yenātivrajya triguṇaṃ madbhāvāyopapadyate
BhP niṣevitenānimittena svadharmeṇa mahīyasā
BhP kriyāyogena śastena nātihiṃsreṇa nityaśaḥ
BhP maddhiṣṇyadarśanasparśa pūjāstutyabhivandanaiḥ
BhP bhūteṣu madbhāvanayā sattvenāsaṅgamena ca
BhP mahatāṃ bahumānena dīnānām anukampayā
BhP maitryā caivātmatulyeṣu yamena niyamena ca
BhP ādhyātmikānuśravaṇān nāmasaṅkīrtanāc ca me
BhP ārjavenāryasaṅgena nirahaṅkriyayā tathā
BhP maddharmaṇo guṇair etaiḥ parisaṃśuddha āśayaḥ
BhP puruṣasyāñjasābhyeti śrutamātraguṇaṃ hi mām
BhP yathā vātaratho ghrāṇam āvṛṅkte gandha āśayāt
BhP evaṃ yogarataṃ ceta ātmānam avikāri yat
BhP ahaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu bhūtātmāvasthitaḥ sadā
BhP tam avajñāya māṃ martyaḥ kurute 'rcāviḍambanam
BhP yo māṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu santam ātmānam īśvaram
BhP hitvārcāṃ bhajate mauḍhyād bhasmany eva juhoti saḥ
BhP dviṣataḥ parakāye māṃ mānino bhinnadarśinaḥ
BhP bhūteṣu baddhavairasya na manaḥ śāntim ṛcchati
BhP aham uccāvacair dravyaiḥ kriyayotpannayānaghe
BhP naiva tuṣye 'rcito 'rcāyāṃ bhūtagrāmāvamāninaḥ
BhP arcādāv arcayet tāvad īśvaraṃ māṃ svakarmakṛt
BhP yāvan na veda svahṛdi sarvabhūteṣv avasthitam
BhP ātmanaś ca parasyāpi yaḥ karoty antarodaram
BhP tasya bhinnadṛśo mṛtyur vidadhe bhayam ulbaṇam
BhP atha māṃ sarvabhūteṣu bhūtātmānaṃ kṛtālayam
BhP arhayed dānamānābhyāṃ maitryābhinnena cakṣuṣā
BhP jīvāḥ śreṣṭhā hy ajīvānāṃ tataḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ śubhe
BhP tataḥ sacittāḥ pravarās tataś cendriyavṛttayaḥ
BhP tatrāpi sparśavedibhyaḥ pravarā rasavedinaḥ
BhP tebhyo gandhavidaḥ śreṣṭhās tataḥ śabdavido varāḥ
BhP rūpabhedavidas tatra tataś cobhayatodataḥ
BhP teṣāṃ bahupadāḥ śreṣṭhāś catuṣpādas tato dvipāt
BhP tato varṇāś ca catvāras teṣāṃ brāhmaṇa uttamaḥ
BhP brāhmaṇeṣv api vedajño hy arthajño 'bhyadhikas tataḥ
BhP arthajñāt saṃśayacchettā tataḥ śreyān svakarmakṛt
BhP muktasaṅgas tato bhūyān adogdhā dharmam ātmanaḥ
BhP tasmān mayy arpitāśeṣa kriyārthātmā nirantaraḥ
BhP mayy arpitātmanaḥ puṃso mayi sannyastakarmaṇaḥ
BhP na paśyāmi paraṃ bhūtam akartuḥ samadarśanāt
BhP manasaitāni bhūtāni praṇamed bahumānayan
BhP īśvaro jīvakalayā praviṣṭo bhagavān iti
BhP bhaktiyogaś ca yogaś ca mayā mānavy udīritaḥ
BhP yayor ekatareṇaiva puruṣaḥ puruṣaṃ vrajet
BhP etad bhagavato rūpaṃ brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ
BhP paraṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ daivaṃ karmaviceṣṭitam
BhP rūpabhedāspadaṃ divyaṃ kāla ity abhidhīyate
BhP bhūtānāṃ mahadādīnāṃ yato bhinnadṛśāṃ bhayam
BhP yo 'ntaḥ praviśya bhūtāni bhūtair atty akhilāśrayaḥ
BhP sa viṣṇvākhyo 'dhiyajño 'sau kālaḥ kalayatāṃ prabhuḥ
BhP na cāsya kaścid dayito na dveṣyo na ca bāndhavaḥ
BhP āviśaty apramatto 'sau pramattaṃ janam antakṛt
BhP yadbhayād vāti vāto 'yaṃ sūryas tapati yadbhayāt
BhP yadbhayād varṣate devo bhagaṇo bhāti yadbhayāt
BhP yad vanaspatayo bhītā latāś cauṣadhibhiḥ saha
BhP sve sve kāle 'bhigṛhṇanti puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca
BhP sravanti sarito bhītā notsarpaty udadhir yataḥ
BhP agnir indhe sagiribhir bhūr na majjati yadbhayāt
BhP nabho dadāti śvasatāṃ padaṃ yanniyamād adaḥ
BhP lokaṃ svadehaṃ tanute mahān saptabhir āvṛtam
BhP guṇābhimānino devāḥ sargādiṣv asya yadbhayāt
BhP vartante 'nuyugaṃ yeṣāṃ vaśa etac carācaram
BhP so 'nanto 'ntakaraḥ kālo 'nādir ādikṛd avyayaḥ
BhP janaṃ janena janayan mārayan mṛtyunāntakam
BhP kapila uvāca
BhP tasyaitasya jano nūnaṃ nāyaṃ vedoruvikramam
BhP kālyamāno 'pi balino vāyor iva ghanāvaliḥ
BhP yaṃ yam artham upādatte duḥkhena sukhahetave
BhP taṃ taṃ dhunoti bhagavān pumān chocati yatkṛte
BhP yad adhruvasya dehasya sānubandhasya durmatiḥ
BhP dhruvāṇi manyate mohād gṛhakṣetravasūni ca
BhP jantur vai bhava etasmin yāṃ yāṃ yonim anuvrajet
BhP tasyāṃ tasyāṃ sa labhate nirvṛtiṃ na virajyate
BhP narakastho 'pi dehaṃ vai na pumāṃs tyaktum icchati
BhP nārakyāṃ nirvṛtau satyāṃ devamāyāvimohitaḥ
BhP ātmajāyāsutāgāra paśudraviṇabandhuṣu
BhP nirūḍhamūlahṛdaya ātmānaṃ bahu manyate
BhP sandahyamānasarvāṅga eṣām udvahanādhinā
BhP karoty avirataṃ mūḍho duritāni durāśayaḥ
BhP ākṣiptātmendriyaḥ strīṇām asatīnāṃ ca māyayā
BhP raho racitayālāpaiḥ śiśūnāṃ kalabhāṣiṇām
BhP gṛheṣu kūṭadharmeṣu duḥkhatantreṣv atandritaḥ
BhP kurvan duḥkhapratīkāraṃ sukhavan manyate gṛhī
BhP arthair āpāditair gurvyā hiṃsayetastataś ca tān
BhP puṣṇāti yeṣāṃ poṣeṇa śeṣabhug yāty adhaḥ svayam
BhP vārtāyāṃ lupyamānāyām ārabdhāyāṃ punaḥ punaḥ
BhP lobhābhibhūto niḥsattvaḥ parārthe kurute spṛhām
BhP kuṭumbabharaṇākalpo mandabhāgyo vṛthodyamaḥ
BhP śriyā vihīnaḥ kṛpaṇo dhyāyan chvasiti mūḍhadhīḥ
BhP evaṃ svabharaṇākalpaṃ tatkalatrādayas tathā
BhP nādriyante yathā pūrvaṃ kīnāśā iva gojaram
BhP tatrāpy ajātanirvedo bhriyamāṇaḥ svayam bhṛtaiḥ
BhP jarayopāttavairūpyo maraṇābhimukho gṛhe
BhP āste 'vamatyopanyastaṃ gṛhapāla ivāharan
BhP āmayāvy apradīptāgnir alpāhāro 'lpaceṣṭitaḥ
BhP vāyunotkramatottāraḥ kaphasaṃruddhanāḍikaḥ
BhP kāsaśvāsakṛtāyāsaḥ kaṇṭhe ghuraghurāyate
BhP śayānaḥ pariśocadbhiḥ parivītaḥ svabandhubhiḥ
BhP vācyamāno 'pi na brūte kālapāśavaśaṃ gataḥ
BhP evaṃ kuṭumbabharaṇe vyāpṛtātmājitendriyaḥ
BhP mriyate rudatāṃ svānām uruvedanayāstadhīḥ
BhP yamadūtau tadā prāptau bhīmau sarabhasekṣaṇau
BhP sa dṛṣṭvā trastahṛdayaḥ śakṛnmūtraṃ vimuñcati
BhP yātanādeha āvṛtya pāśair baddhvā gale balāt
BhP nayato dīrgham adhvānaṃ daṇḍyaṃ rājabhaṭā yathā
BhP tayor nirbhinnahṛdayas tarjanair jātavepathuḥ
BhP pathi śvabhir bhakṣyamāṇa ārto 'ghaṃ svam anusmaran
BhP kṣuttṛṭparīto 'rkadavānalānilaiḥ santapyamānaḥ pathi taptavāluke
BhP kṛcchreṇa pṛṣṭhe kaśayā ca tāḍitaś calaty aśakto 'pi nirāśramodake
BhP tatra tatra patan chrānto mūrcchitaḥ punar utthitaḥ
BhP pathā pāpīyasā nītas tarasā yamasādanam
BhP yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi navatiṃ nava cādhvanaḥ
BhP tribhir muhūrtair dvābhyāṃ vā nītaḥ prāpnoti yātanāḥ
BhP ādīpanaṃ svagātrāṇāṃ veṣṭayitvolmukādibhiḥ
BhP ātmamāṃsādanaṃ kvāpi svakṛttaṃ parato 'pi vā
BhP jīvataś cāntrābhyuddhāraḥ śvagṛdhrair yamasādane
BhP sarpavṛścikadaṃśādyair daśadbhiś cātmavaiśasam
BhP kṛntanaṃ cāvayavaśo gajādibhyo bhidāpanam
BhP pātanaṃ giriśṛṅgebhyo rodhanaṃ cāmbugartayoḥ
BhP yās tāmisrāndhatāmisrā rauravādyāś ca yātanāḥ
BhP bhuṅkte naro vā nārī vā mithaḥ saṅgena nirmitāḥ
BhP atraiva narakaḥ svarga iti mātaḥ pracakṣate
BhP yā yātanā vai nārakyas tā ihāpy upalakṣitāḥ
BhP evaṃ kuṭumbaṃ bibhrāṇa udaram bhara eva vā
BhP visṛjyehobhayaṃ pretya bhuṅkte tatphalam īdṛśam
BhP ekaḥ prapadyate dhvāntaṃ hitvedaṃ svakalevaram
BhP kuśaletarapātheyo bhūtadroheṇa yad bhṛtam
BhP daivenāsāditaṃ tasya śamalaṃ niraye pumān
BhP bhuṅkte kuṭumbapoṣasya hṛtavitta ivāturaḥ
BhP kevalena hy adharmeṇa kuṭumbabharaṇotsukaḥ
BhP yāti jīvo 'ndhatāmisraṃ caramaṃ tamasaḥ padam
BhP adhastān naralokasya yāvatīr yātanādayaḥ
BhP kramaśaḥ samanukramya punar atrāvrajec chuciḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP karmaṇā daivanetreṇa jantur dehopapattaye
BhP striyāḥ praviṣṭa udaraṃ puṃso retaḥkaṇāśrayaḥ
BhP kalalaṃ tv ekarātreṇa pañcarātreṇa budbudam
BhP daśāhena tu karkandhūḥ peśy aṇḍaṃ vā tataḥ param
BhP māsena tu śiro dvābhyāṃ bāhvaṅghryādyaṅgavigrahaḥ
BhP nakhalomāsthicarmāṇi liṅgacchidrodbhavas tribhiḥ
BhP caturbhir dhātavaḥ sapta pañcabhiḥ kṣuttṛḍudbhavaḥ
BhP ṣaḍbhir jarāyuṇā vītaḥ kukṣau bhrāmyati dakṣiṇe
BhP mātur jagdhānnapānādyair edhaddhātur asammate
BhP śete viṇmūtrayor garte sa jantur jantusambhave
BhP kṛmibhiḥ kṣatasarvāṅgaḥ saukumāryāt pratikṣaṇam
BhP mūrcchām āpnoty urukleśas tatratyaiḥ kṣudhitair muhuḥ
BhP kaṭutīkṣṇoṣṇalavaṇa rūkṣāmlādibhir ulbaṇaiḥ
BhP mātṛbhuktair upaspṛṣṭaḥ sarvāṅgotthitavedanaḥ
BhP ulbena saṃvṛtas tasminn antraiś ca bahir āvṛtaḥ
BhP āste kṛtvā śiraḥ kukṣau bhugnapṛṣṭhaśirodharaḥ
BhP akalpaḥ svāṅgaceṣṭāyāṃ śakunta iva pañjare
BhP tatra labdhasmṛtir daivāt karma janmaśatodbhavam
BhP smaran dīrgham anucchvāsaṃ śarma kiṃ nāma vindate
BhP ārabhya saptamān māsāl labdhabodho 'pi vepitaḥ
BhP naikatrāste sūtivātair viṣṭhābhūr iva sodaraḥ
BhP nāthamāna ṛṣir bhītaḥ saptavadhriḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
BhP stuvīta taṃ viklavayā vācā yenodare 'rpitaḥ
BhP jantur uvāca
BhP tasyopasannam avituṃ jagad icchayātta
BhP nānātanor bhuvi calaccaraṇāravindam
BhP so 'haṃ vrajāmi śaraṇaṃ hy akutobhayaṃ me
BhP yenedṛśī gatir adarśy asato 'nurūpā
BhP yas tv atra baddha iva karmabhir āvṛtātmā
BhP bhūtendriyāśayamayīm avalambya māyām
BhP āste viśuddham avikāram akhaṇḍabodham
BhP ātapyamānahṛdaye 'vasitaṃ namāmi
BhP yaḥ pañcabhūtaracite rahitaḥ śarīre
BhP cchanno 'yathendriyaguṇārthacidātmako 'ham
BhP tenāvikuṇṭhamahimānam ṛṣiṃ tam enaṃ
BhP vande paraṃ prakṛtipūruṣayoḥ pumāṃsam
BhP yanmāyayoruguṇakarmanibandhane 'smin
BhP sāṃsārike pathi caraṃs tadabhiśrameṇa
BhP naṣṭasmṛtiḥ punar ayaṃ pravṛṇīta lokaṃ
BhP yuktyā kayā mahadanugraham antareṇa
BhP jñānaṃ yad etad adadhāt katamaḥ sa devas
BhP traikālikaṃ sthiracareṣv anuvartitāṃśaḥ
BhP taṃ jīvakarmapadavīm anuvartamānās
BhP tāpatrayopaśamanāya vayaṃ bhajema
BhP dehy anyadehavivare jaṭharāgnināsṛg
BhP viṇmūtrakūpapatito bhṛśataptadehaḥ
BhP icchann ito vivasituṃ gaṇayan svamāsān
BhP nirvāsyate kṛpaṇadhīr bhagavan kadā nu
BhP yenedṛśīṃ gatim asau daśamāsya īśa
BhP saṅgrāhitaḥ purudayena bhavādṛśena
BhP svenaiva tuṣyatu kṛtena sa dīnanāthaḥ
BhP ko nāma tatprati vināñjalim asya kuryāt
BhP paśyaty ayaṃ dhiṣaṇayā nanu saptavadhriḥ
BhP śārīrake damaśarīry aparaḥ svadehe
BhP yatsṛṣṭayāsaṃ tam ahaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ
BhP paśye bahir hṛdi ca caityam iva pratītam
BhP so 'haṃ vasann api vibho bahuduḥkhavāsaṃ
BhP garbhān na nirjigamiṣe bahir andhakūpe
BhP yatropayātam upasarpati devamāyā
BhP mithyā matir yadanu saṃsṛticakram etat
BhP tasmād ahaṃ vigataviklava uddhariṣya
BhP ātmānam āśu tamasaḥ suhṛdātmanaiva
BhP bhūyo yathā vyasanam etad anekarandhraṃ
BhP mā me bhaviṣyad upasāditaviṣṇupādaḥ
BhP kapila uvāca
BhP evaṃ kṛtamatir garbhe daśamāsyaḥ stuvann ṛṣiḥ
BhP sadyaḥ kṣipaty avācīnaṃ prasūtyai sūtimārutaḥ
BhP tenāvasṛṣṭaḥ sahasā kṛtvāvāk śira āturaḥ
BhP viniṣkrāmati kṛcchreṇa nirucchvāso hatasmṛtiḥ
BhP patito bhuvy asṛṅmiśraḥ viṣṭhābhūr iva ceṣṭate
BhP rorūyati gate jñāne viparītāṃ gatiṃ gataḥ
BhP paracchandaṃ na viduṣā puṣyamāṇo janena saḥ
BhP anabhipretam āpannaḥ pratyākhyātum anīśvaraḥ
BhP śāyito 'śuciparyaṅke jantuḥ svedajadūṣite
BhP neśaḥ kaṇḍūyane 'ṅgānām āsanotthānaceṣṭane
BhP tudanty āmatvacaṃ daṃśā maśakā matkuṇādayaḥ
BhP rudantaṃ vigatajñānaṃ kṛmayaḥ kṛmikaṃ yathā
BhP ity evaṃ śaiśavaṃ bhuktvā duḥkhaṃ paugaṇḍam eva ca
BhP alabdhābhīpsito 'jñānād iddhamanyuḥ śucārpitaḥ
BhP saha dehena mānena vardhamānena manyunā
BhP karoti vigrahaṃ kāmī kāmiṣv antāya cātmanaḥ
BhP bhūtaiḥ pañcabhir ārabdhe dehe dehy abudho 'sakṛt
BhP ahaṃ mamety asadgrāhaḥ karoti kumatir matim
BhP tadarthaṃ kurute karma yadbaddho yāti saṃsṛtim
BhP yo 'nuyāti dadat kleśam avidyākarmabandhanaḥ
BhP yady asadbhiḥ pathi punaḥ śiśnodarakṛtodyamaiḥ
BhP āsthito ramate jantus tamo viśati pūrvavat
BhP satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā maunaṃ buddhiḥ śrīr hrīr yaśaḥ kṣamā
BhP śamo damo bhagaś ceti yatsaṅgād yāti saṅkṣayam
BhP teṣv aśānteṣu mūḍheṣu khaṇḍitātmasv asādhuṣu
BhP saṅgaṃ na kuryāc chocyeṣu yoṣitkrīḍāmṛgeṣu ca
BhP na tathāsya bhaven moho bandhaś cānyaprasaṅgataḥ
BhP yoṣitsaṅgād yathā puṃso yathā tatsaṅgisaṅgataḥ
BhP prajāpatiḥ svāṃ duhitaraṃ dṛṣṭvā tadrūpadharṣitaḥ
BhP rohidbhūtāṃ so 'nvadhāvad ṛkṣarūpī hatatrapaḥ
BhP tatsṛṣṭasṛṣṭasṛṣṭeṣu ko nv akhaṇḍitadhīḥ pumān
BhP ṛṣiṃ nārāyaṇam ṛte yoṣinmayyeha māyayā
BhP balaṃ me paśya māyāyāḥ strīmayyā jayino diśām
BhP yā karoti padākrāntān bhrūvijṛmbheṇa kevalam
BhP saṅgaṃ na kuryāt pramadāsu jātu yogasya pāraṃ param ārurukṣuḥ
BhP matsevayā pratilabdhātmalābho vadanti yā nirayadvāram asya
BhP yopayāti śanair māyā yoṣid devavinirmitā
BhP tām īkṣetātmano mṛtyuṃ tṛṇaiḥ kūpam ivāvṛtam
BhP yāṃ manyate patiṃ mohān manmāyām ṛṣabhāyatīm
BhP strītvaṃ strīsaṅgataḥ prāpto vittāpatyagṛhapradam
BhP tām ātmano vijānīyāt patyapatyagṛhātmakam
BhP daivopasāditaṃ mṛtyuṃ mṛgayor gāyanaṃ yathā
BhP dehena jīvabhūtena lokāl lokam anuvrajan
BhP bhuñjāna eva karmāṇi karoty avirataṃ pumān
BhP jīvo hy asyānugo deho bhūtendriyamanomayaḥ
BhP tannirodho 'sya maraṇam āvirbhāvas tu sambhavaḥ
BhP dravyopalabdhisthānasya dravyekṣāyogyatā yadā
BhP tat pañcatvam ahaṃmānād utpattir dravyadarśanam
BhP yathākṣṇor dravyāvayava darśanāyogyatā yadā
BhP tadaiva cakṣuṣo draṣṭur draṣṭṛtvāyogyatānayoḥ
BhP tasmān na kāryaḥ santrāso na kārpaṇyaṃ na sambhramaḥ
BhP buddhvā jīvagatiṃ dhīro muktasaṅgaś cared iha
BhP samyagdarśanayā buddhyā yogavairāgyayuktayā
BhP māyāviracite loke caren nyasya kalevaram
BhP kapila uvāca
BhP atha yo gṛhamedhīyān dharmān evāvasan gṛhe
BhP kāmam arthaṃ ca dharmān svān dogdhi bhūyaḥ piparti tān
BhP sa cāpi bhagavaddharmāt kāmamūḍhaḥ parāṅmukhaḥ
BhP yajate kratubhir devān pitṃś ca śraddhayānvitaḥ
BhP tacchraddhayākrāntamatiḥ pitṛdevavrataḥ pumān
BhP gatvā cāndramasaṃ lokaṃ somapāḥ punar eṣyati
BhP yadā cāhīndraśayyāyāṃ śete 'nantāsano hariḥ
BhP tadā lokā layaṃ yānti ta ete gṛhamedhinām
BhP ye svadharmān na duhyanti dhīrāḥ kāmārthahetave
BhP niḥsaṅgā nyastakarmāṇaḥ praśāntāḥ śuddhacetasaḥ
BhP nivṛttidharmaniratā nirmamā nirahaṅkṛtāḥ
BhP svadharmāptena sattvena pariśuddhena cetasā
BhP sūryadvāreṇa te yānti puruṣaṃ viśvatomukham
BhP parāvareśaṃ prakṛtim asyotpattyantabhāvanam
BhP dviparārdhāvasāne yaḥ pralayo brahmaṇas tu te
BhP tāvad adhyāsate lokaṃ parasya paracintakāḥ
BhP kṣmāmbho'nalānilaviyanmanaindriyārtha
BhP bhūtādibhiḥ parivṛtaṃ pratisañjihīrṣuḥ
BhP avyākṛtaṃ viśati yarhi guṇatrayātmākālaṃ
BhP parākhyam anubhūya paraḥ svayambhūḥ
BhP evaṃ paretya bhagavantam anupraviṣṭāye
BhP yogino jitamarunmanaso virāgāḥ
BhP tenaiva sākam amṛtaṃ puruṣaṃ purāṇaṃ
BhP brahma pradhānam upayānty agatābhimānāḥ
BhP atha taṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ hṛtpadmeṣu kṛtālayam
BhP śrutānubhāvaṃ śaraṇaṃ vraja bhāvena bhāmini
BhP ādyaḥ sthiracarāṇāṃ yo vedagarbhaḥ saharṣibhiḥ
BhP yogeśvaraiḥ kumārādyaiḥ siddhair yogapravartakaiḥ
BhP bhedadṛṣṭyābhimānena niḥsaṅgenāpi karmaṇā
BhP kartṛtvāt saguṇaṃ brahma puruṣaṃ puruṣarṣabham
BhP sa saṃsṛtya punaḥ kāle kāleneśvaramūrtinā
BhP jāte guṇavyatikare yathāpūrvaṃ prajāyate
BhP aiśvaryaṃ pārameṣṭhyaṃ ca te 'pi dharmavinirmitam
BhP niṣevya punar āyānti guṇavyatikare sati
BhP ye tv ihāsaktamanasaḥ karmasu śraddhayānvitāḥ
BhP kurvanty apratiṣiddhāni nityāny api ca kṛtsnaśaḥ
BhP rajasā kuṇṭhamanasaḥ kāmātmāno 'jitendriyāḥ
BhP pitn yajanty anudinaṃ gṛheṣv abhiratāśayāḥ
BhP traivargikās te puruṣā vimukhā harimedhasaḥ
BhP kathāyāṃ kathanīyoru vikramasya madhudviṣaḥ
BhP nūnaṃ daivena vihatā ye cācyutakathāsudhām
BhP hitvā śṛṇvanty asadgāthāḥ purīṣam iva viḍbhujaḥ
BhP dakṣiṇena pathāryamṇaḥ pitṛlokaṃ vrajanti te
BhP prajām anu prajāyante śmaśānāntakriyākṛtaḥ
BhP tatas te kṣīṇasukṛtāḥ punar lokam imaṃ sati
BhP patanti vivaśā devaiḥ sadyo vibhraṃśitodayāḥ
BhP tasmāt tvaṃ sarvabhāvena bhajasva parameṣṭhinam
BhP tadguṇāśrayayā bhaktyā bhajanīyapadāmbujam
BhP vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogaḥ prayojitaḥ
BhP janayaty āśu vairāgyaṃ jñānaṃ yad brahmadarśanam
BhP yadāsya cittam artheṣu sameṣv indriyavṛttibhiḥ
BhP na vigṛhṇāti vaiṣamyaṃ priyam apriyam ity uta
BhP sa tadaivātmanātmānaṃ niḥsaṅgaṃ samadarśanam
BhP heyopādeyarahitam ārūḍhaṃ padam īkṣate
BhP jñānamātraṃ paraṃ brahma paramātmeśvaraḥ pumān
BhP dṛśyādibhiḥ pṛthag bhāvair bhagavān eka īyate
BhP etāvān eva yogena samagreṇeha yoginaḥ
BhP yujyate 'bhimato hy artho yad asaṅgas tu kṛtsnaśaḥ
BhP jñānam ekaṃ parācīnair indriyair brahma nirguṇam
BhP avabhāty artharūpeṇa bhrāntyā śabdādidharmiṇā
BhP yathā mahān ahaṃrūpas trivṛt pañcavidhaḥ svarāṭ
BhP ekādaśavidhas tasya vapur aṇḍaṃ jagad yataḥ
BhP etad vai śraddhayā bhaktyā yogābhyāsena nityaśaḥ
BhP samāhitātmā niḥsaṅgo viraktyā paripaśyati
BhP ity etat kathitaṃ gurvi jñānaṃ tad brahmadarśanam
BhP yenānubuddhyate tattvaṃ prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca
BhP jñānayogaś ca manniṣṭho nairguṇyo bhaktilakṣaṇaḥ
BhP dvayor apy eka evārtho bhagavacchabdalakṣaṇaḥ
BhP yathendriyaiḥ pṛthagdvārair artho bahuguṇāśrayaḥ
BhP eko nāneyate tadvad bhagavān śāstravartmabhiḥ
BhP kriyayā kratubhir dānais tapaḥsvādhyāyamarśanaiḥ
BhP ātmendriyajayenāpi sannyāsena ca karmaṇām
BhP yogena vividhāṅgena bhaktiyogena caiva hi
BhP dharmeṇobhayacihnena yaḥ pravṛttinivṛttimān
BhP ātmatattvāvabodhena vairāgyeṇa dṛḍhena ca
BhP īyate bhagavān ebhiḥ saguṇo nirguṇaḥ svadṛk
BhP prāvocaṃ bhaktiyogasya svarūpaṃ te caturvidham
BhP kālasya cāvyaktagater yo 'ntardhāvati jantuṣu
BhP jīvasya saṃsṛtīr bahvīr avidyākarmanirmitāḥ
BhP yāsv aṅga praviśann ātmā na veda gatim ātmanaḥ
BhP naitat khalāyopadiśen nāvinītāya karhicit
BhP na stabdhāya na bhinnāya naiva dharmadhvajāya ca
BhP na lolupāyopadiśen na gṛhārūḍhacetase
BhP nābhaktāya ca me jātu na madbhaktadviṣām api
BhP śraddadhānāya bhaktāya vinītāyānasūyave
BhP bhūteṣu kṛtamaitrāya śuśrūṣābhiratāya ca
BhP bahirjātavirāgāya śāntacittāya dīyatām
BhP nirmatsarāya śucaye yasyāhaṃ preyasāṃ priyaḥ
BhP ya idaṃ śṛṇuyād amba śraddhayā puruṣaḥ sakṛt
BhP yo vābhidhatte maccittaḥ sa hy eti padavīṃ ca me
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ niśamya kapilasya vaco janitrīsā kardamasya dayitā kila devahūtiḥ
BhP visrastamohapaṭalā tam abhipraṇamyatuṣṭāva tattvaviṣayāṅkitasiddhibhūmim
BhP devahūtir uvāca
BhP athāpy ajo 'ntaḥsalile śayānaṃ bhūtendriyārthātmamayaṃ vapus te
BhP guṇapravāhaṃ sadaśeṣabījaṃ dadhyau svayaṃ yajjaṭharābjajātaḥ
BhP sa eva viśvasya bhavān vidhatte guṇapravāheṇa vibhaktavīryaḥ
BhP sargādy anīho 'vitathābhisandhir ātmeśvaro 'tarkyasahasraśaktiḥ
BhP sa tvaṃ bhṛto me jaṭhareṇa nātha kathaṃ nu yasyodara etad āsīt
BhP viśvaṃ yugānte vaṭapatra ekaḥ śete sma māyāśiśur aṅghripānaḥ
BhP tvaṃ dehatantraḥ praśamāya pāpmanāṃ nideśabhājāṃ ca vibho vibhūtaye
BhP yathāvatārās tava sūkarādayas tathāyam apy ātmapathopalabdhaye
BhP yannāmadheyaśravaṇānukīrtanād yatprahvaṇād yatsmaraṇād api kvacit
BhP śvādo 'pi sadyaḥ savanāya kalpate kutaḥ punas te bhagavan nu darśanāt
BhP aho bata śvapaco 'to garīyān yajjihvāgre vartate nāma tubhyam
BhP tepus tapas te juhuvuḥ sasnur āryā brahmānūcur nāma gṛṇanti ye te
BhP taṃ tvām ahaṃ brahma paraṃ pumāṃsaṃ pratyaksrotasy ātmani saṃvibhāvyam
BhP svatejasā dhvastaguṇapravāhaṃ vande viṣṇuṃ kapilaṃ vedagarbham
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP īḍito bhagavān evaṃ kapilākhyaḥ paraḥ pumān
BhP vācāviklavayety āha mātaraṃ mātṛvatsalaḥ
BhP kapila uvāca
BhP mārgeṇānena mātas te susevyenoditena me
BhP āsthitena parāṃ kāṣṭhām acirād avarotsyasi
BhP śraddhatsvaitan mataṃ mahyaṃ juṣṭaṃ yad brahmavādibhiḥ
BhP yena mām abhayaṃ yāyā mṛtyum ṛcchanty atadvidaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti pradarśya bhagavān satīṃ tām ātmano gatim
BhP svamātrā brahmavādinyā kapilo 'numato yayau
BhP sā cāpi tanayoktena yogādeśena yogayuk
BhP tasminn āśrama āpīḍe sarasvatyāḥ samāhitā
BhP abhīkṣṇāvagāhakapiśān jaṭilān kuṭilālakān
BhP ātmānaṃ cogratapasā bibhratī cīriṇaṃ kṛśam
BhP prajāpateḥ kardamasya tapoyogavijṛmbhitam
BhP svagārhasthyam anaupamyaṃ prārthyaṃ vaimānikair api
BhP payaḥphenanibhāḥ śayyā dāntā rukmaparicchadāḥ
BhP āsanāni ca haimāni susparśāstaraṇāni ca
BhP svacchasphaṭikakuḍyeṣu mahāmārakateṣu ca
BhP ratnapradīpā ābhānti lalanā ratnasaṃyutāḥ
BhP gṛhodyānaṃ kusumitai ramyaṃ bahvamaradrumaiḥ
BhP kūjadvihaṅgamithunaṃ gāyanmattamadhuvratam
BhP yatra praviṣṭam ātmānaṃ vibudhānucarā jaguḥ
BhP vāpyām utpalagandhinyāṃ kardamenopalālitam
BhP hitvā tad īpsitatamam apy ākhaṇḍalayoṣitām
BhP kiñcic cakāra vadanaṃ putraviśleṣaṇāturā
BhP vanaṃ pravrajite patyāv apatyavirahāturā
BhP jñātatattvāpy abhūn naṣṭe vatse gaur iva vatsalā
BhP tam eva dhyāyatī devam apatyaṃ kapilaṃ harim
BhP babhūvācirato vatsa niḥspṛhā tādṛśe gṛhe
BhP dhyāyatī bhagavadrūpaṃ yad āha dhyānagocaram
BhP sutaḥ prasannavadanaṃ samastavyastacintayā
BhP bhaktipravāhayogena vairāgyeṇa balīyasā
BhP yuktānuṣṭhānajātena jñānena brahmahetunā
BhP viśuddhena tadātmānam ātmanā viśvatomukham
BhP svānubhūtyā tirobhūta māyāguṇaviśeṣaṇam
BhP brahmaṇy avasthitamatir bhagavaty ātmasaṃśraye
BhP nivṛttajīvāpattitvāt kṣīṇakleśāptanirvṛtiḥ
BhP nityārūḍhasamādhitvāt parāvṛttaguṇabhramā
BhP na sasmāra tadātmānaṃ svapne dṛṣṭam ivotthitaḥ
BhP taddehaḥ parataḥ poṣo 'py akṛśaś cādhyasambhavāt
BhP babhau malair avacchannaḥ sadhūma iva pāvakaḥ
BhP svāṅgaṃ tapoyogamayaṃ muktakeśaṃ gatāmbaram
BhP daivaguptaṃ na bubudhe vāsudevapraviṣṭadhīḥ
BhP evaṃ sā kapiloktena mārgeṇācirataḥ param
BhP ātmānaṃ brahmanirvāṇaṃ bhagavantam avāpa ha
BhP tad vīrāsīt puṇyatamaṃ kṣetraṃ trailokyaviśrutam
BhP nāmnā siddhapadaṃ yatra sā saṃsiddhim upeyuṣī
BhP tasyās tad yogavidhuta mārtyaṃ martyam abhūt sarit
BhP srotasāṃ pravarā saumya siddhidā siddhasevitā
BhP kapilo 'pi mahāyogī bhagavān pitur āśramāt
BhP mātaraṃ samanujñāpya prāgudīcīṃ diśaṃ yayau
BhP siddhacāraṇagandharvair munibhiś cāpsarogaṇaiḥ
BhP stūyamānaḥ samudreṇa dattārhaṇaniketanaḥ
BhP āste yogaṃ samāsthāya sāṅkhyācāryair abhiṣṭutaḥ
BhP trayāṇām api lokānām upaśāntyai samāhitaḥ
BhP etan nigaditaṃ tāta yat pṛṣṭo 'haṃ tavānagha
BhP kapilasya ca saṃvādo devahūtyāś ca pāvanaḥ
BhP ya idam anuśṛṇoti yo 'bhidhatte kapilamuner matam ātmayogaguhyam
BhP bhagavati kṛtadhīḥ suparṇaketāv upalabhate bhagavatpadāravindam
